## .github/workflows/build.yml

Path: `.github/workflows/build.yml`

```yaml
     1	name: CI
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  push:
     5	    branches: [ "master", "main" ]
     6	  pull_request:
     7	    branches: [ "master", "main" ]
     8	
     9	jobs:
    10	  build:
    11	    name: Build & Test
    12	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    13	
    14	    services:
    15	      postgres:
    16	        image: postgres:15
    17	        env:
    18	          POSTGRES_USER: postgres
    19	          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
    20	          POSTGRES_DB: postgres
    21	        ports:
    22	          - 5432:5432
    23	        options: >-
    24	          --health-cmd "pg_isready -U postgres"
    25	          --health-interval 10s
    26	          --health-timeout 5s
    27	          --health-retries 5
    28	
    29	    steps:
    30	      - name: Checkout source
    31	        uses: actions/checkout@v4
    32	
    33	      - name: Set up Java 17
    34	        uses: actions/setup-java@v4
    35	        with:
    36	          java-version: '17'
    37	          distribution: 'temurin'
    38	          cache: maven
    39	
    40	      # Testcontainers spins up its own PostgreSQL / Kafka containers, so we
    41	      # only need Docker-in-Docker access (provided by ubuntu-latest by default).
    42	      - name: Grant execute permission to Maven wrapper
    43	        run: chmod +x mvnw
    44	
    45	      - name: Build and run unit + integration tests
    46	        env:
    47	          DB_USERNAME: postgres
    48	          DB_PASSWORD: postgres
    49	          JWT_SECRET: mysupersecuresecretkeythatislongenough123
    50	          INTERNAL_SECRET: veryStrongInternalSecret123
    51	          # Testcontainers manages its own Kafka/PG; these are fallback values.
    52	          KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS: localhost:9092
    53	          ZIPKIN_URL: http://localhost:9411/api/v2/spans
    54	          SPRING_PROFILES_ACTIVE: test
    55	        run: ./mvnw clean verify --batch-mode -Djava.security.egd=file:/dev/./urandom
    56	
    57	      - name: Upload test reports
    58	        if: always()
    59	        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
    60	        with:
    61	          name: surefire-reports
    62	          path: '**/target/surefire-reports/**'
    63	          retention-days: 7
    64	
    65	  docker-build:
    66	    name: Docker build (smoke)
    67	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    68	    # Only run on direct pushes, not PRs, to avoid double builds
    69	    if: github.event_name == 'push'
    70	    strategy:
    71	      fail-fast: false
    72	      matrix:
    73	        service:
    74	          - api-gateway
    75	          - auth-service
    76	          - user-service
    77	          - product-service
    78	          - order-service
    79	          - review-service
    80	          - payment-service
    81	    steps:
    82	      - name: Checkout source
    83	        uses: actions/checkout@v4
    84	
    85	      - name: Set up Docker Buildx
    86	        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
    87	
    88	      - name: Build Docker image for ${{ matrix.service }}
    89	        uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
    90	        with:
    91	          context: .
    92	          file: ./${{ matrix.service }}/dockerfile
    93	          push: false
    94	          tags: ecommerce/${{ matrix.service }}:ci
    95	          cache-from: type=gha
    96	          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

## .mvn/wrapper/maven-wrapper.properties

Path: `.mvn/wrapper/maven-wrapper.properties`

```properties
     1	wrapperVersion=3.3.4
     2	distributionType=only-script
     3	distributionUrl=https://repo.maven.apache.org/maven2/org/apache/maven/apache-maven/3.9.12/apache-maven-3.9.12-bin.zip
```

## api-gateway/.mvn/wrapper/maven-wrapper.properties

Path: `api-gateway/.mvn/wrapper/maven-wrapper.properties`

```properties
     1	wrapperVersion=3.3.4
     2	distributionType=only-script
     3	distributionUrl=https://repo.maven.apache.org/maven2/org/apache/maven/apache-maven/3.9.12/apache-maven-3.9.12-bin.zip
```

## api-gateway/dockerfile

Path: `api-gateway/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	# Copy parent pom + all module poms so Maven can resolve the multi-module graph
     6	COPY pom.xml .
     7	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     8	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     9	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
    10	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    11	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    12	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    13	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    14	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    15	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    16	RUN mvn -pl api-gateway dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    17	
    18	# Copy source and build only this service
    19	COPY api-gateway/src api-gateway/src
    20	RUN mvn -pl api-gateway package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    21	
    22	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    23	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    24	WORKDIR /app
    25	COPY --from=builder /workspace/api-gateway/target/*.jar app.jar
    26	EXPOSE 8080
    27	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## api-gateway/pom.xml

Path: `api-gateway/pom.xml`

```xml
     1	<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/filter/CorrelationIdGlobalFilter.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/filter/CorrelationIdGlobalFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.filter;
     2	
     3	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     4	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     5	import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GatewayFilterChain;
     6	import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GlobalFilter;
     7	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     8	import org.springframework.http.server.reactive.ServerHttpRequest;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.server.ServerWebExchange;
    11	import reactor.core.publisher.Mono;
    12	
    13	import java.util.UUID;
    14	
    15	/**
    16	 * API Gateway correlation-ID filter.
    17	 *
    18	 * <p>For each incoming request:
    19	 * <ol>
    20	 *   <li>Reads or generates a {@code X-Correlation-Id} header.
    21	 *   <li>Forwards the header to downstream services so they can correlate logs.
    22	 *   <li>Echoes the value back in the response header.
    23	 * </ol>
    24	 *
    25	 * <p>Downstream services (servlet-based) use {@code CorrelationIdFilter} to
    26	 * pick up this header and put it in their MDC.
    27	 */
    28	@Component
    29	@Slf4j
    30	public class CorrelationIdGlobalFilter implements GlobalFilter, Ordered {
    31	
    32	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    33	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    34	
    35	    @Override
    36	    public Mono<Void> filter(ServerWebExchange exchange, GatewayFilterChain chain) {
    37	
    38	        String correlationId = exchange.getRequest().getHeaders()
    39	                .getFirst(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    40	
    41	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    42	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    43	        }
    44	
    45	        final String finalCorrelationId = correlationId;
    46	
    47	        // Forward the header to downstream services
    48	        ServerHttpRequest mutatedRequest = exchange.getRequest().mutate()
    49	                .header(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, finalCorrelationId)
    50	                .build();
    51	
    52	        ServerWebExchange mutatedExchange = exchange.mutate()
    53	                .request(mutatedRequest)
    54	                .build();
    55	
    56	        // Echo back in the response
    57	        mutatedExchange.getResponse().getHeaders().add(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, finalCorrelationId);
    58	
    59	        return chain.filter(mutatedExchange)
    60	                .contextWrite(ctx -> ctx.put(MDC_KEY, finalCorrelationId));
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    @Override
    64	    public int getOrder() {
    65	        // Run before the rate limit filter
    66	        return Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE;
    67	    }
    68	}
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/filter/RateLimitGlobalFilter.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/filter/RateLimitGlobalFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.filter;
     2	
     3	import io.github.bucket4j.Bandwidth;
     4	import io.github.bucket4j.Bucket;
     5	import io.github.bucket4j.BucketConfiguration;
     6	import io.github.bucket4j.Refill;
     7	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     8	import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GatewayFilterChain;
     9	import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GlobalFilter;
    10	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
    11	import org.springframework.data.redis.core.ReactiveStringRedisTemplate;
    12	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
    13	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    14	import org.springframework.web.server.ServerWebExchange;
    15	import reactor.core.publisher.Mono;
    16	import reactor.core.scheduler.Schedulers;
    17	
    18	import java.time.Duration;
    19	import java.util.Map;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * Global rate-limiting filter for the API Gateway.
    24	 *
    25	 * <p>Implements a token bucket algorithm using Bucket4j with an in-memory
    26	 * store (one bucket per client IP). Each IP is allowed 100 requests per
    27	 * minute. Requests exceeding the limit receive HTTP 429 Too Many Requests.
    28	 *
    29	 * <p>The Redis reactive template is injected as an optional future upgrade
    30	 * path for distributed bucket synchronisation across multiple gateway replicas.
    31	 */
    32	@Component
    33	@Slf4j
    34	public class RateLimitGlobalFilter implements GlobalFilter, Ordered {
    35	
    36	    private static final int REQUEST_LIMIT = 100;
    37	    private static final Duration REFILL_DURATION = Duration.ofMinutes(1);
    38	
    39	    /** Per-IP token buckets — suitable for a single-node gateway deployment. */
    40	    private final Map<String, Bucket> buckets = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    41	
    42	    private final ReactiveStringRedisTemplate redisTemplate;
    43	
    44	    public RateLimitGlobalFilter(ReactiveStringRedisTemplate redisTemplate) {
    45	        this.redisTemplate = redisTemplate;
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    @Override
    49	    public Mono<Void> filter(ServerWebExchange exchange, GatewayFilterChain chain) {
    50	        String clientIp = resolveClientIp(exchange);
    51	
    52	        return Mono.fromCallable(() -> resolveBucket(clientIp).tryConsume(1))
    53	                .subscribeOn(Schedulers.boundedElastic())
    54	                .flatMap(allowed -> {
    55	                    if (allowed) {
    56	                        return chain.filter(exchange);
    57	                    }
    58	                    log.warn("Rate limit exceeded for IP: {}", clientIp);
    59	                    exchange.getResponse().setStatusCode(HttpStatus.TOO_MANY_REQUESTS);
    60	                    exchange.getResponse().getHeaders().add("X-Rate-Limit-Retry-After-Seconds", "60");
    61	                    return exchange.getResponse().setComplete();
    62	                });
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    @Override
    66	    public int getOrder() {
    67	        // Run early in the filter chain, before routing
    68	        return Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE + 1;
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    // ─── Helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    72	
    73	    private Bucket resolveBucket(String clientIp) {
    74	        return buckets.computeIfAbsent(clientIp, ip -> {
    75	            Bandwidth limit = Bandwidth.classic(
    76	                    REQUEST_LIMIT,
    77	                    Refill.greedy(REQUEST_LIMIT, REFILL_DURATION)
    78	            );
    79	            return Bucket.builder().addLimit(limit).build();
    80	        });
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    private String resolveClientIp(ServerWebExchange exchange) {
    84	        // Prefer X-Forwarded-For for requests passing through a load balancer
    85	        String forwarded = exchange.getRequest().getHeaders().getFirst("X-Forwarded-For");
    86	        if (forwarded != null && !forwarded.isBlank()) {
    87	            return forwarded.split(",")[0].trim();
    88	        }
    89	        var remoteAddress = exchange.getRequest().getRemoteAddress();
    90	        return remoteAddress != null ? remoteAddress.getAddress().getHostAddress() : "unknown";
    91	    }
    92	}
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/InternalSecretFilterConfig.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/InternalSecretFilterConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.security;
     2	
     3	import io.jsonwebtoken.Claims;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     6	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     7	import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GlobalFilter;
     8	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     9	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
    10	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    11	import org.springframework.http.HttpHeaders;
    12	import org.springframework.http.server.reactive.ServerHttpRequest;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Gateway-level security filters applied to every forwarded request.
    16	 *
    17	 * Order of operations (single filter, single mutate call):
    18	 *  1. Strip any client-supplied X-User-* headers (prevent header spoofing).
    19	 *  2. If a valid Bearer token is present, extract JWT claims and inject
    20	 *     X-User-UUID, X-User-Role, X-User-Email so downstream services know
    21	 *     who the caller is without ever touching a JWT themselves.
    22	 *  3. Inject X-Internal-Secret so downstream services can reject requests
    23	 *     that bypass the gateway entirely.
    24	 */
    25	@Slf4j
    26	@Configuration
    27	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    28	public class InternalSecretFilterConfig {
    29	
    30	    private final JwtUtil jwtUtil;
    31	
    32	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    33	    private String internalSecret;
    34	
    35	    @Bean
    36	    @Order(Integer.MIN_VALUE) // Run before any route-level filter
    37	    public GlobalFilter securityHeadersFilter() {
    38	        return (exchange, chain) -> {
    39	
    40	            ServerHttpRequest.Builder mutated = exchange.getRequest().mutate();
    41	
    42	            // ── Step 1: Strip spoofable identity headers from the incoming client request ──
    43	            mutated.headers(h -> {
    44	                h.remove("X-User-UUID");
    45	                h.remove("X-User-Role");
    46	                h.remove("X-User-Email");
    47	            });
    48	
    49	            // ── Step 2: Inject validated identity from JWT (if present) ──
    50	            String authHeader = exchange.getRequest()
    51	                    .getHeaders()
    52	                    .getFirst(HttpHeaders.AUTHORIZATION);
    53	
    54	            if (authHeader != null && authHeader.startsWith("Bearer ")) {
    55	                String token = authHeader.substring(7);
    56	                try {
    57	                    Claims claims = jwtUtil.validateToken(token);
    58	                    String uuid = claims.get("uuid", String.class);
    59	                    String role = claims.get("role", String.class);
    60	                    String email = claims.getSubject();
    61	
    62	                    if (uuid != null)  mutated.header("X-User-UUID", uuid);
    63	                    if (role != null)  mutated.header("X-User-Role", role);
    64	                    if (email != null) mutated.header("X-User-Email", email);
    65	
    66	                } catch (Exception e) {
    67	                    // JWT is invalid — SecurityConfig will have already rejected
    68	                    // authenticated routes. For public routes we just skip headers.
    69	                    log.debug("Could not extract JWT claims for header injection: {}", e.getMessage());
    70	                }
    71	            }
    72	
    73	            // ── Step 3: Inject internal secret so downstream services reject direct access ──
    74	            mutated.header("X-Internal-Secret", internalSecret);
    75	
    76	            return chain.filter(
    77	                    exchange.mutate().request(mutated.build()).build()
    78	            );
    79	        };
    80	    }
    81	}
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/JwtAuthenticationConverter.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/JwtAuthenticationConverter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.security;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.http.HttpHeaders;
     4	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     5	import org.springframework.security.core.Authentication;
     6	import org.springframework.security.web.server.authentication.ServerAuthenticationConverter;
     7	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     8	import org.springframework.web.server.ServerWebExchange;
     9	import reactor.core.publisher.Mono;
    10	
    11	@Component
    12	public class JwtAuthenticationConverter implements ServerAuthenticationConverter {
    13	
    14	    @Override
    15	    public Mono<Authentication> convert(ServerWebExchange exchange) {
    16	
    17	        String authHeader = exchange.getRequest()
    18	                .getHeaders()
    19	                .getFirst(HttpHeaders.AUTHORIZATION);
    20	
    21	        if (authHeader == null || !authHeader.startsWith("Bearer ")) {
    22	            return Mono.empty();
    23	        }
    24	
    25	        String token = authHeader.substring(7);
    26	
    27	        Authentication authentication =
    28	                new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(token, token);
    29	
    30	        return Mono.just(authentication);
    31	    }
    32	}
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/JwtAuthenticationManager.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/JwtAuthenticationManager.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.security;
     2	
     3	import io.jsonwebtoken.Claims;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.security.authentication.BadCredentialsException;
     6	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     7	import org.springframework.security.core.Authentication;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
     9	import org.springframework.security.core.AuthenticationException;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import reactor.core.publisher.Mono;
    12	
    13	import java.util.List;
    14	
    15	@Component
    16	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    17	public class JwtAuthenticationManager implements
    18	        org.springframework.security.authentication.ReactiveAuthenticationManager {
    19	
    20	    private final JwtUtil jwtUtil;
    21	
    22	    @Override
    23	    public Mono<Authentication> authenticate(Authentication authentication)
    24	            throws AuthenticationException {
    25	
    26	        String token = authentication.getCredentials().toString();
    27	
    28	        try {
    29	            Claims claims = jwtUtil.validateToken(token);
    30	
    31	            String role = claims.get("role", String.class);
    32	            String uuid = claims.get("uuid", String.class);
    33	            String email = claims.getSubject();
    34	
    35	            List<SimpleGrantedAuthority> authorities =
    36	                    List.of(new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role));
    37	
    38	            UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken auth =
    39	                    new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(
    40	                            email,
    41	                            null,
    42	                            authorities
    43	                    );
    44	            // Store uuid so ClaimsForwardingFilter can read it without re-parsing
    45	            auth.setDetails(uuid);
    46	
    47	            return Mono.just(auth);
    48	
    49	        } catch (Exception e) {
    50	            // Return error so Spring Security properly sends 401 Unauthorized
    51	            return Mono.error(new BadCredentialsException("Invalid or expired JWT token"));
    52	        }
    53	    }
    54	}
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/JwtUtil.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/JwtUtil.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.security;
     2	
     3	import io.jsonwebtoken.*;
     4	import io.jsonwebtoken.security.Keys;
     5	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     6	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     7	
     8	import java.security.Key;
     9	
    10	@Component
    11	public class JwtUtil {
    12	
    13	    private final Key signingKey;
    14	
    15	    public JwtUtil(@Value("${jwt.secret}") String secret) {
    16	        this.signingKey = Keys.hmacShaKeyFor(secret.getBytes());
    17	    }
    18	
    19	    public Claims validateToken(String token) {
    20	
    21	        return Jwts.parserBuilder()
    22	                .setSigningKey(signingKey)
    23	                .build()
    24	                .parseClaimsJws(token)
    25	                .getBody();
    26	    }
    27	}
```

## api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `api-gateway/src/main/java/com/sourabh/api_gateway/security/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.api_gateway.security;
     2	
     3	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     4	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     6	import org.springframework.security.authentication.ReactiveAuthenticationManager;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.reactive.EnableWebFluxSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.config.web.server.SecurityWebFiltersOrder;
     9	import org.springframework.security.config.web.server.ServerHttpSecurity;
    10	import org.springframework.security.web.server.SecurityWebFilterChain;
    11	import org.springframework.security.web.server.authentication.AuthenticationWebFilter;
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * Gateway-level security.
    15	 *
    16	 * JWT is validated HERE only — downstream services never see raw JWTs.
    17	 * Public paths are whitelisted; everything else requires a valid Bearer token.
    18	 */
    19	@Configuration
    20	@EnableWebFluxSecurity
    21	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    22	public class SecurityConfig {
    23	
    24	    // Paths that do NOT require a JWT (login, register, Swagger, etc.)
    25	    private static final String[] PUBLIC_PATHS = {
    26	            "/api/auth/login",
    27	            "/api/auth/refresh",
    28	            "/api/user/register",
    29	            "/api/user/verify-otp",
    30	            "/api/user/resend-otp",
    31	            // Swagger UI (served by gateway itself)
    32	            "/swagger-ui.html",
    33	            "/swagger-ui/**",
    34	            "/v3/api-docs/**",
    35	            "/webjars/**",
    36	            // Per-service OpenAPI docs fetched by the aggregated Swagger UI
    37	            "/api/auth/v3/api-docs",
    38	            "/api/user/v3/api-docs",
    39	            "/api/product/v3/api-docs",
    40	            "/api/order/v3/api-docs",
    41	            "/api/review/v3/api-docs",
    42	            "/api/payment/v3/api-docs",
    43	            // Public product catalog (read-only)
    44	            "/api/product"
    45	    };
    46	
    47	    @Bean
    48	    public SecurityWebFilterChain securityWebFilterChain(
    49	            ServerHttpSecurity http,
    50	            JwtAuthenticationManager jwtAuthManager,
    51	            JwtAuthenticationConverter jwtAuthConverter) {
    52	
    53	        // Build a dedicated filter that plugs our JWT manager + converter
    54	        AuthenticationWebFilter jwtFilter = new AuthenticationWebFilter(
    55	                (ReactiveAuthenticationManager) jwtAuthManager);
    56	        jwtFilter.setServerAuthenticationConverter(jwtAuthConverter);
    57	
    58	        return http
    59	                .csrf(ServerHttpSecurity.CsrfSpec::disable)
    60	                .formLogin(ServerHttpSecurity.FormLoginSpec::disable)
    61	                .httpBasic(ServerHttpSecurity.HttpBasicSpec::disable)
    62	                .logout(ServerHttpSecurity.LogoutSpec::disable)
    63	                // Register the JWT filter in the authentication slot
    64	                .addFilterAt(jwtFilter, SecurityWebFiltersOrder.AUTHENTICATION)
    65	                .authorizeExchange(exchange -> exchange
    66	                        .pathMatchers(PUBLIC_PATHS).permitAll()
    67	                        .anyExchange().authenticated()
    68	                )
    69	                .build();
    70	    }
    71	}
```

## auth-service/dockerfile

Path: `auth-service/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl auth-service dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY auth-service/src auth-service/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl auth-service package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/auth-service/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8080
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	
     8	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    11	
    12	import java.io.IOException;
    13	
    14	@Component
    15	public class InternalSecretFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    16	
    17	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    18	    private String internalSecret;
    19	
    20	    @Override
    21	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    22	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    23	                                    FilterChain filterChain)
    24	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    25	
    26	        String header = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (!internalSecret.equals(header)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    34	    }
    35	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/config/OpenApiConfig.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/config/OpenApiConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.config;
     2	
     3	import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.OpenAPI;
     4	import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.servers.Server;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	
     8	import java.util.List;
     9	
    10	@Configuration
    11	public class OpenApiConfig {
    12	
    13	    @Bean
    14	    public OpenAPI customOpenAPI() {
    15	        Server server = new Server();
    16	        server.setUrl("/");
    17	        return new OpenAPI().servers(List.of(server));
    18	    }
    19	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/config/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/config/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     4	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     6	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.method.configuration.EnableMethodSecurity;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.userdetails.UserDetailsService;
     9	import org.springframework.security.crypto.bcrypt.BCryptPasswordEncoder;
    10	import org.springframework.security.crypto.password.PasswordEncoder;
    11	import org.springframework.security.provisioning.InMemoryUserDetailsManager;
    12	import org.springframework.security.web.SecurityFilterChain;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Auth-service security config.
    16	 *
    17	 * JWT validation is handled exclusively at the API Gateway.
    18	 * This service only needs to:
    19	 *   1. Permit all requests (gateway forwards with X-Internal-Secret, checked
    20	 *      by InternalSecretFilter before Spring Security runs).
    21	 *   2. Provide a PasswordEncoder bean for BCrypt operations.
    22	 *
    23	 * @EnableMethodSecurity enables @PreAuthorize annotations on controller methods.
    24	 */
    25	@Configuration
    26	@EnableMethodSecurity
    27	public class SecurityConfig {
    28	
    29	    @Bean
    30	    public UserDetailsService userDetailsService() {
    31	        return new InMemoryUserDetailsManager();
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @Bean
    35	    public SecurityFilterChain securityFilterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
    36	        http
    37	                .csrf(csrf -> csrf.disable())
    38	                .formLogin(form -> form.disable())
    39	                .httpBasic(basic -> basic.disable())
    40	                .exceptionHandling(ex -> ex
    41	                        // Return plain 403 — never emit WWW-Authenticate which triggers browser Basic-Auth popup
    42	                        .authenticationEntryPoint((req, res, e) ->
    43	                                res.sendError(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN, "Forbidden"))
    44	                )
    45	                .authorizeHttpRequests(auth -> auth
    46	                        .anyRequest().permitAll()  // InternalSecretFilter guards all paths
    47	                );
    48	        return http.build();
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    @Bean
    52	    public PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder() {
    53	        return new BCryptPasswordEncoder();
    54	    }
    55	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/controller/AuthController.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/controller/AuthController.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.controller;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.auth_service.dto.request.LoginRequest;
     4	import com.sourabh.auth_service.dto.response.AuthResponse;
     5	import com.sourabh.auth_service.service.AuthService;
     6	import jakarta.validation.Valid;
     7	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     8	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     9	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    10	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
    11	
    12	@RestController
    13	@RequestMapping("/api/auth")
    14	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    15	@Slf4j
    16	public class AuthController {
    17	
    18	    private final AuthService authService;
    19	
    20	    @PostMapping("/login")
    21	    public ResponseEntity<AuthResponse> login(@Valid @RequestBody LoginRequest request) {
    22	        return ResponseEntity.ok(authService.login(request));
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    @PostMapping("/refresh")
    26	    public ResponseEntity<AuthResponse> refresh(@RequestParam String refreshToken) {
    27	        return ResponseEntity.ok(authService.refreshToken(refreshToken));
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    @PostMapping("/logout")
    31	    public ResponseEntity<Void> logout(@RequestParam String refreshToken) {
    32	        authService.logout(refreshToken);
    33	        return ResponseEntity.noContent().build();
    34	    }
    35	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/entity/RefreshToken.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/entity/RefreshToken.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.*;
     5	
     6	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
     7	
     8	@Entity
     9	@Getter
    10	@Setter
    11	@Builder
    12	@NoArgsConstructor
    13	@AllArgsConstructor
    14	public class RefreshToken {
    15	
    16	    @Id
    17	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    18	    private Long id;
    19	
    20	    @Column(nullable = false, unique = true)
    21	    private String token;
    22	
    23	    @Column(nullable = false)
    24	    private String userUuid;
    25	
    26	    @Column(nullable = false)
    27	    private LocalDateTime expiryDate;
    28	
    29	    @Column(nullable = false)
    30	    private boolean revoked;
    31	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.exception;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.auth_service.common.ErrorResponse;
     4	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     5	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
     7	import org.springframework.validation.FieldError;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
     9	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ExceptionHandler;
    10	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestControllerAdvice;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	import java.util.List;
    14	import java.util.stream.Collectors;
    15	
    16	@Slf4j
    17	@RestControllerAdvice
    18	public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
    19	
    20	    @ExceptionHandler(AuthException.class)
    21	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleAuthException(AuthException ex) {
    22	        return buildError("AUTH_ERROR", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.UNAUTHORIZED);
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    @ExceptionHandler(UserAccountException.class)
    26	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleUserAccountException(UserAccountException ex) {
    27	        return buildError("USER_ACCOUNT_ERROR", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.FORBIDDEN);
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    @ExceptionHandler(UserNotFoundException.class)
    31	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleUserNotFoundException(UserNotFoundException ex) {
    32	        return buildError("USER_NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    36	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    37	        List<String> errors = ex.getBindingResult()
    38	                .getFieldErrors()
    39	                .stream()
    40	                .map(fe -> fe.getField() + " : " + fe.getDefaultMessage())
    41	                .collect(Collectors.toList());
    42	
    43	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    44	                .errorCode("VALIDATION_ERROR")
    45	                .message("Validation failed")
    46	                .details(errors)
    47	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    48	                .build();
    49	
    50	        return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(response);
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    54	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGenericException(Exception ex) {
    55	        log.error("Unexpected error in auth-service: {}", ex.getMessage(), ex);
    56	        return buildError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", "Something went wrong", HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR);
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    private ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> buildError(String code, String message, HttpStatus status) {
    60	        return new ResponseEntity<>(
    61	                ErrorResponse.builder()
    62	                        .errorCode(code)
    63	                        .message(message)
    64	                        .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    65	                        .build(),
    66	                status);
    67	    }
    68	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.filter;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     8	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     9	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.UUID;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Picks up the {@code X-Correlation-Id} header set by the API Gateway and
    18	 * stores it in SLF4J MDC so it appears in every log statement for the request.
    19	 *
    20	 * <p>Also attaches the header to the HTTP response so callers can trace
    21	 * requests end-to-end.
    22	 */
    23	@Component
    24	@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    25	public class CorrelationIdFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    26	
    27	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    28	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    29	
    30	    @Override
    31	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    32	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    33	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    34	        String correlationId = request.getHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    35	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    36	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        MDC.put(MDC_KEY, correlationId);
    40	        response.addHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, correlationId);
    41	
    42	        try {
    43	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    44	        } finally {
    45	            MDC.remove(MDC_KEY);
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/security/JwtAuthenticationFilter.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/security/JwtAuthenticationFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.security;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.auth_service.util.JwtUtil;
     4	import io.jsonwebtoken.JwtException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     7	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     8	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     9	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    10	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    11	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
    12	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
    13	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    14	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    15	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    16	
    17	import java.io.IOException;
    18	import java.util.Collections;
    19	
    20	@Component
    21	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    22	@Slf4j
    23	public class JwtAuthenticationFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    24	
    25	    private final JwtUtil jwtUtil;
    26	
    27	    @Override
    28	    protected void doFilterInternal(
    29	            HttpServletRequest request,
    30	            HttpServletResponse response,
    31	            FilterChain filterChain)
    32	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    33	
    34	        String header = request.getHeader("Authorization");
    35	
    36	        if (header == null || !header.startsWith("Bearer ")) {
    37	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    38	            return;
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        String token = header.substring(7);
    42	
    43	        try {
    44	            if (jwtUtil.validateToken(token)) {
    45	
    46	                String email = jwtUtil.extractEmail(token);
    47	                String role = jwtUtil.extractRole(token);
    48	
    49	                UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken authentication =
    50	                        new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(
    51	                                email,
    52	                                null,
    53	                                Collections.singletonList(
    54	                                        new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role)
    55	                                )
    56	                        );
    57	
    58	                SecurityContextHolder.getContext()
    59	                        .setAuthentication(authentication);
    60	            }
    61	
    62	        } catch (JwtException e) {
    63	            log.error("Invalid JWT token: {}", e.getMessage());
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    67	    }
    68	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/service/impl/AuthServiceImpl.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/service/impl/AuthServiceImpl.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.service.impl;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.auth_service.dto.UserDto;
     4	import com.sourabh.auth_service.dto.request.LoginRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.auth_service.dto.response.AuthResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.auth_service.entity.RefreshToken;
     7	import com.sourabh.auth_service.exception.AuthException;
     8	import com.sourabh.auth_service.exception.UserAccountException;
     9	import com.sourabh.auth_service.exception.UserNotFoundException;
    10	import com.sourabh.auth_service.repository.RefreshTokenRepository;
    11	import com.sourabh.auth_service.service.AuthService;
    12	import com.sourabh.auth_service.util.JwtUtil;
    13	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    14	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    15	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
    16	import org.springframework.http.HttpEntity;
    17	import org.springframework.http.HttpHeaders;
    18	import org.springframework.http.HttpMethod;
    19	import org.springframework.security.crypto.password.PasswordEncoder;
    20	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    21	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    22	import org.springframework.web.client.HttpClientErrorException;
    23	import org.springframework.web.client.RestTemplate;
    24	
    25	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    26	import java.util.Optional;
    27	import java.util.UUID;
    28	
    29	@Service
    30	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    31	@Slf4j
    32	public class AuthServiceImpl implements AuthService {
    33	
    34	    private final RestTemplate restTemplate;
    35	    private final JwtUtil jwtUtil;
    36	    private final PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder;
    37	    private final RefreshTokenRepository refreshTokenRepository;
    38	
    39	    @Value("${jwt.refresh-token-expiration}")
    40	    private long refreshTokenExpiration;
    41	
    42	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    43	    private String internalSecret;
    44	
    45	    private static final String USER_BY_EMAIL_URL = "http://user-service:8080/api/user/internal/email/";
    46	    private static final String USER_BY_UUID_URL  = "http://user-service:8080/api/user/internal/uuid/";
    47	
    48	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    49	    // LOGIN
    50	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    51	
    52	    @Override
    53	    @Transactional
    54	    public AuthResponse login(LoginRequest request) {
    55	        log.info("Login attempt for email: {}", request.getEmail());
    56	
    57	        UserDto user = fetchUser(USER_BY_EMAIL_URL + request.getEmail())
    58	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AuthException("Invalid credentials"));
    59	
    60	        validateActiveAccount(user);
    61	
    62	        if (!passwordEncoder.matches(request.getPassword(), user.getPassword())) {
    63	            throw new AuthException("Invalid credentials");
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        String accessToken       = jwtUtil.generateAccessToken(user.getEmail(), user.getUuid(), user.getRole());
    67	        String refreshTokenValue = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    68	
    69	        refreshTokenRepository.save(buildRefreshToken(refreshTokenValue, user.getUuid()));
    70	
    71	        log.info("Login successful for user: {}", user.getEmail());
    72	        return buildAuthResponse(accessToken, refreshTokenValue);
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    76	    // REFRESH TOKEN (rotation: revoke old, issue new)
    77	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    78	
    79	    @Override
    80	    @Transactional
    81	    public AuthResponse refreshToken(String refreshTokenValue) {
    82	        RefreshToken refreshToken = refreshTokenRepository.findByToken(refreshTokenValue)
    83	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AuthException("Invalid refresh token"));
    84	
    85	        if (refreshToken.isRevoked()) {
    86	            throw new AuthException("Refresh token has been revoked");
    87	        }
    88	        if (refreshToken.getExpiryDate().isBefore(LocalDateTime.now())) {
    89	            throw new AuthException("Refresh token has expired");
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        UserDto user = fetchUser(USER_BY_UUID_URL + refreshToken.getUserUuid())
    93	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
    94	
    95	        if (!"ACTIVE".equalsIgnoreCase(user.getStatus())) {
    96	            throw new UserAccountException("User account is no longer active");
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        // Rotate: revoke old, issue new pair
   100	        refreshToken.setRevoked(true);
   101	        refreshTokenRepository.save(refreshToken);
   102	
   103	        String newAccessToken       = jwtUtil.generateAccessToken(user.getEmail(), user.getUuid(), user.getRole());
   104	        String newRefreshTokenValue = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   105	
   106	        refreshTokenRepository.save(buildRefreshToken(newRefreshTokenValue, user.getUuid()));
   107	
   108	        return buildAuthResponse(newAccessToken, newRefreshTokenValue);
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   112	    // Private helpers
   113	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   114	
   115	    /**
   116	     * Generic internal user fetch — attaches X-Internal-Secret header.
   117	     * Returns empty Optional on 404; logs and returns empty on other client errors.
   118	     */
   119	    private Optional<UserDto> fetchUser(String url) {
   120	        try {
   121	            HttpHeaders headers = new HttpHeaders();
   122	            headers.set("X-Internal-Secret", internalSecret);
   123	            UserDto body = restTemplate
   124	                    .exchange(url, HttpMethod.GET, new HttpEntity<>(headers), UserDto.class)
   125	                    .getBody();
   126	            return Optional.ofNullable(body);
   127	        } catch (HttpClientErrorException.NotFound e) {
   128	            return Optional.empty();
   129	        } catch (HttpClientErrorException e) {
   130	            log.warn("HTTP error fetching user from {}: {} {}", url, e.getStatusCode(), e.getMessage());
   131	            return Optional.empty();
   132	        }
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    private void validateActiveAccount(UserDto user) {
   136	        if (!user.isEmailVerified()) {
   137	            throw new UserAccountException("Email not verified");
   138	        }
   139	        if (!"ACTIVE".equalsIgnoreCase(user.getStatus())) {
   140	            throw new UserAccountException("User account is not active");
   141	        }
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    private RefreshToken buildRefreshToken(String token, String userUuid) {
   145	        return RefreshToken.builder()
   146	                .token(token)
   147	                .userUuid(userUuid)
   148	                .expiryDate(LocalDateTime.now().plusSeconds(refreshTokenExpiration / 1000))
   149	                .revoked(false)
   150	                .build();
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    private AuthResponse buildAuthResponse(String accessToken, String refreshToken) {
   154	        return AuthResponse.builder()
   155	                .accessToken(accessToken)
   156	                .refreshToken(refreshToken)
   157	                .tokenType("Bearer")
   158	                .build();
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   162	    // LOGOUT — revoke the supplied refresh token
   163	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   164	
   165	    @Override
   166	    @Transactional
   167	    public void logout(String refreshTokenValue) {
   168	        RefreshToken refreshToken = refreshTokenRepository.findByToken(refreshTokenValue)
   169	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AuthException("Invalid refresh token"));
   170	
   171	        if (!refreshToken.isRevoked()) {
   172	            refreshToken.setRevoked(true);
   173	            refreshTokenRepository.save(refreshToken);
   174	            log.info("User logged out: userUuid={}", refreshToken.getUserUuid());
   175	        }
   176	    }
   177	}
```

## auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/util/JwtUtil.java

Path: `auth-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/auth_service/util/JwtUtil.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.auth_service.util;
     2	
     3	import io.jsonwebtoken.*;
     4	import io.jsonwebtoken.security.Keys;
     5	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     6	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     7	
     8	import java.security.Key;
     9	import java.util.Date;
    10	import java.util.Map;
    11	
    12	@Component
    13	public class JwtUtil {
    14	
    15	    private final Key signingKey;
    16	    private final long accessTokenExpiration;
    17	
    18	    public JwtUtil(
    19	            @Value("${jwt.secret}") String secret,
    20	            @Value("${jwt.access-token-expiration}") long accessTokenExpiration) {
    21	
    22	        this.signingKey = Keys.hmacShaKeyFor(secret.getBytes());
    23	        this.accessTokenExpiration = accessTokenExpiration;
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    // ==========================
    27	    // Generate Access Token
    28	    // ==========================
    29	
    30	    public String generateAccessToken(
    31	            String email,
    32	            String userUuid,
    33	            String role) {
    34	
    35	        return Jwts.builder()
    36	                .setSubject(email)
    37	                .addClaims(Map.of(
    38	                        "uuid", userUuid,
    39	                        "role", role
    40	                ))
    41	                .setIssuedAt(new Date())
    42	                .setExpiration(new Date(System.currentTimeMillis() + accessTokenExpiration))
    43	                .signWith(signingKey, SignatureAlgorithm.HS256)
    44	                .compact();
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    // ==========================
    48	    // Extract Claims
    49	    // ==========================
    50	
    51	    public String extractEmail(String token) {
    52	        return extractAllClaims(token).getSubject();
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    public String extractUserUuid(String token) {
    56	        return extractAllClaims(token).get("uuid", String.class);
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    public String extractRole(String token) {
    60	        return extractAllClaims(token).get("role", String.class);
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    // ==========================
    64	    // Validate Token
    65	    // ==========================
    66	
    67	    public boolean validateToken(String token) {
    68	        try {
    69	            extractAllClaims(token);
    70	            return true;
    71	        } catch (JwtException | IllegalArgumentException e) {
    72	            return false;
    73	        }
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    // ==========================
    77	    // Internal Helper
    78	    // ==========================
    79	
    80	    private Claims extractAllClaims(String token) {
    81	
    82	        return Jwts.parserBuilder()
    83	                .setSigningKey(signingKey)
    84	                .build()
    85	                .parseClaimsJws(token)
    86	                .getBody();
    87	    }
    88	}
```

```properties
    15	jwt.refresh-token-expiration=604800000
```

## auth-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql

Path: `auth-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql`

```sql
     1	-- auth-service: initial schema
     2	-- Creates refresh_token table; user data lives in user-service's DB.
     3	
     4	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS refresh_token (
     5	    id           BIGSERIAL    PRIMARY KEY,
     6	    token        VARCHAR(512) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
     7	    user_uuid    VARCHAR(36)  NOT NULL,
     8	    expiry_date  TIMESTAMP    NOT NULL,
     9	    revoked      BOOLEAN      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE
    10	);
    11	
    12	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_refresh_token_user_uuid ON refresh_token(user_uuid);
    13	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_refresh_token_token     ON refresh_token(token);
```

## config-server/dockerfile

Path: `config-server/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl config-server dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY config-server/src config-server/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl config-server package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/config-server/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8888
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## config-server/src/main/java/com/sourabh/config_server/ConfigServerApplication.java

Path: `config-server/src/main/java/com/sourabh/config_server/ConfigServerApplication.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.config_server;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
     4	import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;
     5	import org.springframework.cloud.config.server.EnableConfigServer;
     6	
     7	@SpringBootApplication
     8	@EnableConfigServer
     9	public class ConfigServerApplication {
    10	    public static void main(String[] args) {
    11	        SpringApplication.run(ConfigServerApplication.class, args);
    12	    }
    13	}
```

## config-server/src/main/resources/config/application.properties

Path: `config-server/src/main/resources/config/application.properties`

```properties
     1	# ==========================================================
     2	# SHARED CONFIG — applies to ALL services
     3	# Individual service files override specific properties.
     4	# ==========================================================
     5	
     6	# Eureka client registration (all services)
     7	eureka.client.service-url.defaultZone=${EUREKA_URL:http://eureka-server:8761/eureka}
     8	eureka.client.fetch-registry=true
     9	eureka.client.register-with-eureka=true
    10	eureka.instance.prefer-ip-address=true
    11	eureka.instance.lease-renewal-interval-in-seconds=10
    12	eureka.instance.lease-expiration-duration-in-seconds=30
    13	
    14	# Distributed Tracing (Zipkin)
    15	management.tracing.sampling.probability=1.0
    16	management.zipkin.tracing.endpoint=${ZIPKIN_URL:http://zipkin:9411/api/v2/spans}
    17	
    18	# Actuator
    19	management.endpoints.web.exposure.include=health,info,metrics,prometheus,refresh
    20	management.endpoint.health.show-details=always
    21	management.metrics.export.prometheus.enabled=true
    22	
    23	# Logging pattern (JSON-friendly with traceId)
    24	logging.pattern.console=%d{yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss.SSS} [%thread] %-5level [traceId=%X{traceId}] [spanId=%X{spanId}] %logger{36} - %msg%n
    25	
    26	# Shared secrets (override with env vars in production)
    27	jwt.secret=${JWT_SECRET:mysupersecuresecretkeythatislongenough123}
    28	internal.secret=${INTERNAL_SECRET:veryStrongInternalSecret123}
```

## docker-compose.yml

Path: `docker-compose.yml`

```yaml
     1	version: '3.8'
     2	
     3	# Shared environment — single source of truth for secrets.
     4	# Override with a .env file or Docker secrets in production.
     5	x-common-env: &common-env
     6	  DB_USERNAME: postgres
     7	  DB_PASSWORD: postgres
     8	  JWT_SECRET: mysupersecuresecretkeythatislongenough123
     9	  INTERNAL_SECRET: veryStrongInternalSecret123
    10	  KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS: kafka:9092
    11	  ZIPKIN_URL: http://zipkin:9411/api/v2/spans
    12	  EUREKA_URL: http://eureka-server:8761/eureka
    13	  CONFIG_SERVER_URL: http://config-server:8888
    14	  REDIS_HOST: redis
    15	  REDIS_PORT: 6379
    16	
    17	services:
    18	
    19	  postgres:
    20	    image: postgres:15
    21	    environment:
    22	      POSTGRES_USER: postgres
    23	      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
    24	    ports:
    25	      - "5432:5432"
    26	    volumes:
    27	      - pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    28	      - ./init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    29	    healthcheck:
    30	      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U postgres"]
    31	      interval: 10s
    32	      timeout: 5s
    33	      retries: 5
    34	      start_period: 10s
    35	
    36	  redis:
    37	    image: redis:7
    38	    ports:
    39	      - "6379:6379"
    40	    healthcheck:
    41	      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
    42	      interval: 10s
    43	      timeout: 5s
    44	      retries: 5
    45	      start_period: 5s
    46	
    47	  kafka:
    48	    image: apache/kafka:3.7.0
    49	    environment:
    50	      KAFKA_NODE_ID: 1
    51	      KAFKA_PROCESS_ROLES: broker,controller
    52	      KAFKA_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://:9092,CONTROLLER://:9093,PLAINTEXT_HOST://:29092
    53	      KAFKA_ADVERTISED_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://kafka:9092,PLAINTEXT_HOST://localhost:29092
    54	      KAFKA_CONTROLLER_LISTENER_NAMES: CONTROLLER
    55	      KAFKA_LISTENER_SECURITY_PROTOCOL_MAP: CONTROLLER:PLAINTEXT,PLAINTEXT:PLAINTEXT,PLAINTEXT_HOST:PLAINTEXT
    56	      KAFKA_CONTROLLER_QUORUM_VOTERS: 1@kafka:9093
    57	      KAFKA_OFFSETS_TOPIC_REPLICATION_FACTOR: 1
```

## eureka-server/dockerfile

Path: `eureka-server/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl eureka-server dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY eureka-server/src eureka-server/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl eureka-server package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/eureka-server/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8761
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## eureka-server/pom.xml

Path: `eureka-server/pom.xml`

```xml
     1	<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
     2	<project xmlns="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0"
     3	         xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"
     4	         xsi:schemaLocation="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0 https://maven.apache.org/xsd/maven-4.0.0.xsd">
     5	    <modelVersion>4.0.0</modelVersion>
     6	
     7	    <parent>
     8	        <groupId>com.sourabh</groupId>
     9	        <artifactId>ecommerce-backend</artifactId>
    10	        <version>1.0.0</version>
    11	        <relativePath>../pom.xml</relativePath>
    12	    </parent>
    13	
    14	    <artifactId>eureka-server</artifactId>
    15	    <version>1.0.0</version>
    16	    <name>eureka-server</name>
    17	
    18	    <dependencies>
    19	        <dependency>
    20	            <groupId>org.springframework.cloud</groupId>
    21	            <artifactId>spring-cloud-starter-netflix-eureka-server</artifactId>
    22	        </dependency>
    23	        <dependency>
    24	            <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
    25	            <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-actuator</artifactId>
    26	        </dependency>
    27	        <!-- Exclude ribbon/archaius from pulling in old deps -->
    28	        <dependency>
    29	            <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
    30	            <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-test</artifactId>
    31	            <scope>test</scope>
    32	        </dependency>
    33	    </dependencies>
    34	</project>
```

## eureka-server/src/main/java/com/sourabh/eureka_server/EurekaServerApplication.java

Path: `eureka-server/src/main/java/com/sourabh/eureka_server/EurekaServerApplication.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.eureka_server;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
     4	import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;
     5	import org.springframework.cloud.netflix.eureka.server.EnableEurekaServer;
     6	
     7	@SpringBootApplication
     8	@EnableEurekaServer
     9	public class EurekaServerApplication {
    10	    public static void main(String[] args) {
    11	        SpringApplication.run(EurekaServerApplication.class, args);
    12	    }
    13	}
```

## eureka-server/src/main/resources/application.properties

Path: `eureka-server/src/main/resources/application.properties`

```properties
     1	spring.application.name=eureka-server
     2	server.port=8761
     3	
     4	# Standalone mode - do not try to register with or fetch from itself
     5	eureka.client.register-with-eureka=false
     6	eureka.client.fetch-registry=false
     7	eureka.server.wait-time-in-ms-when-sync-empty=0
     8	
     9	eureka.instance.hostname=eureka-server
    10	
    11	management.endpoints.web.exposure.include=health,info
    12	management.endpoint.health.show-details=always
    13	
    14	logging.level.com.netflix.eureka=WARN
    15	logging.level.com.netflix.discovery=WARN
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/OrderServiceApplication.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
     4	import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.config.EnableJpaAuditing;
     5	import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;
     6	import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.EnableFeignClients;
     7	
     8	@SpringBootApplication
     9	@EnableJpaAuditing
    10	@EnableFeignClients
    11	public class OrderServiceApplication {
    12	
    13	    public static void main(String[] args) {
    14	        SpringApplication.run(OrderServiceApplication.class, args);
    15	    }
    16	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/common/ErrorResponse.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/common/ErrorResponse.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.common;
     2	
     3	import lombok.Builder;
     4	import lombok.Getter;
     5	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
     6	import java.util.List;
     7	
     8	@Getter
     9	@Builder
    10	public class ErrorResponse {
    11	    private String errorCode;
    12	    private String message;
    13	    private List<String> details;
    14	    private LocalDateTime timestamp;
    15	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/common/PageResponse.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/common/PageResponse.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.common;
     2	
     3	import lombok.Builder;
     4	import lombok.Getter;
     5	
     6	import java.util.List;
     7	
     8	@Getter
     9	@Builder
    10	public class PageResponse<T> {
    11	
    12	    private List<T> content;
    13	    private int page;
    14	    private int size;
    15	    private long totalElements;
    16	    private int totalPages;
    17	    private boolean last;
    18	}
```

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.config;
     2	
     3	import feign.RequestInterceptor;
     4	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	
     8	@Configuration
     9	public class FeignConfig {
    10	
    11	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    12	    private String internalSecret;
    13	
    14	    /**
    15	     * Adds X-Internal-Secret to every outbound Feign request so
    16	     * downstream services' InternalSecretFilter accepts the call.
    17	     * Named 'feignOutboundSecretInterceptor' to avoid collision with the
    18	     * inbound InternalSecretInterceptor security @Component.
    19	     */
    20	    @Bean
    21	    public RequestInterceptor feignOutboundSecretInterceptor() {
    22	        return template -> template.header("X-Internal-Secret", internalSecret);
    23	    }
    24	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
     9	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.Collections;
    15	import java.util.List;
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Reads the {@code X-User-Role} header forwarded by the API Gateway and
    19	 * populates the Spring Security context so that {@code @PreAuthorize}
    20	 * method-level annotations can be evaluated.
    21	 */
    22	@Component
    23	public class HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    24	
    25	    @Override
    26	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    27	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    28	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    29	        String role = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    30	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    31	
    32	        if (role != null && !role.isBlank()) {
    33	            List<SimpleGrantedAuthority> authorities =
    34	                    Collections.singletonList(new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role.toUpperCase()));
    35	            UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken authentication =
    36	                    new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(userUuid, null, authorities);
    37	            SecurityContextHolder.getContext().setAuthentication(authentication);
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    41	    }
    42	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	
     8	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    11	
    12	import java.io.IOException;
    13	
    14	@Component
    15	public class InternalSecretFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    16	
    17	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    18	    private String internalSecret;
    19	
    20	    @Override
    21	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    22	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    23	                                    FilterChain filterChain)
    24	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    25	
    26	        String header = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (!internalSecret.equals(header)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    34	    }
    35	}
```
