## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.config;
     2	
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
     5	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.jsontype.impl.LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator;
     6	import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
     7	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.EnableCaching;
     8	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     9	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
    10	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheConfiguration;
    11	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheManager;
    12	import org.springframework.data.redis.connection.RedisConnectionFactory;
    13	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer;
    14	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.RedisSerializationContext;
    15	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.StringRedisSerializer;
    16	
    17	import java.time.Duration;
    18	import java.util.HashMap;
    19	import java.util.Map;
    20	
    21	@Configuration
    22	@EnableCaching
    23	public class RedisCacheConfig {
    24	
    25	    /** Cache name — used in @Cacheable/@CacheEvict throughout order-service */
    26	    public static final String ORDERS_CACHE = "orders";
    27	
    28	    @Bean
    29	    public RedisCacheManager cacheManager(RedisConnectionFactory factory) {
    30	
    31	        ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
    32	        om.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    33	        om.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
    34	        om.activateDefaultTyping(
    35	                LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator.instance,
    36	                ObjectMapper.DefaultTyping.NON_FINAL);
    37	        GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer jsonSerializer =
    38	                new GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer(om);
    39	
    40	        RedisCacheConfiguration defaultConfig = RedisCacheConfiguration
    41	                .defaultCacheConfig()
    42	                .serializeKeysWith(
    43	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    44	                                .fromSerializer(new StringRedisSerializer()))
    45	                .serializeValuesWith(
    46	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    47	                                .fromSerializer(jsonSerializer))
    48	                .disableCachingNullValues();
    49	
    50	        Map<String, RedisCacheConfiguration> cacheConfigs = new HashMap<>();
    51	        cacheConfigs.put(ORDERS_CACHE, defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(10)));
    52	
    53	        return RedisCacheManager.builder(factory)
    54	                .cacheDefaults(defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(10)))
    55	                .withInitialCacheConfigurations(cacheConfigs)
    56	                .build();
    57	    }
    58	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.method.configuration.EnableMethodSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
     9	import org.springframework.security.config.http.SessionCreationPolicy;
    10	import org.springframework.security.web.SecurityFilterChain;
    11	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter;
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * JWT validation happens at the API Gateway; this service trusts the
    15	 * forwarded {@code X-User-Role} header for method-level RBAC via {@code @PreAuthorize}.
    16	 */
    17	@Configuration
    18	@EnableMethodSecurity
    19	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    20	public class SecurityConfig {
    21	
    22	    private final HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter headerRoleAuthFilter;
    23	
    24	    @Bean
    25	    public SecurityFilterChain securityFilterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
    26	        http
    27	                .csrf(csrf -> csrf.disable())
    28	                .formLogin(form -> form.disable())
    29	                .httpBasic(basic -> basic.disable())
    30	                .sessionManagement(session -> session.sessionCreationPolicy(SessionCreationPolicy.STATELESS))
    31	                .exceptionHandling(ex -> ex
    32	                        .authenticationEntryPoint((req, res, e) ->
    33	                                res.sendError(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN, "Forbidden"))
    34	                )
    35	                .authorizeHttpRequests(auth -> auth.anyRequest().permitAll())
    36	                .addFilterBefore(headerRoleAuthFilter, UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter.class);
    37	        return http.build();
    38	    }
    39	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/WebConfig.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/config/WebConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.config;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.security.InternalSecretInterceptor;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     6	import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.InterceptorRegistry;
     7	import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.WebMvcConfigurer;
     8	
     9	@Configuration
    10	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    11	public class WebConfig implements WebMvcConfigurer {
    12	
    13	    private final InternalSecretInterceptor internalSecretInterceptor;
    14	
    15	    @Override
    16	    public void addInterceptors(InterceptorRegistry registry) {
    17	
    18	        registry.addInterceptor(internalSecretInterceptor)
    19	                .addPathPatterns("/api/orders/**");
    20	    }
    21	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/controller/OrderController.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/controller/OrderController.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.controller;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.request.CreateOrderRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.response.OrderResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.order_service.service.OrderService;
     7	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     8	import jakarta.validation.Valid;
     9	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    10	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    11	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    12	import org.springframework.security.access.prepost.PreAuthorize;
    13	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
    14	
    15	@RestController
    16	@RequestMapping("/api/order")
    17	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    18	@Slf4j
    19	public class OrderController {
    20	
    21	    private final OrderService orderService;
    22	
    23	    // =========================
    24	    // CREATE ORDER (BUYER)
    25	    // =========================
    26	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('BUYER')")
    27	    @PostMapping
    28	    public ResponseEntity<OrderResponse> createOrder(
    29	            @Valid @RequestBody CreateOrderRequest request,
    30	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    31	
    32	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    33	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    34	
    35	        OrderResponse response =
    36	                orderService.createOrder(request, role, buyerUuid);
    37	
    38	        return ResponseEntity.ok(response);
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    // =========================
    42	    // LIST ORDERS
    43	    // =========================
    44	    @GetMapping
    45	    public ResponseEntity<PageResponse<OrderResponse>> listOrders(
    46	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
    47	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size,
    48	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    49	
    50	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    51	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    52	
    53	        PageResponse<OrderResponse> response =
    54	                orderService.listOrders(page, size, role, buyerUuid);
    55	
    56	        return ResponseEntity.ok(response);
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('SELLER')")
    60	    @GetMapping("/seller")
    61	    public ResponseEntity<PageResponse<OrderResponse>> sellerOrders(
    62	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
    63	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size,
    64	            HttpServletRequest request) {
    65	
    66	        String sellerUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    67	
    68	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
    69	                orderService.listSellerOrders(page, size, sellerUuid)
    70	        );
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    @PreAuthorize("hasAnyRole('BUYER', 'ADMIN')")
    74	    @PutMapping("/{uuid}/status")
    75	    public ResponseEntity<OrderResponse> updateStatus(
    76	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    77	            @RequestParam String status,
    78	            HttpServletRequest request) {
    79	
    80	        String role = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    81	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    82	
    83	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
    84	                orderService.updateOrderStatus(uuid, role, userUuid, status)
    85	        );
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    @PutMapping("/internal/payment-update/{uuid}")
    89	    public ResponseEntity<Void> updatePaymentStatus(
    90	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    91	            @RequestParam String status) {
    92	
    93	        orderService.updatePaymentStatus(uuid, status);
    94	        return ResponseEntity.ok().build();
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    // =========================
    98	    // GET SINGLE ORDER
    99	    // =========================
   100	    @GetMapping("/{uuid}")
   101	    public ResponseEntity<OrderResponse> getOrder(
   102	            @PathVariable String uuid,
   103	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
   104	        String role     = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
   105	        String userUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
   106	        return ResponseEntity.ok(orderService.getOrderByUuid(uuid, role, userUuid));
   107	    }
   108	
   109	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/entity/BaseAuditEntity.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/entity/BaseAuditEntity.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.Column;
     4	import jakarta.persistence.EntityListeners;
     5	import jakarta.persistence.MappedSuperclass;
     6	import lombok.Getter;
     7	import lombok.Setter;
     8	import org.springframework.data.annotation.CreatedDate;
     9	import org.springframework.data.annotation.LastModifiedDate;
    10	import org.springframework.data.jpa.domain.support.AuditingEntityListener;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Shared audit fields for all entities.
    16	 * Spring Data JPA populates {@code createdAt} and {@code updatedAt}
    17	 * automatically when {@code @EnableJpaAuditing} is present on the main class.
    18	 */
    19	@MappedSuperclass
    20	@EntityListeners(AuditingEntityListener.class)
    21	@Getter
    22	@Setter
    23	public abstract class BaseAuditEntity {
    24	
    25	    @CreatedDate
    26	    @Column(updatable = false)
    27	    private LocalDateTime createdAt;
    28	
    29	    @LastModifiedDate
    30	    private LocalDateTime updatedAt;
    31	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/entity/Order.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/entity/Order.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.*;
     5	
     6	import java.util.List;
     7	
     8	@Entity
     9	@Getter
    10	@Setter
    11	@Builder
    12	@NoArgsConstructor
    13	@AllArgsConstructor
    14	@Table(name = "orders")
    15	public class Order extends BaseAuditEntity {
    16	
    17	    @Id
    18	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    19	    private Long id;
    20	
    21	    @Column(unique = true, nullable = false)
    22	    private String uuid;
    23	
    24	    @Column(nullable = false)
    25	    private String buyerUuid;
    26	
    27	    @Column(nullable = false)
    28	    private Double totalAmount;
    29	
    30	    @Enumerated(EnumType.STRING)
    31	    private OrderStatus status;
    32	
    33	    @Enumerated(EnumType.STRING)
    34	    private PaymentStatus paymentStatus;
    35	
    36	    @Builder.Default
    37	    private Boolean isDeleted = false;
    38	
    39	    @OneToMany(mappedBy = "order",
    40	            cascade = CascadeType.ALL,
    41	            orphanRemoval = true)
    42	    private List<OrderItem> items;
    43	}
    44	
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/entity/ProcessedEvent.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/entity/ProcessedEvent.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
     5	import lombok.Builder;
     6	import lombok.Data;
     7	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
     8	
     9	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Tracks processed Kafka event IDs to provide idempotent event consumption.
    13	 * Before processing any event, check if its eventId is already recorded here.
    14	 */
    15	@Entity
    16	@Table(name = "processed_events", indexes = {
    17	        @Index(name = "idx_processed_events_event_id", columnList = "event_id", unique = true)
    18	})
    19	@Data
    20	@Builder
    21	@NoArgsConstructor
    22	@AllArgsConstructor
    23	public class ProcessedEvent {
    24	
    25	    @Id
    26	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    27	    private Long id;
    28	
    29	    @Column(name = "event_id", nullable = false, unique = true, length = 64)
    30	    private String eventId;
    31	
    32	    @Column(name = "topic", nullable = false, length = 128)
    33	    private String topic;
    34	
    35	    @Column(name = "processed_at", nullable = false)
    36	    private LocalDateTime processedAt;
    37	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.exception;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.common.ErrorResponse;
     4	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     5	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
     7	import org.springframework.validation.FieldError;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
     9	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ExceptionHandler;
    10	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestControllerAdvice;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	import java.util.List;
    14	
    15	@Slf4j
    16	@RestControllerAdvice
    17	public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
    18	
    19	    @ExceptionHandler(OrderNotFoundException.class)
    20	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleNotFound(OrderNotFoundException ex) {
    21	        return buildError("ORDER_NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    @ExceptionHandler(OrderAccessException.class)
    25	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleAccess(OrderAccessException ex) {
    26	        return buildError("ORDER_ACCESS_DENIED", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.FORBIDDEN);
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    @ExceptionHandler(OrderStateException.class)
    30	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleState(OrderStateException ex) {
    31	        return buildError("ORDER_INVALID_STATE", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    35	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    36	        List<String> errors = ex.getBindingResult()
    37	                .getAllErrors()
    38	                .stream()
    39	                .map(e -> ((FieldError) e).getField() + " : " + e.getDefaultMessage())
    40	                .toList();
    41	
    42	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    43	                .errorCode("VALIDATION_ERROR")
    44	                .message("Validation failed")
    45	                .details(errors)
    46	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    47	                .build();
    48	
    49	        return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(response);
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    53	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneral(Exception ex) {
    54	        log.error("Unhandled exception", ex);
    55	        return buildError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", "Something went wrong", HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR);
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    private ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> buildError(String code, String message, HttpStatus status) {
    59	        return new ResponseEntity<>(
    60	                ErrorResponse.builder()
    61	                        .errorCode(code)
    62	                        .message(message)
    63	                        .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    64	                        .build(),
    65	                status);
    66	    }
    67	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/feign/ProductServiceClient.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/feign/ProductServiceClient.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.feign;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.ProductDto;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.feign.fallback.ProductServiceClientFallback;
     5	import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.FeignClient;
     6	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
     7	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PutMapping;
     9	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestParam;
    10	
    11	@FeignClient(
    12	        name = "product-service",
    13	        url = "${service.product.url}",
    14	        fallback = ProductServiceClientFallback.class
    15	)
    16	public interface ProductServiceClient {
    17	
    18	    @GetMapping("/api/product/{uuid}")
    19	    ProductDto getProduct(@PathVariable("uuid") String uuid);
    20	
    21	    @PutMapping("/api/product/internal/reduce-stock/{uuid}")
    22	    void reduceStock(@PathVariable("uuid") String uuid, @RequestParam("quantity") int quantity);
    23	
    24	    /**
    25	     * Saga compensation: restore stock when payment fails.
    26	     */
    27	    @PutMapping("/api/product/internal/restore-stock/{uuid}")
    28	    void restoreStock(@PathVariable("uuid") String uuid, @RequestParam("quantity") int quantity);
    29	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/feign/fallback/ProductServiceClientFallback.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.feign.fallback;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.ProductDto;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderStateException;
     5	import com.sourabh.order_service.feign.ProductServiceClient;
     6	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     7	
     8	@Component
     9	public class ProductServiceClientFallback implements ProductServiceClient {
    10	
    11	    @Override
    12	    public ProductDto getProduct(String uuid) {
    13	        throw new OrderStateException("Product service is currently unavailable. Please try again later.");
    14	    }
    15	
    16	    @Override
    17	    public void reduceStock(String uuid, int quantity) {
    18	        throw new OrderStateException("Product service is currently unavailable. Stock could not be reduced.");
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    @Override
    22	    public void restoreStock(String uuid, int quantity) {
    23	        // Best-effort: log and continue. A real implementation would use an outbox/retry mechanism.
    24	        throw new OrderStateException("Product service is currently unavailable. Stock could not be restored.");
    25	    }
    26	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.filter;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     8	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     9	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.UUID;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Picks up the {@code X-Correlation-Id} header set by the API Gateway and
    18	 * stores it in SLF4J MDC so it appears in every log statement for the request.
    19	 *
    20	 * <p>Also attaches the header to the HTTP response so callers can trace
    21	 * requests end-to-end.
    22	 */
    23	@Component
    24	@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    25	public class CorrelationIdFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    26	
    27	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    28	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    29	
    30	    @Override
    31	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    32	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    33	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    34	        String correlationId = request.getHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    35	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    36	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        MDC.put(MDC_KEY, correlationId);
    40	        response.addHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, correlationId);
    41	
    42	        try {
    43	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    44	        } finally {
    45	            MDC.remove(MDC_KEY);
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/kafka/consumer/PaymentEventConsumer.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/kafka/consumer/PaymentEventConsumer.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.kafka.consumer;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.ProcessedEvent;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.feign.ProductServiceClient;
     5	import com.sourabh.order_service.kafka.event.PaymentCompletedEvent;
     6	import com.sourabh.order_service.repository.OrderRepository;
     7	import com.sourabh.order_service.repository.ProcessedEventRepository;
     8	import com.sourabh.order_service.service.OrderService;
     9	import feign.FeignException;
    10	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    11	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    12	import org.springframework.kafka.annotation.KafkaListener;
    13	import org.springframework.kafka.annotation.RetryableTopic;
    14	import org.springframework.kafka.retrytopic.TopicSuffixingStrategy;
    15	import org.springframework.retry.annotation.Backoff;
    16	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    17	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    18	
    19	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    20	
    21	@Component
    22	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    23	@Slf4j
    24	public class PaymentEventConsumer {
    25	
    26	    private final OrderService orderService;
    27	    private final OrderRepository orderRepository;
    28	    private final ProductServiceClient productServiceClient;
    29	    private final ProcessedEventRepository processedEventRepository;
    30	
    31	    private static final String TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED = "payment.completed";
    32	
    33	    @RetryableTopic(
    34	            attempts = "3",
    35	            backoff = @Backoff(delay = 1000, multiplier = 2.0),
    36	            topicSuffixingStrategy = TopicSuffixingStrategy.SUFFIX_WITH_INDEX_VALUE,
    37	            dltTopicSuffix = ".DLT",
    38	            autoCreateTopics = "true"
    39	    )
    40	    @KafkaListener(topics = TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED, groupId = "order-service")
    41	    @Transactional
    42	    public void handlePaymentCompleted(PaymentCompletedEvent event) {
    43	        log.info("Received PaymentCompletedEvent: orderUuid={}, status={}, paymentUuid={}",
    44	                event.getOrderUuid(), event.getStatus(), event.getPaymentUuid());
    45	
    46	        // Idempotency guard — use paymentUuid as deduplication key
    47	        String idempotencyKey = "payment-completed:" + event.getPaymentUuid();
    48	        if (processedEventRepository.existsByEventId(idempotencyKey)) {
    49	            log.warn("Duplicate PaymentCompletedEvent, skipping: paymentUuid={}", event.getPaymentUuid());
    50	            return;
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        // Update order payment status (also cancels order if FAILED)
    54	        orderService.updatePaymentStatus(event.getOrderUuid(), event.getStatus());
    55	
    56	        // Saga compensation: restore stock if payment failed
    57	        if ("FAILED".equalsIgnoreCase(event.getStatus())) {
    58	            compensateFailedPayment(event.getOrderUuid());
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        // Record as processed
    62	        processedEventRepository.save(ProcessedEvent.builder()
    63	                .eventId(idempotencyKey)
    64	                .topic(TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED)
    65	                .processedAt(LocalDateTime.now())
    66	                .build());
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    /**
    70	     * Compensation step: restores product stock after a failed payment.
    71	     * The order has already been cancelled by {@code updatePaymentStatus}.
    72	     */
    73	    private void compensateFailedPayment(String orderUuid) {
    74	        orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(orderUuid).ifPresent(order -> {
    75	            if (order.getItems() == null || order.getItems().isEmpty()) {
    76	                log.warn("No order items for compensation: orderUuid={}", orderUuid);
    77	                return;
    78	            }
    79	            order.getItems().forEach(item -> {
    80	                try {
    81	                    productServiceClient.restoreStock(item.getProductUuid(), item.getQuantity());
    82	                    log.info("Stock restored for compensation: productUuid={}, quantity={}",
    83	                            item.getProductUuid(), item.getQuantity());
    84	                } catch (FeignException e) {
    85	                    // Log and continue — compensation must not block saga acknowledgment.
    86	                    // In production, use outbox pattern for guaranteed delivery.
    87	                    log.error("Failed to restore stock for productUuid={}: {}",
    88	                            item.getProductUuid(), e.getMessage());
    89	                }
    90	            });
    91	        });
    92	    }
    93	}
    94	
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.security;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     5	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     6	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     7	import org.springframework.web.servlet.HandlerInterceptor;
     8	
     9	@Component
    10	public class InternalSecretInterceptor implements HandlerInterceptor {
    11	
    12	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    13	    private String expectedSecret;
    14	
    15	    @Override
    16	    public boolean preHandle(HttpServletRequest request,
    17	                             HttpServletResponse response,
    18	                             Object handler) throws Exception {
    19	
    20	        String providedSecret =
    21	                request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    22	
    23	        if (providedSecret == null ||
    24	                !providedSecret.equals(expectedSecret)) {
    25	
    26	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    27	            return false;
    28	        }
    29	
    30	        return true;
    31	    }
    32	}
```

## order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/service/impl/OrderServiceImpl.java

Path: `order-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/order_service/service/impl/OrderServiceImpl.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.service.impl;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.ProductDto;
     5	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.request.CreateOrderRequest;
     6	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.response.OrderItemResponse;
     7	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.response.OrderResponse;
     8	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.Order;
     9	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.OrderItem;
    10	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.OrderStatus;
    11	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.PaymentStatus;
    12	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderAccessException;
    13	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderNotFoundException;
    14	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderStateException;
    15	import com.sourabh.order_service.feign.ProductServiceClient;
    16	import com.sourabh.order_service.kafka.event.OrderCreatedEvent;
    17	import com.sourabh.order_service.repository.OrderRepository;
    18	import com.sourabh.order_service.service.OrderService;
    19	import feign.FeignException;
    20	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    21	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    22	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.CacheEvict;
    23	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.Cacheable;
    24	import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
    25	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
    26	import org.springframework.data.domain.Pageable;
    27	import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort;
    28	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    29	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    30	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    31	
    32	import java.util.List;
    33	import java.util.UUID;
    34	
    35	@Service
    36	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    37	@Slf4j
    38	public class OrderServiceImpl implements OrderService {
    39	
    40	    private final OrderRepository orderRepository;
    41	    private final ProductServiceClient productServiceClient;
    42	    private final KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    43	
    44	    private static final String TOPIC_ORDER_CREATED = "order.created";
    45	
    46	    @Override
    47	    @Transactional
    48	    public OrderResponse createOrder(CreateOrderRequest request, String role, String buyerUuid) {
    49	
    50	        if (!"BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
    51	            throw new OrderAccessException("Only buyers can place orders");
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        ProductDto product = fetchProduct(request.getProductUuid());
    55	
    56	        if (!"ACTIVE".equalsIgnoreCase(product.getStatus())) {
    57	            throw new OrderStateException("Product is not active");
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        try {
    61	            productServiceClient.reduceStock(request.getProductUuid(), request.getQuantity());
    62	        } catch (FeignException e) {
    63	            throw new OrderStateException("Failed to reduce product stock: " + e.getMessage());
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        double totalAmount = product.getPrice() * request.getQuantity();
    67	
    68	        Order order = Order.builder()
    69	                .uuid(UUID.randomUUID().toString())
    70	                .buyerUuid(buyerUuid)
    71	                .totalAmount(totalAmount)
    72	                .status(OrderStatus.CREATED)
    73	                .paymentStatus(PaymentStatus.PENDING)
    74	                .isDeleted(false)
    75	                .build();
    76	
    77	        OrderItem item = OrderItem.builder()
    78	                .productUuid(product.getUuid())
    79	                .sellerUuid(product.getSellerUuid())
    80	                .price(product.getPrice())
    81	                .quantity(request.getQuantity())
    82	                .order(order)
    83	                .build();
    84	
    85	        order.setItems(List.of(item));
    86	        orderRepository.save(order);
    87	
    88	        // Saga: publish order.created so payment-service can auto-process payment
    89	        kafkaTemplate.send(TOPIC_ORDER_CREATED,
    90	                new OrderCreatedEvent(order.getUuid(), buyerUuid, product.getUuid(),
    91	                        request.getQuantity(), totalAmount));
    92	
    93	        log.info("Order created and order.created event published: orderUuid={}, productUuid={}",
    94	                order.getUuid(), product.getUuid());
    95	        return mapToResponse(order);
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    @Override
    99	    public PageResponse<OrderResponse> listOrders(int page, int size, String role, String buyerUuid) {
   100	
   101	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, Sort.by("createdAt").descending());
   102	
   103	        Page<Order> orderPage = "BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)
   104	                ? orderRepository.findByBuyerUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(buyerUuid, pageable)
   105	                : orderRepository.findByIsDeletedFalse(pageable);
   106	
   107	        return toPageResponse(orderPage);
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    @Override
   111	    public PageResponse<OrderResponse> listSellerOrders(int page, int size, String sellerUuid) {
   112	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, Sort.by("createdAt").descending());
   113	        return toPageResponse(orderRepository.findOrdersBySeller(sellerUuid, pageable));
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    @Override
   117	    @Transactional
   118	    @CacheEvict(value = "orders", key = "#uuid")
   119	    public OrderResponse updateOrderStatus(String uuid, String role, String buyerUuid, String newStatus) {
   120	
   121	        Order order = orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   122	                .orElseThrow(() -> new OrderNotFoundException("Order not found: " + uuid));
   123	
   124	        OrderStatus requestedStatus = OrderStatus.valueOf(newStatus.toUpperCase());
   125	
   126	        if ("BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
   127	            return cancelByBuyer(order, buyerUuid, requestedStatus);
   128	        }
   129	        if ("ADMIN".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
   130	            return advanceByAdmin(order, requestedStatus);
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        throw new OrderAccessException("Unauthorized action");
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    @Override
   137	    @Cacheable(value = "orders", key = "#uuid")
   138	    public OrderResponse getOrderByUuid(String uuid, String role, String userUuid) {
   139	        log.debug("Cache miss for order uuid={} — fetching from DB", uuid);
   140	        Order order = orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   141	                .orElseThrow(() -> new OrderNotFoundException("Order not found: " + uuid));
   142	
   143	        // Buyers can only see their own orders
   144	        if ("BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role) && !order.getBuyerUuid().equals(userUuid)) {
   145	            throw new OrderAccessException("You can only view your own orders");
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        return mapToResponse(order);
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    @Override
   152	    @Transactional
   153	    @CacheEvict(value = "orders", key = "#uuid")
   154	    public void updatePaymentStatus(String uuid, String status) {
   155	        Order order = orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   156	                .orElseThrow(() -> new OrderNotFoundException("Order not found: " + uuid));
   157	
   158	        PaymentStatus paymentStatus = PaymentStatus.valueOf(status);
   159	        order.setPaymentStatus(paymentStatus);
   160	
   161	        if (paymentStatus == PaymentStatus.FAILED) {
   162	            order.setStatus(OrderStatus.CANCELLED);
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        orderRepository.save(order);
   166	        log.info("Payment status updated: orderUuid={}, paymentStatus={}", uuid, status);
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   170	    // Private helpers
   171	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172	
   173	    private OrderResponse cancelByBuyer(Order order, String buyerUuid, OrderStatus requestedStatus) {
   174	        if (!order.getBuyerUuid().equals(buyerUuid)) {
   175	            throw new OrderAccessException("You can only modify your own order");
   176	        }
   177	        if (requestedStatus != OrderStatus.CANCELLED) {
   178	            throw new OrderStateException("Buyer can only cancel an order");
   179	        }
   180	        if (order.getStatus() != OrderStatus.CREATED) {
   181	            throw new OrderStateException("Order cannot be cancelled at this stage");
   182	        }
   183	        order.setStatus(OrderStatus.CANCELLED);
   184	        orderRepository.save(order);
   185	
   186	        // Saga compensation: restore stock for all items
   187	        if (order.getItems() != null) {
   188	            order.getItems().forEach(item -> {
   189	                try {
   190	                    productServiceClient.restoreStock(item.getProductUuid(), item.getQuantity());
   191	                    log.info("Stock restored for cancelled order: productUuid={}, qty={}",
   192	                            item.getProductUuid(), item.getQuantity());
   193	                } catch (Exception e) {
   194	                    log.error("Failed to restore stock for productUuid={}: {}",
   195	                            item.getProductUuid(), e.getMessage());
   196	                }
   197	            });
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        log.info("Order cancelled by buyer: uuid={}", order.getUuid());
   201	        return mapToResponse(order);
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    private OrderResponse advanceByAdmin(Order order, OrderStatus requestedStatus) {
   205	        OrderStatus current = order.getStatus();
   206	        OrderStatus expected = switch (current) {
   207	            case CREATED   -> OrderStatus.CONFIRMED;
   208	            case CONFIRMED -> OrderStatus.SHIPPED;
   209	            case SHIPPED   -> OrderStatus.DELIVERED;
   210	            default -> throw new OrderStateException("Order cannot transition further from: " + current);
   211	        };
   212	
   213	        if (requestedStatus != expected) {
   214	            throw new OrderStateException(
   215	                    "Invalid transition from " + current + " to " + requestedStatus + ". Expected: " + expected);
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        order.setStatus(requestedStatus);
   219	        orderRepository.save(order);
   220	        log.info("Order status updated by admin: uuid={}, newStatus={}", order.getUuid(), requestedStatus);
   221	        return mapToResponse(order);
   222	    }
   223	
   224	    private ProductDto fetchProduct(String productUuid) {
   225	        try {
   226	            return productServiceClient.getProduct(productUuid);
   227	        } catch (FeignException.NotFound e) {
   228	            throw new OrderStateException("Product not found: " + productUuid);
   229	        }
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    private PageResponse<OrderResponse> toPageResponse(Page<Order> orderPage) {
   233	        List<OrderResponse> responses = orderPage.getContent()
   234	                .stream()
   235	                .map(this::mapToResponse)
   236	                .toList();
   237	
   238	        return PageResponse.<OrderResponse>builder()
   239	                .content(responses)
   240	                .page(orderPage.getNumber())
   241	                .size(orderPage.getSize())
   242	                .totalElements(orderPage.getTotalElements())
   243	                .totalPages(orderPage.getTotalPages())
   244	                .last(orderPage.isLast())
   245	                .build();
   246	    }
   247	
   248	    private OrderResponse mapToResponse(Order order) {
   249	        List<OrderItemResponse> itemResponses = order.getItems() == null
   250	                ? List.of()
   251	                : order.getItems().stream()
   252	                        .map(item -> OrderItemResponse.builder()
   253	                                .productUuid(item.getProductUuid())
   254	                                .sellerUuid(item.getSellerUuid())
   255	                                .price(item.getPrice())
   256	                                .quantity(item.getQuantity())
   257	                                .build())
   258	                        .toList();
   259	
   260	        return OrderResponse.builder()
   261	                .uuid(order.getUuid())
   262	                .buyerUuid(order.getBuyerUuid())
   263	                .totalAmount(order.getTotalAmount())
   264	                .status(order.getStatus().name())
   265	                .paymentStatus(order.getPaymentStatus().name())
   266	                .items(itemResponses)
   267	                .createdAt(order.getCreatedAt())
   268	                .updatedAt(order.getUpdatedAt())
   269	                .build();
   270	    }
   271	}
```

## order-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql

Path: `order-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql`

```sql
     1	-- order-service: initial schema
     2	
     3	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orders (
     4	    id             BIGSERIAL        PRIMARY KEY,
     5	    uuid           VARCHAR(36)      NOT NULL UNIQUE,
     6	    buyer_uuid     VARCHAR(36)      NOT NULL,
     7	    total_amount   DOUBLE PRECISION NOT NULL,
     8	    status         VARCHAR(20),
     9	    payment_status VARCHAR(20),
    10	    is_deleted     BOOLEAN          NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    11	    created_at     TIMESTAMP,
    12	    updated_at     TIMESTAMP
    13	);
    14	
    15	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_orders_uuid       ON orders(uuid);
    16	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_orders_buyer_uuid ON orders(buyer_uuid);
    17	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_orders_status     ON orders(status);
    18	
    19	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS order_item (
    20	    id           BIGSERIAL        PRIMARY KEY,
    21	    product_uuid VARCHAR(36),
    22	    seller_uuid  VARCHAR(36),
    23	    price        DOUBLE PRECISION,
    24	    quantity     INTEGER,
    25	    order_id     BIGINT           REFERENCES orders(id)
    26	);
    27	
    28	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_order_item_order_id     ON order_item(order_id);
    29	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_order_item_product_uuid ON order_item(product_uuid);
    30	
    31	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS processed_events (
    32	    id           BIGSERIAL    PRIMARY KEY,
    33	    event_id     VARCHAR(64)  NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    34	    topic        VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
    35	    processed_at TIMESTAMP    NOT NULL
    36	);
    37	
    38	CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_processed_events_event_id ON processed_events(event_id);
```

## order-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/order_service/repository/OrderRepositoryIntegrationTest.java

Path: `order-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/order_service/repository/OrderRepositoryIntegrationTest.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.repository;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.Order;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.OrderItem;
     5	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.OrderStatus;
     6	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.PaymentStatus;
     7	import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
     8	import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
     9	import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
    10	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
    11	import org.springframework.boot.test.autoconfigure.jdbc.AutoConfigureTestDatabase;
    12	import org.springframework.boot.test.autoconfigure.orm.jpa.DataJpaTest;
    13	import org.springframework.boot.testcontainers.service.connection.ServiceConnection;
    14	import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
    15	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
    16	import org.testcontainers.containers.PostgreSQLContainer;
    17	import org.testcontainers.junit.jupiter.Container;
    18	import org.testcontainers.junit.jupiter.Testcontainers;
    19	
    20	import java.util.List;
    21	import java.util.Optional;
    22	
    23	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
    24	
    25	@DataJpaTest
    26	@AutoConfigureTestDatabase(replace = AutoConfigureTestDatabase.Replace.NONE)
    27	@Testcontainers
    28	@DisplayName("OrderRepository Integration Tests (Testcontainers)")
    29	class OrderRepositoryIntegrationTest {
    30	
    31	    @Container
    32	    @ServiceConnection
    33	    static PostgreSQLContainer<?> postgres = new PostgreSQLContainer<>("postgres:15");
    34	
    35	    @Autowired
    36	    private OrderRepository orderRepository;
    37	
    38	    private Order order1;
    39	    private Order order2;
    40	
    41	    @BeforeEach
    42	    void setUp() {
    43	        orderRepository.deleteAll();
    44	
    45	        order1 = Order.builder()
    46	                .uuid("order-buyer1-a")
    47	                .buyerUuid("buyer-1")
    48	                .totalAmount(100.0)
    49	                .status(OrderStatus.CREATED)
    50	                .paymentStatus(PaymentStatus.PENDING)
    51	                .isDeleted(false)
    52	                .build();
    53	
    54	        OrderItem item = OrderItem.builder()
    55	                .productUuid("prod-uuid")
    56	                .sellerUuid("seller-1")
    57	                .price(100.0)
    58	                .quantity(1)
    59	                .order(order1)
    60	                .build();
    61	        order1.setItems(List.of(item));
    62	
    63	        order2 = Order.builder()
    64	                .uuid("order-buyer2-a")
    65	                .buyerUuid("buyer-2")
    66	                .totalAmount(200.0)
    67	                .status(OrderStatus.CONFIRMED)
    68	                .paymentStatus(PaymentStatus.PENDING)
    69	                .isDeleted(false)
    70	                .build();
    71	        order2.setItems(List.of());
    72	
    73	        Order deletedOrder = Order.builder()
    74	                .uuid("order-deleted")
    75	                .buyerUuid("buyer-1")
    76	                .totalAmount(50.0)
    77	                .status(OrderStatus.CANCELLED)
    78	                .paymentStatus(PaymentStatus.FAILED)
    79	                .isDeleted(true)
    80	                .build();
    81	        deletedOrder.setItems(List.of());
    82	
    83	        orderRepository.saveAll(List.of(order1, order2, deletedOrder));
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    @Test
    87	    @DisplayName("findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse: returns non-deleted order")
    88	    void findByUuid_notDeleted_found() {
    89	        Optional<Order> result = orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-buyer1-a");
    90	        assertThat(result).isPresent();
    91	        assertThat(result.get().getBuyerUuid()).isEqualTo("buyer-1");
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    @Test
    95	    @DisplayName("findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse: does not return soft-deleted order")
    96	    void findByUuid_deleted_notFound() {
    97	        Optional<Order> result = orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-deleted");
    98	        assertThat(result).isEmpty();
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    @Test
   102	    @DisplayName("findByIsDeletedFalse: returns only non-deleted orders")
   103	    void findByIsDeletedFalse_onlyActive() {
   104	        Page<Order> page = orderRepository.findByIsDeletedFalse(PageRequest.of(0, 10));
   105	        assertThat(page.getTotalElements()).isEqualTo(2);
   106	        assertThat(page.getContent()).noneMatch(Order::getIsDeleted);
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    @Test
   110	    @DisplayName("findByBuyerUuidAndIsDeletedFalse: returns orders for specific buyer only")
   111	    void findByBuyerUuid_returnsOnlyBuyersOrders() {
   112	        Page<Order> page = orderRepository.findByBuyerUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("buyer-1", PageRequest.of(0, 10));
   113	        assertThat(page.getTotalElements()).isEqualTo(1);
   114	        assertThat(page.getContent().get(0).getUuid()).isEqualTo("order-buyer1-a");
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    @Test
   118	    @DisplayName("findOrdersBySeller: returns orders containing seller's items")
   119	    void findOrdersBySeller_returnsMatchingOrders() {
   120	        Page<Order> page = orderRepository.findOrdersBySeller("seller-1", PageRequest.of(0, 10));
   121	        assertThat(page.getTotalElements()).isEqualTo(1);
   122	        assertThat(page.getContent().get(0).getUuid()).isEqualTo("order-buyer1-a");
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    @Test
   126	    @DisplayName("findOrdersBySeller: returns empty for unknown seller")
   127	    void findOrdersBySeller_unknownSeller_empty() {
   128	        Page<Order> page = orderRepository.findOrdersBySeller("unknown-seller", PageRequest.of(0, 10));
   129	        assertThat(page.getTotalElements()).isZero();
   130	    }
   131	}
```

## order-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/order_service/service/OrderServiceImplTest.java

Path: `order-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/order_service/service/OrderServiceImplTest.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.order_service.service;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.ProductDto;
     4	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.request.CreateOrderRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.order_service.dto.response.OrderResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.Order;
     7	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.OrderStatus;
     8	import com.sourabh.order_service.entity.PaymentStatus;
     9	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderAccessException;
    10	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderNotFoundException;
    11	import com.sourabh.order_service.exception.OrderStateException;
    12	import com.sourabh.order_service.feign.ProductServiceClient;
    13	import com.sourabh.order_service.repository.OrderRepository;
    14	import com.sourabh.order_service.service.impl.OrderServiceImpl;
    15	import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
    16	import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
    17	import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
    18	import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtendWith;
    19	import org.mockito.InjectMocks;
    20	import org.mockito.Mock;
    21	import org.mockito.junit.jupiter.MockitoExtension;
    22	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    23	
    24	import java.util.List;
    25	import java.util.Optional;
    26	
    27	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
    28	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThatThrownBy;
    29	import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.any;
    30	import static org.mockito.Mockito.*;
    31	
    32	@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
    33	@DisplayName("OrderServiceImpl Unit Tests")
    34	class OrderServiceImplTest {
    35	
    36	    @Mock private OrderRepository orderRepository;
    37	    @Mock private ProductServiceClient productServiceClient;
    38	    @Mock private KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    39	
    40	    @InjectMocks
    41	    private OrderServiceImpl orderService;
    42	
    43	    private ProductDto activeProduct;
    44	    private Order sampleOrder;
    45	
    46	    @BeforeEach
    47	    void setUp() {
    48	        activeProduct = new ProductDto();
    49	        activeProduct.setUuid("prod-uuid");
    50	        activeProduct.setStatus("ACTIVE");
    51	        activeProduct.setPrice(100.0);
    52	        activeProduct.setSellerUuid("seller-uuid");
    53	
    54	        sampleOrder = Order.builder()
    55	                .uuid("order-uuid")
    56	                .buyerUuid("buyer-uuid")
    57	                .totalAmount(100.0)
    58	                .status(OrderStatus.CREATED)
    59	                .paymentStatus(PaymentStatus.PENDING)
    60	                .isDeleted(false)
    61	                .items(List.of())
    62	                .build();
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    66	    // createOrder
    67	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    68	
    69	    @Test
    70	    @DisplayName("createOrder: success — buyer creates valid order")
    71	    void createOrder_success() {
    72	        CreateOrderRequest req = new CreateOrderRequest();
    73	        req.setProductUuid("prod-uuid");
    74	        req.setQuantity(2);
    75	
    76	        when(productServiceClient.getProduct("prod-uuid")).thenReturn(activeProduct);
    77	        when(orderRepository.save(any())).thenReturn(sampleOrder);
    78	
    79	        OrderResponse response = orderService.createOrder(req, "BUYER", "buyer-uuid");
    80	
    81	        assertThat(response).isNotNull();
    82	        verify(productServiceClient).reduceStock("prod-uuid", 2);
    83	        verify(orderRepository).save(any(Order.class));
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    @Test
    87	    @DisplayName("createOrder: fails — non-buyer role rejected")
    88	    void createOrder_nonBuyer_throwsOrderAccessException() {
    89	        CreateOrderRequest req = new CreateOrderRequest();
    90	        req.setProductUuid("prod-uuid");
    91	        req.setQuantity(1);
    92	
    93	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> orderService.createOrder(req, "SELLER", "seller-uuid"))
    94	                .isInstanceOf(OrderAccessException.class)
    95	                .hasMessageContaining("Only buyers");
    96	
    97	        verifyNoInteractions(productServiceClient, orderRepository);
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    @Test
   101	    @DisplayName("createOrder: fails — product is not ACTIVE")
   102	    void createOrder_inactiveProduct_throwsOrderStateException() {
   103	        activeProduct.setStatus("INACTIVE");
   104	        CreateOrderRequest req = new CreateOrderRequest();
   105	        req.setProductUuid("prod-uuid");
   106	        req.setQuantity(1);
   107	
   108	        when(productServiceClient.getProduct("prod-uuid")).thenReturn(activeProduct);
   109	
   110	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> orderService.createOrder(req, "BUYER", "buyer-uuid"))
   111	                .isInstanceOf(OrderStateException.class)
   112	                .hasMessageContaining("not active");
   113	
   114	        verify(orderRepository, never()).save(any());
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   118	    // getOrderByUuid
   119	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   120	
   121	    @Test
   122	    @DisplayName("getOrderByUuid: returns order when found")
   123	    void getOrderByUuid_found() {
   124	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   125	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   126	
   127	        OrderResponse response = orderService.getOrderByUuid("order-uuid", "ADMIN", "admin-uuid");
   128	
   129	        assertThat(response.getUuid()).isEqualTo("order-uuid");
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    @Test
   133	    @DisplayName("getOrderByUuid: throws when not found")
   134	    void getOrderByUuid_notFound_throwsOrderNotFoundException() {
   135	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("bad-uuid"))
   136	                .thenReturn(Optional.empty());
   137	
   138	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> orderService.getOrderByUuid("bad-uuid", "ADMIN", "admin-uuid"))
   139	                .isInstanceOf(OrderNotFoundException.class);
   140	    }
   141	
   142	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   143	    // updateOrderStatus — buyer cancels
   144	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   145	
   146	    @Test
   147	    @DisplayName("updateOrderStatus: buyer can cancel a CREATED order")
   148	    void updateStatus_buyerCancels_success() {
   149	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   150	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   151	        when(orderRepository.save(any())).thenReturn(sampleOrder);
   152	
   153	        OrderResponse response = orderService.updateOrderStatus("order-uuid", "BUYER", "buyer-uuid", "CANCELLED");
   154	
   155	        assertThat(response.getStatus()).isEqualTo("CANCELLED");
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    @Test
   159	    @DisplayName("updateOrderStatus: buyer cannot cancel another buyer's order")
   160	    void updateStatus_buyerWrongOwner_throwsOrderAccessException() {
   161	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   162	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   163	
   164	        assertThatThrownBy(() ->
   165	                orderService.updateOrderStatus("order-uuid", "BUYER", "other-buyer", "CANCELLED"))
   166	                .isInstanceOf(OrderAccessException.class)
   167	                .hasMessageContaining("your own order");
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    @Test
   171	    @DisplayName("updateOrderStatus: buyer can only use CANCELLED — not SHIPPED")
   172	    void updateStatus_buyerSetShipped_throwsOrderStateException() {
   173	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   174	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   175	
   176	        assertThatThrownBy(() ->
   177	                orderService.updateOrderStatus("order-uuid", "BUYER", "buyer-uuid", "SHIPPED"))
   178	                .isInstanceOf(OrderStateException.class)
   179	                .hasMessageContaining("only cancel");
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   183	    // updateOrderStatus — admin advances
   184	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   185	
   186	    @Test
   187	    @DisplayName("updateOrderStatus: admin advances CREATED → CONFIRMED")
   188	    void updateStatus_adminConfirms_success() {
   189	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   190	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   191	        when(orderRepository.save(any())).thenReturn(sampleOrder);
   192	
   193	        OrderResponse response = orderService.updateOrderStatus("order-uuid", "ADMIN", null, "CONFIRMED");
   194	
   195	        assertThat(response.getStatus()).isEqualTo("CONFIRMED");
   196	    }
   197	
   198	    @Test
   199	    @DisplayName("updateOrderStatus: admin invalid transition CREATED → SHIPPED throws")
   200	    void updateStatus_adminInvalidTransition_throwsOrderStateException() {
   201	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   202	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   203	
   204	        assertThatThrownBy(() ->
   205	                orderService.updateOrderStatus("order-uuid", "ADMIN", null, "SHIPPED"))
   206	                .isInstanceOf(OrderStateException.class)
   207	                .hasMessageContaining("Invalid transition");
   208	    }
   209	
   210	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   211	    // updatePaymentStatus
   212	    // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   213	
   214	    @Test
   215	    @DisplayName("updatePaymentStatus: FAILED payment cancels order")
   216	    void updatePaymentStatus_failed_cancelsOrder() {
   217	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   218	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   219	        when(orderRepository.save(any())).thenReturn(sampleOrder);
   220	
   221	        orderService.updatePaymentStatus("order-uuid", "FAILED");
   222	
   223	        assertThat(sampleOrder.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.CANCELLED);
   224	        assertThat(sampleOrder.getPaymentStatus()).isEqualTo(PaymentStatus.FAILED);
   225	    }
   226	
   227	    @Test
   228	    @DisplayName("updatePaymentStatus: SUCCESS does not cancel order")
   229	    void updatePaymentStatus_success_doesNotCancelOrder() {
   230	        when(orderRepository.findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse("order-uuid"))
   231	                .thenReturn(Optional.of(sampleOrder));
   232	        when(orderRepository.save(any())).thenReturn(sampleOrder);
   233	
   234	        orderService.updatePaymentStatus("order-uuid", "SUCCESS");
   235	
   236	        assertThat(sampleOrder.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.CREATED);
   237	        assertThat(sampleOrder.getPaymentStatus()).isEqualTo(PaymentStatus.SUCCESS);
   238	    }
   239	}
```

## payment-service/dockerfile

Path: `payment-service/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl payment-service dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY payment-service/src payment-service/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl payment-service package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/payment-service/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8080
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
     9	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.Collections;
    15	import java.util.List;
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Reads the {@code X-User-Role} header forwarded by the API Gateway and
    19	 * populates the Spring Security context so that {@code @PreAuthorize}
    20	 * method-level annotations can be evaluated.
    21	 */
    22	@Component
    23	public class HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    24	
    25	    @Override
    26	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    27	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    28	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    29	        String role = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    30	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    31	
    32	        if (role != null && !role.isBlank()) {
    33	            List<SimpleGrantedAuthority> authorities =
    34	                    Collections.singletonList(new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role.toUpperCase()));
    35	            UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken authentication =
    36	                    new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(userUuid, null, authorities);
    37	            SecurityContextHolder.getContext().setAuthentication(authentication);
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    41	    }
    42	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	
     8	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    11	
    12	import java.io.IOException;
    13	
    14	@Component
    15	public class InternalSecretFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    16	
    17	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    18	    private String internalSecret;
    19	
    20	    @Override
    21	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    22	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    23	                                    FilterChain filterChain)
    24	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    25	
    26	        String header = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (!internalSecret.equals(header)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    34	    }
    35	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/OpenApiConfig.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/OpenApiConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.config;
     2	
     3	import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.OpenAPI;
     4	import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.servers.Server;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	
     8	import java.util.List;
     9	
    10	@Configuration
    11	public class OpenApiConfig {
    12	
    13	    @Bean
    14	    public OpenAPI customOpenAPI() {
    15	        Server server = new Server();
    16	        server.setUrl("/");
    17	        return new OpenAPI().servers(List.of(server));
    18	    }
    19	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/config/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.method.configuration.EnableMethodSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
     9	import org.springframework.security.config.http.SessionCreationPolicy;
    10	import org.springframework.security.web.SecurityFilterChain;
    11	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter;
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * JWT validation happens at the API Gateway; this service trusts the
    15	 * forwarded {@code X-User-Role} header for method-level RBAC via {@code @PreAuthorize}.
    16	 */
    17	@Configuration
    18	@EnableMethodSecurity
    19	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    20	public class SecurityConfig {
    21	
    22	    private final HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter headerRoleAuthFilter;
    23	
    24	    @Bean
    25	    public SecurityFilterChain securityFilterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
    26	        http
    27	                .csrf(csrf -> csrf.disable())
    28	                .formLogin(form -> form.disable())
    29	                .httpBasic(basic -> basic.disable())
    30	                .sessionManagement(session -> session.sessionCreationPolicy(SessionCreationPolicy.STATELESS))
    31	                .exceptionHandling(ex -> ex
    32	                        .authenticationEntryPoint((req, res, e) ->
    33	                                res.sendError(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN, "Forbidden"))
    34	                )
    35	                .authorizeHttpRequests(auth -> auth.anyRequest().permitAll())
    36	                .addFilterBefore(headerRoleAuthFilter, UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter.class);
    37	        return http.build();
    38	    }
    39	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/controller/PaymentController.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/controller/PaymentController.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.controller;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.payment_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.payment_service.dto.PaymentRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.payment_service.dto.PaymentResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.payment_service.service.PaymentService;
     7	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     8	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     9	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    10	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    11	import org.springframework.security.access.prepost.PreAuthorize;
    12	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
    13	
    14	@RestController
    15	@RequestMapping("/api/payment")
    16	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    17	@Slf4j
    18	public class PaymentController {
    19	
    20	    private final PaymentService paymentService;
    21	
    22	    // =========================
    23	    // INITIATE PAYMENT (BUYER)
    24	    // =========================
    25	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('BUYER')")
    26	    @PostMapping
    27	    public ResponseEntity<String> pay(
    28	            @RequestBody PaymentRequest request,
    29	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    30	        String role      = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    31	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    32	        return ResponseEntity.ok(paymentService.initiatePayment(request, role, buyerUuid));
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    // =========================
    36	    // GET MY PAYMENTS (BUYER paginated)
    37	    // =========================
    38	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('BUYER')")
    39	    @GetMapping
    40	    public ResponseEntity<PageResponse<PaymentResponse>> getMyPayments(
    41	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
    42	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size,
    43	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    44	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    45	        return ResponseEntity.ok(paymentService.getPaymentsByBuyer(buyerUuid, page, size));
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    // =========================
    49	    // GET PAYMENT BY UUID (BUYER own / ADMIN any)
    50	    // =========================
    51	    @PreAuthorize("hasAnyRole('BUYER', 'ADMIN')")
    52	    @GetMapping("/{uuid}")
    53	    public ResponseEntity<PaymentResponse> getPaymentByUuid(
    54	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    55	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    56	        String role      = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    57	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    58	        return ResponseEntity.ok(paymentService.getPaymentByUuid(uuid, role, buyerUuid));
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    // =========================
    62	    // GET PAYMENT BY ORDER UUID (BUYER own / ADMIN any)
    63	    // =========================
    64	    @PreAuthorize("hasAnyRole('BUYER', 'ADMIN')")
    65	    @GetMapping("/order/{orderUuid}")
    66	    public ResponseEntity<PaymentResponse> getPaymentByOrderUuid(
    67	            @PathVariable String orderUuid,
    68	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    69	        String role      = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    70	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    71	        return ResponseEntity.ok(paymentService.getPaymentByOrderUuid(orderUuid, role, buyerUuid));
    72	    }
    73	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/entity/ProcessedEvent.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/entity/ProcessedEvent.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
     5	import lombok.Builder;
     6	import lombok.Data;
     7	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
     8	
     9	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Tracks processed Kafka event IDs to provide idempotent event consumption.
    13	 */
    14	@Entity
    15	@Table(name = "processed_events", indexes = {
    16	        @Index(name = "idx_pe_event_id", columnList = "event_id", unique = true)
    17	})
    18	@Data
    19	@Builder
    20	@NoArgsConstructor
    21	@AllArgsConstructor
    22	public class ProcessedEvent {
    23	
    24	    @Id
    25	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    26	    private Long id;
    27	
    28	    @Column(name = "event_id", nullable = false, unique = true, length = 64)
    29	    private String eventId;
    30	
    31	    @Column(name = "topic", nullable = false, length = 128)
    32	    private String topic;
    33	
    34	    @Column(name = "processed_at", nullable = false)
    35	    private LocalDateTime processedAt;
    36	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.exception;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.payment_service.common.ErrorResponse;
     4	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     5	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
     7	import org.springframework.validation.FieldError;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
     9	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ExceptionHandler;
    10	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestControllerAdvice;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	import java.util.List;
    14	
    15	@Slf4j
    16	@RestControllerAdvice
    17	public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
    18	
    19	    @ExceptionHandler(PaymentException.class)
    20	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handlePayment(PaymentException ex) {
    21	        return buildError("PAYMENT_ERROR", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    @ExceptionHandler(PaymentAccessException.class)
    25	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleAccess(PaymentAccessException ex) {
    26	        return buildError("PAYMENT_ACCESS_DENIED", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.FORBIDDEN);
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    @ExceptionHandler(PaymentNotFoundException.class)
    30	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleNotFound(PaymentNotFoundException ex) {
    31	        return buildError("PAYMENT_NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    35	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    36	        List<String> errors = ex.getBindingResult()
    37	                .getAllErrors()
    38	                .stream()
    39	                .map(e -> ((FieldError) e).getField() + " : " + e.getDefaultMessage())
    40	                .toList();
    41	
    42	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    43	                .errorCode("VALIDATION_ERROR")
    44	                .message("Validation failed")
    45	                .details(errors)
    46	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    47	                .build();
    48	
    49	        return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(response);
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    53	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneral(Exception ex) {
    54	        log.error("Unhandled exception", ex);
    55	        return buildError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", "Something went wrong", HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR);
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    private ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> buildError(String code, String message, HttpStatus status) {
    59	        return new ResponseEntity<>(
    60	                ErrorResponse.builder()
    61	                        .errorCode(code)
    62	                        .message(message)
    63	                        .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    64	                        .build(),
    65	                status);
    66	    }
    67	}
```
