## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.filter;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     8	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     9	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.UUID;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Picks up the {@code X-Correlation-Id} header set by the API Gateway and
    18	 * stores it in SLF4J MDC so it appears in every log statement for the request.
    19	 *
    20	 * <p>Also attaches the header to the HTTP response so callers can trace
    21	 * requests end-to-end.
    22	 */
    23	@Component
    24	@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    25	public class CorrelationIdFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    26	
    27	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    28	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    29	
    30	    @Override
    31	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    32	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    33	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    34	        String correlationId = request.getHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    35	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    36	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        MDC.put(MDC_KEY, correlationId);
    40	        response.addHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, correlationId);
    41	
    42	        try {
    43	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    44	        } finally {
    45	            MDC.remove(MDC_KEY);
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/kafka/consumer/OrderEventConsumer.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/kafka/consumer/OrderEventConsumer.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.kafka.consumer;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.Payment;
     4	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.PaymentStatus;
     5	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.ProcessedEvent;
     6	import com.sourabh.payment_service.kafka.event.OrderCreatedEvent;
     7	import com.sourabh.payment_service.kafka.event.PaymentCompletedEvent;
     8	import com.sourabh.payment_service.repository.PaymentRepository;
     9	import com.sourabh.payment_service.repository.ProcessedEventRepository;
    10	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    11	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    12	import org.springframework.kafka.annotation.RetryableTopic;
    13	import org.springframework.kafka.annotation.KafkaListener;
    14	import org.springframework.kafka.retrytopic.TopicSuffixingStrategy;
    15	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    16	import org.springframework.retry.annotation.Backoff;
    17	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    18	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    19	
    20	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    21	import java.util.UUID;
    22	
    23	/**
    24	 * Consumes order.created events and processes payment automatically as part of
    25	 * the Order-Payment Saga. Idempotent: skips already-processed events.
    26	 */
    27	@Component
    28	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    29	@Slf4j
    30	public class OrderEventConsumer {
    31	
    32	    private final PaymentRepository paymentRepository;
    33	    private final ProcessedEventRepository processedEventRepository;
    34	    private final KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    35	
    36	    private static final String TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED = "payment.completed";
    37	    private static final String TOPIC_ORDER_CREATED = "order.created";
    38	
    39	    @RetryableTopic(
    40	            attempts = "3",
    41	            backoff = @Backoff(delay = 1000, multiplier = 2.0),
    42	            topicSuffixingStrategy = TopicSuffixingStrategy.SUFFIX_WITH_INDEX_VALUE,
    43	            dltTopicSuffix = ".DLT",
    44	            autoCreateTopics = "true"
    45	    )
    46	    @KafkaListener(topics = TOPIC_ORDER_CREATED, groupId = "payment-service")
    47	    @Transactional
    48	    public void handleOrderCreated(OrderCreatedEvent event) {
    49	        log.info("Received OrderCreatedEvent: eventId={}, orderUuid={}", event.getEventId(), event.getOrderUuid());
    50	
    51	        // Idempotency guard — skip if this event was already processed
    52	        if (processedEventRepository.existsByEventId(event.getEventId())) {
    53	            log.warn("Duplicate event detected, skipping: eventId={}", event.getEventId());
    54	            return;
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        // Avoid double-payment for the same order (e.g. REST + event both trigger)
    58	        if (paymentRepository.existsByOrderUuid(event.getOrderUuid())) {
    59	            log.warn("Payment already exists for orderUuid={}, skipping event processing", event.getOrderUuid());
    60	            return;
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        String paymentUuid = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    64	        Payment payment = Payment.builder()
    65	                .uuid(paymentUuid)
    66	                .orderUuid(event.getOrderUuid())
    67	                .buyerUuid(event.getBuyerUuid())
    68	                .amount(event.getTotalAmount())
    69	                .status(PaymentStatus.INITIATED)
    70	                .createdAt(LocalDateTime.now())
    71	                .build();
    72	        paymentRepository.save(payment);
    73	
    74	        // Simulate payment gateway (80% success rate)
    75	        boolean success = Math.random() > 0.2;
    76	        PaymentStatus finalStatus = success ? PaymentStatus.SUCCESS : PaymentStatus.FAILED;
    77	        payment.setStatus(finalStatus);
    78	        paymentRepository.save(payment);
    79	
    80	        log.info("Auto-payment processed via Saga: orderUuid={}, status={}", event.getOrderUuid(), finalStatus);
    81	
    82	        // Mark event as processed
    83	        processedEventRepository.save(ProcessedEvent.builder()
    84	                .eventId(event.getEventId())
    85	                .topic(TOPIC_ORDER_CREATED)
    86	                .processedAt(LocalDateTime.now())
    87	                .build());
    88	
    89	        // Notify order-service of the payment outcome
    90	        kafkaTemplate.send(TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED,
    91	                new PaymentCompletedEvent(event.getOrderUuid(), finalStatus.name(), paymentUuid));
    92	        log.info("PaymentCompletedEvent published for Saga: orderUuid={}, status={}", event.getOrderUuid(), finalStatus);
    93	    }
    94	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/kafka/event/OrderCreatedEvent.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.kafka.event;

     3	import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
     4	import lombok.Data;
     5	import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
     6

    10	 */
```

## payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/service/impl/PaymentServiceImpl.java

Path: `payment-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/service/impl/PaymentServiceImpl.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.service.impl;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.payment_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.payment_service.dto.PaymentRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.payment_service.dto.PaymentResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.Payment;
     7	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.PaymentStatus;
     8	import com.sourabh.payment_service.exception.PaymentAccessException;
     9	import com.sourabh.payment_service.exception.PaymentNotFoundException;
    10	import com.sourabh.payment_service.kafka.event.PaymentCompletedEvent;
    11	import com.sourabh.payment_service.repository.PaymentRepository;
    12	import com.sourabh.payment_service.service.PaymentService;
    13	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    14	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    15	import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
    16	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
    17	import org.springframework.data.domain.Pageable;
    18	import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort;
    19	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    20	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    21	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    22	
    23	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    24	import java.util.List;
    25	import java.util.UUID;
    26	
    27	@Service
    28	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    29	@Transactional
    30	@Slf4j
    31	public class PaymentServiceImpl implements PaymentService {
    32	
    33	    private final PaymentRepository paymentRepository;
    34	    private final KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    35	
    36	    private static final String TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED = "payment.completed";
    37	
    38	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    39	    // INITIATE PAYMENT (Buyer manual flow)
    40	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    41	
    42	    @Override
    43	    public String initiatePayment(PaymentRequest request, String role, String buyerUuid) {
    44	
    45	        if (!"BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
    46	            throw new PaymentAccessException("Only buyers can initiate payments");
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        request.setBuyerUuid(buyerUuid);
    50	
    51	        String paymentUuid = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    52	
    53	        Payment payment = Payment.builder()
    54	                .uuid(paymentUuid)
    55	                .orderUuid(request.getOrderUuid())
    56	                .buyerUuid(buyerUuid)
    57	                .amount(request.getAmount())
    58	                .status(PaymentStatus.INITIATED)
    59	                .createdAt(LocalDateTime.now())
    60	                .build();
    61	
    62	        paymentRepository.save(payment);
    63	
    64	        // Simulate payment gateway (80% success)
    65	        boolean success = Math.random() > 0.2;
    66	        PaymentStatus finalStatus = success ? PaymentStatus.SUCCESS : PaymentStatus.FAILED;
    67	        payment.setStatus(finalStatus);
    68	        paymentRepository.save(payment);
    69	
    70	        log.info("Payment processed: orderUuid={}, status={}", request.getOrderUuid(), finalStatus);
    71	
    72	        kafkaTemplate.send(TOPIC_PAYMENT_COMPLETED,
    73	                new PaymentCompletedEvent(request.getOrderUuid(), finalStatus.name(), paymentUuid));
    74	
    75	        log.info("PaymentCompletedEvent published: orderUuid={}, status={}", request.getOrderUuid(), finalStatus);
    76	        return "Payment " + finalStatus.name();
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    80	    // GET PAYMENTS — buyer history (paginated)
    81	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    82	
    83	    @Override
    84	    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
    85	    public PageResponse<PaymentResponse> getPaymentsByBuyer(String buyerUuid, int page, int size) {
    86	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, Sort.by("createdAt").descending());
    87	        Page<Payment> paymentPage = paymentRepository.findByBuyerUuid(buyerUuid, pageable);
    88	
    89	        List<PaymentResponse> content = paymentPage.getContent()
    90	                .stream()
    91	                .map(this::mapToResponse)
    92	                .toList();
    93	
    94	        return PageResponse.<PaymentResponse>builder()
    95	                .content(content)
    96	                .page(paymentPage.getNumber())
    97	                .size(paymentPage.getSize())
    98	                .totalElements(paymentPage.getTotalElements())
    99	                .totalPages(paymentPage.getTotalPages())
   100	                .last(paymentPage.isLast())
   101	                .build();
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   105	    // GET PAYMENT BY UUID
   106	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   107	
   108	    @Override
   109	    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
   110	    public PaymentResponse getPaymentByUuid(String uuid, String role, String buyerUuid) {
   111	        Payment payment = paymentRepository.findByUuid(uuid)
   112	                .orElseThrow(() -> new PaymentNotFoundException("Payment not found: " + uuid));
   113	
   114	        enforceReadAccess(payment, role, buyerUuid);
   115	        return mapToResponse(payment);
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   119	    // GET PAYMENT BY ORDER UUID
   120	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   121	
   122	    @Override
   123	    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
   124	    public PaymentResponse getPaymentByOrderUuid(String orderUuid, String role, String buyerUuid) {
   125	        Payment payment = paymentRepository.findByOrderUuid(orderUuid)
   126	                .orElseThrow(() -> new PaymentNotFoundException("No payment found for order: " + orderUuid));
   127	
   128	        enforceReadAccess(payment, role, buyerUuid);
   129	        return mapToResponse(payment);
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   133	    // Helpers
   134	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   135	
   136	    /** Buyers may only access their own payments; admins can see all. */
   137	    private void enforceReadAccess(Payment payment, String role, String buyerUuid) {
   138	        if ("BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role) && !payment.getBuyerUuid().equals(buyerUuid)) {
   139	            throw new PaymentAccessException("You can only view your own payments");
   140	        }
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    private PaymentResponse mapToResponse(Payment payment) {
   144	        return PaymentResponse.builder()
   145	                .uuid(payment.getUuid())
   146	                .orderUuid(payment.getOrderUuid())
   147	                .buyerUuid(payment.getBuyerUuid())
   148	                .amount(payment.getAmount())
   149	                .status(payment.getStatus().name())
   150	                .createdAt(payment.getCreatedAt())
   151	                .build();
   152	    }
   153	}
```

## payment-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql

Path: `payment-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql`

```sql
     1	-- payment-service: initial schema
     2	
     3	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS payment (
     4	    id           BIGSERIAL        PRIMARY KEY,
     5	    uuid         VARCHAR(36)      NOT NULL UNIQUE,
     6	    order_uuid   VARCHAR(36)      NOT NULL,
     7	    buyer_uuid   VARCHAR(36)      NOT NULL,
     8	    amount       DOUBLE PRECISION,
     9	    status       VARCHAR(20),
    10	    created_at   TIMESTAMP
    11	);
    12	
    13	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_payment_uuid        ON payment(uuid);
    14	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_payment_order_uuid  ON payment(order_uuid);
    15	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_payment_buyer_uuid  ON payment(buyer_uuid);
    16	
    17	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS processed_events (
    18	    id           BIGSERIAL    PRIMARY KEY,
    19	    event_id     VARCHAR(64)  NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    20	    topic        VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,
    21	    processed_at TIMESTAMP    NOT NULL
    22	);
    23	
    24	CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_pe_event_id ON processed_events(event_id);
```

## payment-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/service/PaymentServiceImplTest.java

Path: `payment-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/payment_service/service/PaymentServiceImplTest.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.payment_service.service;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.payment_service.dto.PaymentRequest;
     4	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.Payment;
     5	import com.sourabh.payment_service.entity.PaymentStatus;
     6	import com.sourabh.payment_service.exception.PaymentAccessException;
     7	import com.sourabh.payment_service.kafka.event.PaymentCompletedEvent;
     8	import com.sourabh.payment_service.repository.PaymentRepository;
     9	import com.sourabh.payment_service.service.impl.PaymentServiceImpl;
    10	import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
    11	import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
    12	import org.junit.jupiter.api.RepeatedTest;
    13	import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
    14	import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtendWith;
    15	import org.mockito.ArgumentCaptor;
    16	import org.mockito.InjectMocks;
    17	import org.mockito.Mock;
    18	import org.mockito.junit.jupiter.MockitoExtension;
    19	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    20	
    21	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
    22	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThatThrownBy;
    23	import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.any;
    24	import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.eq;
    25	import static org.mockito.Mockito.*;
    26	
    27	@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
    28	@DisplayName("PaymentServiceImpl Unit Tests")
    29	class PaymentServiceImplTest {
    30	
    31	    @Mock private PaymentRepository paymentRepository;
    32	    @Mock private KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    33	
    34	    @InjectMocks
    35	    private PaymentServiceImpl paymentService;
    36	
    37	    private PaymentRequest validRequest;
    38	
    39	    @BeforeEach
    40	    void setUp() {
    41	        validRequest = new PaymentRequest();
    42	        validRequest.setOrderUuid("order-uuid");
    43	        validRequest.setAmount(250.00);
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    @Test
    47	    @DisplayName("initiatePayment: fails — role is not BUYER")
    48	    void initiatePayment_notBuyer_throwsPaymentAccessException() {
    49	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> paymentService.initiatePayment(validRequest, "ADMIN", "admin-uuid"))
    50	                .isInstanceOf(PaymentAccessException.class)
    51	                .hasMessageContaining("Only buyers");
    52	
    53	        verifyNoInteractions(paymentRepository, kafkaTemplate);
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    @Test
    57	    @DisplayName("initiatePayment: stamps buyerUuid from header, not request body")
    58	    void initiatePayment_stampsBuyerUuid() {
    59	        validRequest.setBuyerUuid("spoofed-uuid");   // attacker tries to inject different UUID
    60	        when(paymentRepository.save(any())).thenAnswer(i -> i.getArgument(0));
    61	
    62	        paymentService.initiatePayment(validRequest, "BUYER", "real-buyer-uuid");
    63	
    64	        // The overwritten buyerUuid should be the header value, not the body value
    65	        ArgumentCaptor<Payment> captor = ArgumentCaptor.forClass(Payment.class);
    66	        verify(paymentRepository, atLeastOnce()).save(captor.capture());
    67	        assertThat(captor.getAllValues().get(0).getBuyerUuid()).isEqualTo("real-buyer-uuid");
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    @Test
    71	    @DisplayName("initiatePayment: always publishes PaymentCompletedEvent to Kafka")
    72	    void initiatePayment_alwaysPublishesKafkaEvent() {
    73	        when(paymentRepository.save(any())).thenAnswer(i -> i.getArgument(0));
    74	
    75	        paymentService.initiatePayment(validRequest, "BUYER", "buyer-uuid");
    76	
    77	        verify(kafkaTemplate).send(eq("payment.completed"), any(PaymentCompletedEvent.class));
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    @Test
    81	    @DisplayName("initiatePayment: event contains correct orderUuid")
    82	    void initiatePayment_kafkaEventHasCorrectOrderUuid() {
    83	        when(paymentRepository.save(any())).thenAnswer(i -> i.getArgument(0));
    84	
    85	        paymentService.initiatePayment(validRequest, "BUYER", "buyer-uuid");
    86	
    87	        ArgumentCaptor<PaymentCompletedEvent> eventCaptor = ArgumentCaptor.forClass(PaymentCompletedEvent.class);
    88	        verify(kafkaTemplate).send(eq("payment.completed"), eventCaptor.capture());
    89	
    90	        assertThat(eventCaptor.getValue().getOrderUuid()).isEqualTo("order-uuid");
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    @Test
    94	    @DisplayName("initiatePayment: saves payment twice — once INITIATED, once final status")
    95	    void initiatePayment_savesTwice() {
    96	        when(paymentRepository.save(any())).thenAnswer(i -> i.getArgument(0));
    97	
    98	        paymentService.initiatePayment(validRequest, "BUYER", "buyer-uuid");
    99	
   100	        verify(paymentRepository, times(2)).save(any(Payment.class));
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    @RepeatedTest(10)
   104	    @DisplayName("initiatePayment: final status is always SUCCESS or FAILED (never null)")
   105	    void initiatePayment_finalStatusNeverNull() {
   106	        when(paymentRepository.save(any())).thenAnswer(i -> i.getArgument(0));
   107	
   108	        String result = paymentService.initiatePayment(validRequest, "BUYER", "buyer-uuid");
   109	
   110	        assertThat(result).isIn("Payment SUCCESS", "Payment FAILED");
   111	    }
   112	}
```

## product-service/dockerfile

Path: `product-service/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl product-service dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY product-service/src product-service/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl product-service package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/product-service/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8080
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
     9	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.Collections;
    15	import java.util.List;
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Reads the {@code X-User-Role} header forwarded by the API Gateway and
    19	 * populates the Spring Security context so that {@code @PreAuthorize}
    20	 * method-level annotations can be evaluated.
    21	 */
    22	@Component
    23	public class HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    24	
    25	    @Override
    26	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    27	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    28	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    29	        String role = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    30	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    31	
    32	        if (role != null && !role.isBlank()) {
    33	            // Spring Security expects roles prefixed with "ROLE_"
    34	            List<SimpleGrantedAuthority> authorities =
    35	                    Collections.singletonList(new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role.toUpperCase()));
    36	
    37	            UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken authentication =
    38	                    new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(userUuid, null, authorities);
    39	            SecurityContextHolder.getContext().setAuthentication(authentication);
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    43	    }
    44	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	
     8	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    11	
    12	import java.io.IOException;
    13	
    14	@Component
    15	public class InternalSecretFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    16	
    17	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    18	    private String internalSecret;
    19	
    20	    @Override
    21	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    22	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    23	                                    FilterChain filterChain)
    24	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    25	
    26	        String header = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (!internalSecret.equals(header)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    34	    }
    35	}
```

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.config;
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.config;
     2	
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
     5	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.jsontype.impl.LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator;
     6	import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
     7	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.EnableCaching;
     8	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     9	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
    10	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheConfiguration;
    11	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheManager;
    12	import org.springframework.data.redis.connection.RedisConnectionFactory;
    13	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer;
    14	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.RedisSerializationContext;
    15	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.StringRedisSerializer;
    16	
    17	import java.time.Duration;
    18	import java.util.HashMap;
    19	import java.util.Map;
    20	
    21	@Configuration
    22	@EnableCaching
    23	public class RedisCacheConfig {
    24	
    25	    /** Cache name — used in @Cacheable/@CacheEvict throughout product-service */
    26	    public static final String PRODUCTS_CACHE = "products";
    27	
    28	    @Bean
    29	    public RedisCacheManager cacheManager(RedisConnectionFactory factory) {
    30	
    31	        ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
    32	        om.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    33	        om.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
    34	        om.activateDefaultTyping(
    35	                LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator.instance,
    36	                ObjectMapper.DefaultTyping.NON_FINAL);
    37	        GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer jsonSerializer =
    38	                new GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer(om);
    39	
    40	        RedisCacheConfiguration defaultConfig = RedisCacheConfiguration
    41	                .defaultCacheConfig()
    42	                .serializeKeysWith(
    43	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    44	                                .fromSerializer(new StringRedisSerializer()))
    45	                .serializeValuesWith(
    46	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    47	                                .fromSerializer(jsonSerializer))
    48	                .disableCachingNullValues();
    49	
    50	        // Per-cache TTL overrides
    51	        Map<String, RedisCacheConfiguration> cacheConfigs = new HashMap<>();
    52	        cacheConfigs.put(PRODUCTS_CACHE, defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(10)));
    53	
    54	        return RedisCacheManager.builder(factory)
    55	                .cacheDefaults(defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(10)))
    56	                .withInitialCacheConfigurations(cacheConfigs)
    57	                .build();
    58	    }
    59	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.method.configuration.EnableMethodSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
     9	import org.springframework.security.config.http.SessionCreationPolicy;
    10	import org.springframework.security.web.SecurityFilterChain;
    11	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter;
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * Security configuration for product-service.
    15	 *
    16	 * JWT validation and authentication happen exclusively at the API Gateway.
    17	 * This service trusts the forwarded {@code X-User-Role} / {@code X-User-UUID}
    18	 * headers set by the gateway and uses them to populate the Spring Security
    19	 * context for {@code @PreAuthorize} evaluation.
    20	 */
    21	@Configuration
    22	@EnableMethodSecurity
    23	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    24	public class SecurityConfig {
    25	
    26	    private final HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter headerRoleAuthFilter;
    27	
    28	    @Bean
    29	    public SecurityFilterChain securityFilterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
    30	        http
    31	                .csrf(csrf -> csrf.disable())
    32	                .formLogin(form -> form.disable())
    33	                .httpBasic(basic -> basic.disable())
    34	                .sessionManagement(session -> session.sessionCreationPolicy(SessionCreationPolicy.STATELESS))
    35	                .exceptionHandling(ex -> ex
    36	                        .authenticationEntryPoint((req, res, e) ->
    37	                                res.sendError(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN, "Forbidden"))
    38	                )
    39	                .authorizeHttpRequests(auth -> auth.anyRequest().permitAll())
    40	                .addFilterBefore(headerRoleAuthFilter, UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter.class);
    41	        return http.build();
    42	    }
    43	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/WebConfig.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/config/WebConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.config;
     2	
     3	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     4	import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.WebMvcConfigurer;
     5	
     6	/**
     7	 * MVC interceptor registration for product-service.
     8	 *
     9	 * InternalSecretInterceptor is intentionally removed — its function is
    10	 * fully covered by the InternalSecretFilter servlet filter which applies
    11	 * to all request paths before reaching Spring MVC.
    12	 */
    13	@Configuration
    14	public class WebConfig implements WebMvcConfigurer {
    15	    // No interceptors needed — InternalSecretFilter handles gateway validation
    16	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/controller/ProductController.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/controller/ProductController.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.controller;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.product_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request.CreateProductRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request.UpdateProductRequest;
     6	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.response.ProductResponse;
     7	import com.sourabh.product_service.service.ProductService;
     8	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     9	import jakarta.validation.Valid;
    10	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    11	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    12	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    13	import org.springframework.security.access.prepost.PreAuthorize;
    14	import org.springframework.security.core.annotation.AuthenticationPrincipal;
    15	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
    16	
    17	@RestController
    18	@RequestMapping("/api/product")
    19	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    20	@Slf4j
    21	public class ProductController {
    22	
    23	    private final ProductService productService;
    24	
    25	    // =========================
    26	    // CREATE PRODUCT (SELLER)
    27	    // =========================
    28	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('SELLER')")
    29	    @PostMapping
    30	    public ResponseEntity<ProductResponse> createProduct(
    31	            @Valid @RequestBody CreateProductRequest request,
    32	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    33	
    34	        String sellerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    35	
    36	        ProductResponse response =
    37	                productService.createProduct(request, sellerUuid);
    38	
    39	        return ResponseEntity.ok(response);
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    // =========================
    43	    // UPDATE PRODUCT
    44	    // =========================
    45	    @PreAuthorize("hasAnyRole('SELLER', 'ADMIN')")
    46	    @PutMapping("/{uuid}")
    47	    public ResponseEntity<ProductResponse> updateProduct(
    48	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    49	            @Valid @RequestBody UpdateProductRequest request,
    50	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    51	
    52	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    53	        String sellerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    54	
    55	        ProductResponse response =
    56	                productService.updateProduct(uuid, request, role, sellerUuid);
    57	
    58	        return ResponseEntity.ok(response);
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    // =========================
    62	    // APPROVE PRODUCT (ADMIN)
    63	    // =========================
    64	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
    65	    @PutMapping("/admin/approve/{uuid}")
    66	    public ResponseEntity<String> approveProduct(@PathVariable String uuid) {
    67	        return ResponseEntity.ok(productService.approveProduct(uuid));
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    // =========================
    71	    // BLOCK PRODUCT (ADMIN)
    72	    // =========================
    73	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
    74	    @PutMapping("/admin/block/{uuid}")
    75	    public ResponseEntity<String> blockProduct(@PathVariable String uuid) {
    76	        return ResponseEntity.ok(productService.blockProduct(uuid));
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    // =========================
    80	    // UNBLOCK PRODUCT (ADMIN)
    81	    // =========================
    82	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
    83	    @PutMapping("/admin/unblock/{uuid}")
    84	    public ResponseEntity<String> unblockProduct(@PathVariable String uuid) {
    85	        return ResponseEntity.ok(productService.unblockProduct(uuid));
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    // =========================
    89	    // SOFT DELETE
    90	    // =========================
    91	    @PreAuthorize("hasAnyRole('SELLER', 'ADMIN')")
    92	    @DeleteMapping("/{uuid}")
    93	    public ResponseEntity<String> deleteProduct(
    94	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    95	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    96	
    97	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    98	        String sellerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    99	
   100	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
   101	                productService.softDeleteProduct(uuid, role, sellerUuid)
   102	        );
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    // =========================
   106	    // LIST PRODUCTS
   107	    // =========================
   108	    @GetMapping
   109	    public ResponseEntity<PageResponse<ProductResponse>> listProducts(
   110	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
   111	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size,
   112	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "createdAt") String sortBy,
   113	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "desc") String direction,
   114	            @RequestParam(required = false) String keyword,
   115	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
   116	
   117	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
   118	        String sellerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
   119	
   120	        PageResponse<ProductResponse> response =
   121	                productService.listProducts(
   122	                        page,
   123	                        size,
   124	                        sortBy,
   125	                        direction,
   126	                        role,
   127	                        sellerUuid,
   128	                        keyword
   129	                );
   130	
   131	        return ResponseEntity.ok(response);
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    // =========================
   135	    // GET SINGLE PRODUCT
   136	    // =========================
   137	    @GetMapping("/{uuid}")
   138	    public ResponseEntity<ProductResponse> getProduct(
   139	            @PathVariable String uuid,
   140	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
   141	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
   142	        return ResponseEntity.ok(productService.getProductByUuid(uuid, role));
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    @PutMapping("/internal/reduce-stock/{uuid}")
   146	    public ResponseEntity<String> reduceStock(
   147	            @PathVariable String uuid,
   148	            @RequestParam Integer quantity) {
   149	
   150	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
   151	                productService.reduceStock(uuid, quantity)
   152	        );
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    @PutMapping("/internal/restore-stock/{uuid}")
   156	    public ResponseEntity<String> restoreStock(
   157	            @PathVariable String uuid,
   158	            @RequestParam Integer quantity) {
   159	
   160	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
   161	                productService.restoreStock(uuid, quantity)
   162	        );
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    @PutMapping("/internal/update-rating/{uuid}")
   166	    public ResponseEntity<Void> updateRating(
   167	            @PathVariable String uuid,
   168	            @RequestParam Integer rating) {
   169	
   170	        productService.updateRating(uuid, rating);
   171	        return ResponseEntity.ok().build();
   172	    }
   173	
   174	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/dto/request/CreateProductRequest.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.validation.constraints.*;
     4	import lombok.Getter;
     5	import lombok.Setter;
     6	
     7	@Getter
     8	@Setter
     9	public class CreateProductRequest {
    10	
    11	    @NotBlank
    12	    @Size(max = 255)
    13	    private String name;
    14	
    15	    @Size(max = 2000)
    16	    private String description;
    17	
    18	    @NotNull
    19	    @Positive
    20	    private Double price;
    21	
    22	    @NotNull
    23	    @Min(0)
    24	    private Integer stock;
    25	
    26	    @NotBlank
    27	    private String category;
    28	
    29	    @Size(max = 1000)
    30	    private String imageUrl;
    31	}
```

```java
     8	
     9	@Getter

    11	public class UpdateProductRequest {

    17	    private String description;
    18	
    19	    @Positive
    20	    private Double price;
    21	
    22	    @Min(0)
    23	    private Integer stock;

    28	    private String imageUrl;
    29	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/dto/response/ProductResponse.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/dto/response/ProductResponse.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.dto.response;
     2	
     3	import lombok.Builder;
     4	import lombok.Getter;
     5	import lombok.extern.jackson.Jacksonized;
     6	
     7	@Getter
     8	@Builder
     9	@Jacksonized
    10	public class ProductResponse {
    11	
    12	    private String uuid;
    13	    private String name;
    14	    private String description;
    15	    private Double price;
    16	    private Integer stock;
    17	    private String category;
    18	    private String sellerUuid;
    19	    private String status;
    20	    private Double averageRating;
    21	    private Integer totalReviews;
    22	    private String imageUrl;
    23	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/entity/BaseAuditEntity.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/entity/BaseAuditEntity.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.Column;
     4	import jakarta.persistence.EntityListeners;
     5	import jakarta.persistence.MappedSuperclass;
     6	import lombok.Getter;
     7	import lombok.Setter;
     8	import org.springframework.data.annotation.CreatedDate;
     9	import org.springframework.data.annotation.LastModifiedDate;
    10	import org.springframework.data.jpa.domain.support.AuditingEntityListener;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Shared audit fields for all entities.
    16	 * Spring Data JPA populates {@code createdAt} and {@code updatedAt}
    17	 * automatically when {@code @EnableJpaAuditing} is present on the main class.
    18	 */
    19	@MappedSuperclass
    20	@EntityListeners(AuditingEntityListener.class)
    21	@Getter
    22	@Setter
    23	public abstract class BaseAuditEntity {
    24	
    25	    @CreatedDate
    26	    @Column(updatable = false)
    27	    private LocalDateTime createdAt;
    28	
    29	    @LastModifiedDate
    30	    private LocalDateTime updatedAt;
    31	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/entity/Product.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/entity/Product.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.*;
     5	
     6	@Entity
     7	@Getter
     8	@Setter
     9	@Builder
    10	@NoArgsConstructor
    11	@AllArgsConstructor
    12	public class Product extends BaseAuditEntity {
    13	
    14	    @Id
    15	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    16	    private Long id;
    17	
    18	    @Column(unique = true, nullable = false)
    19	    private String uuid;
    20	
    21	    @Column(nullable = false)
    22	    private String name;
    23	
    24	    @Column(length = 2000)
    25	    private String description;
    26	
    27	    @Column(nullable = false)
    28	    private Double price;
    29	
    30	    @Column(nullable = false)
    31	    private Integer stock;
    32	
    33	    @Column(nullable = false)
    34	    private String category;
    35	
    36	    @Column(nullable = false)
    37	    private String sellerUuid;
    38	
    39	    @Enumerated(EnumType.STRING)
    40	    private ProductStatus status;
    41	
    42	    @Builder.Default
    43	    private Boolean isDeleted = false;
    44	
    45	    @Column(nullable = false)
    46	    @Builder.Default
    47	    private Double averageRating = 0.0;
    48	
    49	    @Column(nullable = false)
    50	    @Builder.Default
    51	    private Integer totalReviews = 0;
    52	
    53	    @Column(length = 1000)
    54	    private String imageUrl;
    55	
    56	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.exception;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.product_service.common.ErrorResponse;
     4	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     5	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
     7	import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
     9	
    10	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    11	import java.util.List;
    12	
    13	@RestControllerAdvice
    14	@Slf4j
    15	public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
    16	
    17	    @ExceptionHandler(ProductNotFoundException.class)
    18	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleNotFound(ProductNotFoundException ex) {
    19	
    20	        return buildError(
    21	                "PRODUCT_NOT_FOUND",
    22	                ex.getMessage(),
    23	                HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND
    24	        );
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    @ExceptionHandler(UnauthorizedProductAccessException.class)
    28	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleUnauthorized(UnauthorizedProductAccessException ex) {
    29	
    30	        return buildError(
    31	                "UNAUTHORIZED_PRODUCT_ACTION",
    32	                ex.getMessage(),
    33	                HttpStatus.FORBIDDEN
    34	        );
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    @ExceptionHandler(ProductStateException.class)
    38	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleState(ProductStateException ex) {
    39	
    40	        return buildError(
    41	                "INVALID_PRODUCT_STATE",
    42	                ex.getMessage(),
    43	                HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST
    44	        );
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    48	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    49	
    50	        List<String> errors = ex.getBindingResult()
    51	                .getFieldErrors()
    52	                .stream()
    53	                .map(error ->
    54	                        error.getField() + " : " + error.getDefaultMessage())
    55	                .toList();
    56	
    57	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    58	                .errorCode("VALIDATION_ERROR")
    59	                .message("Validation failed")
    60	                .details(errors)
    61	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    62	                .build();
    63	
    64	        return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(response);
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    68	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneric(Exception ex) {
    69	
    70	        log.error("Unexpected error: {}", ex.getMessage());
    71	
    72	        return buildError(
    73	                "INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR",
    74	                "Something went wrong",
    75	                HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR
    76	        );
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    private ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> buildError(
    80	            String code,
    81	            String message,
    82	            HttpStatus status) {
    83	
    84	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    85	                .errorCode(code)
    86	                .message(message)
    87	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    88	                .build();
    89	
    90	        return new ResponseEntity<>(response, status);
    91	    }
    92	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.filter;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     8	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     9	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.UUID;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Picks up the {@code X-Correlation-Id} header set by the API Gateway and
    18	 * stores it in SLF4J MDC so it appears in every log statement for the request.
    19	 *
    20	 * <p>Also attaches the header to the HTTP response so callers can trace
    21	 * requests end-to-end.
    22	 */
    23	@Component
    24	@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    25	public class CorrelationIdFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    26	
    27	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    28	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    29	
    30	    @Override
    31	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    32	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    33	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    34	        String correlationId = request.getHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    35	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    36	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        MDC.put(MDC_KEY, correlationId);
    40	        response.addHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, correlationId);
    41	
    42	        try {
    43	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    44	        } finally {
    45	            MDC.remove(MDC_KEY);
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/kafka/consumer/ReviewEventConsumer.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/kafka/consumer/ReviewEventConsumer.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.kafka.consumer;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.product_service.kafka.event.ReviewSubmittedEvent;
     4	import com.sourabh.product_service.service.ProductService;
     5	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     6	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     7	import org.springframework.kafka.annotation.KafkaListener;
     8	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     9	
    10	@Component
    11	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    12	@Slf4j
    13	public class ReviewEventConsumer {
    14	
    15	    private final ProductService productService;
    16	
    17	    @KafkaListener(topics = "review.submitted", groupId = "product-service")
    18	    public void handleReviewSubmitted(ReviewSubmittedEvent event) {
    19	        log.info("Received ReviewSubmittedEvent: productUuid={}, rating={}",
    20	                event.getProductUuid(), event.getRating());
    21	        productService.updateRating(event.getProductUuid(), event.getRating());
    22	    }
    23	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.security;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     5	import org.springframework.web.servlet.HandlerInterceptor;
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * No longer active — superseded by InternalSecretFilter (servlet filter).
     9	 * Kept for reference only; not registered in WebConfig, not a Spring bean.
    10	 */
    11	public class InternalSecretInterceptor implements HandlerInterceptor {
    12	
    13	    private final String expectedSecret;
    14	
    15	    public InternalSecretInterceptor(String expectedSecret) {
    16	        this.expectedSecret = expectedSecret;
    17	    }
    18	
    19	
    20	
    21	    @Override
    22	    public boolean preHandle(HttpServletRequest request,
    23	                             HttpServletResponse response,
    24	                             Object handler) throws Exception {
    25	
    26	        String providedSecret = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (providedSecret == null || !providedSecret.equals(expectedSecret)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return false;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        return true;
    34	    }
    35	}
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/service/ProductService.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.service;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request.CreateProductRequest;
     4	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request.UpdateProductRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.response.ProductResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.product_service.common.PageResponse;
     7	
     8	public interface ProductService {
     9	
    10	    ProductResponse createProduct(CreateProductRequest request, String sellerUuid);
    11	
    12	    ProductResponse updateProduct(String uuid,
    13	                                  UpdateProductRequest request,
    14	                                  String role,
    15	                                  String sellerUuid);
    16	
    17	    String approveProduct(String uuid);
    18	
    19	    String blockProduct(String uuid);
    20	
    21	    String unblockProduct(String uuid);
    22	
    23	    String softDeleteProduct(String uuid, String role, String sellerUuid);
    24	
    25	    PageResponse<ProductResponse> listProducts(
    26	            int page,
    27	            int size,
    28	            String sortBy,
    29	            String direction,
    30	            String role,
    31	            String sellerUuid,
    32	            String keyword);
    33	
    34	    /**
    35	     * Returns a product by UUID.
    36	     * Buyers and unauthenticated callers (role = null) only see ACTIVE products.
    37	     * SELLER / ADMIN see any non-deleted product.
    38	     */
    39	    ProductResponse getProductByUuid(String uuid, String role);
    40	
    41	    String reduceStock(String productUuid, Integer quantity);
    42	
    43	    /** Saga compensation: restore stock after a failed payment. */
```

## product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/service/impl/ProductServiceImpl.java

Path: `product-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/product_service/service/impl/ProductServiceImpl.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.product_service.service.impl;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.product_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request.CreateProductRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.request.UpdateProductRequest;
     6	import com.sourabh.product_service.dto.response.ProductResponse;
     7	import com.sourabh.product_service.entity.Product;
     8	import com.sourabh.product_service.entity.ProductStatus;
     9	import com.sourabh.product_service.exception.ProductNotFoundException;
    10	import com.sourabh.product_service.exception.ProductStateException;
    11	import com.sourabh.product_service.exception.UnauthorizedProductAccessException;
    12	import com.sourabh.product_service.repository.ProductRepository;
    13	import com.sourabh.product_service.service.ProductService;
    14	import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaBuilder;
    15	import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Predicate;
    16	import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Root;
    17	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    18	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    19	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.CacheEvict;
    20	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.Cacheable;
    21	import org.springframework.data.domain.*;
    22	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    23	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    24	
    25	import java.util.List;
    26	import java.util.UUID;
    27	
    28	@Service
    29	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    30	@Slf4j
    31	public class ProductServiceImpl implements ProductService {
    32	
    33	    private final ProductRepository productRepository;
    34	
    35	    // ===============================
    36	    // CREATE PRODUCT
    37	    // ===============================
    38	
    39	    @Override
    40	    @Transactional
    41	    public ProductResponse createProduct(CreateProductRequest request, String sellerUuid) {
    42	
    43	        Product product = Product.builder()
    44	                .uuid(UUID.randomUUID().toString())
    45	                .name(request.getName())
    46	                .description(request.getDescription())
    47	                .price(request.getPrice())
    48	                .stock(request.getStock())
    49	                .category(request.getCategory())
    50	                .sellerUuid(sellerUuid)
    51	                .status(ProductStatus.DRAFT)
    52	                .isDeleted(false)
    53	                .imageUrl(request.getImageUrl())
    54	                .build();
    55	
    56	        productRepository.save(product);
    57	
    58	        log.info("Product created by seller: {}", sellerUuid);
    59	
    60	        return mapToResponse(product);
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    // ===============================
    64	    // UPDATE PRODUCT
    65	    // ===============================
    66	
    67	    @Override
    68	    @Transactional
    69	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#uuid")
    70	    public ProductResponse updateProduct(
    71	            String uuid,
    72	            UpdateProductRequest request,
    73	            String role,
    74	            String sellerUuid) {
    75	
    76	        Product product = productRepository
    77	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
    78	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
    79	
    80	        if ("SELLER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
    81	
    82	            if (!product.getSellerUuid().equals(sellerUuid)) {
    83	                throw new UnauthorizedProductAccessException("You can only update your own product");
    84	            }
    85	
    86	            if (product.getStatus() == ProductStatus.BLOCKED) {
    87	                throw new ProductStateException("Blocked product cannot be updated");
    88	            }
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        if (request.getName() != null)
    92	            product.setName(request.getName());
    93	
    94	        if (request.getDescription() != null)
    95	            product.setDescription(request.getDescription());
    96	
    97	        if (request.getPrice() != null)
    98	            product.setPrice(request.getPrice());
    99	
   100	        if (request.getStock() != null)
   101	            product.setStock(request.getStock());
   102	
   103	        if (request.getCategory() != null)
   104	            product.setCategory(request.getCategory());
   105	
   106	        if (request.getImageUrl() != null)
   107	            product.setImageUrl(request.getImageUrl());
   108	
   109	        productRepository.save(product);
   110	
   111	        log.info("Product updated: uuid={}, by role={}, sellerUuid={}", uuid, role, sellerUuid);
   112	
   113	        return mapToResponse(product);
   114	    }
   115	    // ===============================
   116	
   117	    @Override
   118	    @Transactional
   119	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#uuid")
   120	    public String approveProduct(String uuid) {
   121	
   122	        Product product = productRepository
   123	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   124	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   125	
   126	        product.setStatus(ProductStatus.ACTIVE);
   127	        productRepository.save(product);
   128	
   129	        log.info("Product approved: uuid={}", uuid);
   130	        return "Product approved";
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    // ===============================
   134	    // BLOCK PRODUCT (ADMIN)
   135	    // ===============================
   136	
   137	    @Override
   138	    @Transactional
   139	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#uuid")
   140	    public String blockProduct(String uuid) {
   141	
   142	        Product product = productRepository
   143	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   144	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   145	
   146	        product.setStatus(ProductStatus.BLOCKED);
   147	        productRepository.save(product);
   148	
   149	        log.info("Product blocked: uuid={}", uuid);
   150	        return "Product blocked";
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    // ===============================
   154	    // UNBLOCK PRODUCT (ADMIN)
   155	    // ===============================
   156	
   157	    @Override
   158	    @Transactional
   159	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#uuid")
   160	    public String unblockProduct(String uuid) {
   161	
   162	        Product product = productRepository
   163	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   164	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   165	
   166	        if (product.getStatus() != ProductStatus.BLOCKED) {
   167	            throw new ProductStateException("Product is not blocked");
   168	        }
   169	        // Return to DRAFT so seller must resubmit for approval
   170	        product.setStatus(ProductStatus.DRAFT);
   171	        productRepository.save(product);
   172	
   173	        log.info("Product unblocked (set to DRAFT): uuid={}", uuid);
   174	        return "Product unblocked and set back to DRAFT for re-approval";
   175	    }
   176	
   177	    // ===============================
   178	    // SOFT DELETE
   179	    // ===============================
   180	
   181	    @Override
   182	    @Transactional
   183	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#uuid")
   184	    public String softDeleteProduct(
   185	            String uuid,
   186	            String role,
   187	            String sellerUuid) {
   188	
   189	        Product product = productRepository
   190	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   191	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   192	
   193	        if ("SELLER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)
   194	                && !product.getSellerUuid().equals(sellerUuid)) {
   195	            throw new UnauthorizedProductAccessException("You can only delete your own product");
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        product.setIsDeleted(true);
   199	        productRepository.save(product);
   200	
   201	        log.info("Product soft-deleted: uuid={}, by role={}", uuid, role);
   202	        return "Product deleted";
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    // ===============================
   206	    // LIST PRODUCTS
   207	    // ===============================
   208	
   209	    @Override
   210	    public PageResponse<ProductResponse> listProducts(
   211	            int page,
   212	            int size,
   213	            String sortBy,
   214	            String direction,
   215	            String role,
   216	            String sellerUuid,
   217	            String keyword) {
   218	
   219	        Sort sort = direction.equalsIgnoreCase("asc")
   220	                ? Sort.by(sortBy).ascending()
   221	                : Sort.by(sortBy).descending();
   222	
   223	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, sort);
   224	
   225	        Page<Product> productPage;
   226	
   227	        if ("BUYER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
   228	
   229	            productPage = productRepository.findAll(
   230	                    (root, query, cb) -> cb.and(
   231	                            cb.isFalse(root.get("isDeleted")),
   232	                            cb.equal(root.get("status"), ProductStatus.ACTIVE),
   233	                            keywordPredicate(cb, root, keyword)
   234	                    ),
   235	                    pageable
   236	            );
   237	
   238	        } else if ("SELLER".equalsIgnoreCase(role)) {
   239	
   240	            productPage = productRepository.findAll(
   241	                    (root, query, cb) -> cb.and(
   242	                            cb.isFalse(root.get("isDeleted")),
   243	                            cb.equal(root.get("sellerUuid"), sellerUuid),
   244	                            keywordPredicate(cb, root, keyword)
   245	                    ),
   246	                    pageable
   247	            );
   248	
   249	        } else { // ADMIN
   250	
   251	            productPage = productRepository.findAll(
   252	                    (root, query, cb) -> cb.and(
   253	                            cb.isFalse(root.get("isDeleted")),
   254	                            keywordPredicate(cb, root, keyword)
   255	                    ),
   256	                    pageable
   257	            );
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        List<ProductResponse> responses = productPage.getContent()
   261	                .stream()
   262	                .map(this::mapToResponse)
   263	                .toList();
   264	
   265	        return PageResponse.<ProductResponse>builder()
   266	                .content(responses)
   267	                .page(productPage.getNumber())
   268	                .size(productPage.getSize())
   269	                .totalElements(productPage.getTotalElements())
   270	                .totalPages(productPage.getTotalPages())
   271	                .last(productPage.isLast())
   272	                .build();
   273	    }
   274	
   275	    // ===============================
   276	    @Override
   277	    @Cacheable(value = "products", key = "#uuid")
   278	    public ProductResponse getProductByUuid(String uuid, String role) {
   279	        log.debug("Cache miss for product uuid={} — fetching from DB", uuid);
   280	        Product product = productRepository
   281	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(uuid)
   282	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found: " + uuid));
   283	
   284	        // Buyers and unauthenticated callers only see ACTIVE products
   285	        boolean isPrivileged = "ADMIN".equalsIgnoreCase(role) || "SELLER".equalsIgnoreCase(role);
   286	        if (!isPrivileged && product.getStatus() != ProductStatus.ACTIVE) {
   287	            throw new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found: " + uuid);
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        return mapToResponse(product);
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    // HELPER METHODS
   294	    // ===============================
   295	
   296	    private ProductResponse mapToResponse(Product product) {
   297	
   298	        return ProductResponse.builder()
   299	                .uuid(product.getUuid())
   300	                .name(product.getName())
   301	                .description(product.getDescription())
   302	                .price(product.getPrice())
   303	                .stock(product.getStock())
   304	                .category(product.getCategory())
   305	                .sellerUuid(product.getSellerUuid())
   306	                .status(product.getStatus().name())
   307	                .averageRating(product.getAverageRating())
   308	                .totalReviews(product.getTotalReviews())
   309	                .imageUrl(product.getImageUrl())
   310	                .build();
   311	    }
   312	
   313	    private Predicate keywordPredicate(
   314	            CriteriaBuilder cb,
   315	            Root<Product> root,
   316	            String keyword) {
   317	
   318	        if (keyword == null || keyword.isBlank()) {
   319	            return cb.conjunction();
   320	        }
   321	
   322	        String pattern = "%" + keyword.toLowerCase() + "%";
   323	
   324	        return cb.or(
   325	                cb.like(cb.lower(root.get("name")), pattern),
   326	                cb.like(cb.lower(root.get("description")), pattern),
   327	                cb.like(cb.lower(root.get("category")), pattern)
   328	        );
   329	    }
   330	
   331	    @Override
   332	    @Transactional
   333	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#productUuid")
   334	    public String reduceStock(String productUuid, Integer quantity) {
   335	
   336	        Product product = productRepository
   337	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(productUuid)
   338	                .orElseThrow(() ->
   339	                        new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   340	
   341	        if (product.getStatus() != ProductStatus.ACTIVE) {
   342	            throw new ProductStateException("Product is not active");
   343	        }
   344	
   345	        if (product.getStock() < quantity) {
   346	            throw new ProductStateException("Insufficient stock");
   347	        }
   348	
   349	        product.setStock(product.getStock() - quantity);
   350	
   351	        if (product.getStock() == 0) {
   352	            product.setStatus(ProductStatus.OUT_OF_STOCK);
   353	        }
   354	
   355	        productRepository.save(product);
   356	
   357	        log.info("Stock reduced for product uuid={} by quantity={}, remaining={}",
   358	                productUuid, quantity, product.getStock());
   359	        return "Stock reduced successfully";
   360	    }
   361	
   362	    @Override
   363	    @Transactional
   364	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#productUuid")
   365	    public String restoreStock(String productUuid, Integer quantity) {
   366	
   367	        Product product = productRepository
   368	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(productUuid)
   369	                .orElseThrow(() ->
   370	                        new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   371	
   372	        product.setStock(product.getStock() + quantity);
   373	
   374	        // If the product was out of stock, make it active again
   375	        if (product.getStatus() == ProductStatus.OUT_OF_STOCK && product.getStock() > 0) {
   376	            product.setStatus(ProductStatus.ACTIVE);
   377	        }
   378	
   379	        productRepository.save(product);
   380	
   381	        log.info("Stock restored for product uuid={} by quantity={}, new stock={}",
   382	                productUuid, quantity, product.getStock());
   383	        return "Stock restored successfully";
   384	    }
   385	
   386	    @Override
   387	    @Transactional
   388	    @CacheEvict(value = "products", key = "#productUuid")
   389	    public void updateRating(String productUuid, Integer rating) {
   390	
   391	        Product product = productRepository
   392	                .findByUuidAndIsDeletedFalse(productUuid)
   393	                .orElseThrow(() ->
   394	                        new ProductNotFoundException("Product not found"));
   395	
   396	        int currentCount = product.getTotalReviews();
   397	        double currentAverage = product.getAverageRating();
   398	
   399	        double newAverage =
   400	                ((currentAverage * currentCount) + rating)
   401	                        / (currentCount + 1);
   402	
   403	        product.setTotalReviews(currentCount + 1);
   404	        product.setAverageRating(newAverage);
   405	
   406	        productRepository.save(product);
   407	
   408	        log.info("Rating updated for product uuid={}: newAverage={}, totalReviews={}",
   409	                productUuid, String.format("%.2f", newAverage), currentCount + 1);
   410	    }
   411	
   412	}
```

## product-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql

Path: `product-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql`

```sql
     1	-- product-service: initial schema
     2	
     3	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS product (
     4	    id              BIGSERIAL      PRIMARY KEY,
     5	    uuid            VARCHAR(36)    NOT NULL UNIQUE,
     6	    name            VARCHAR(255)   NOT NULL,
     7	    description     VARCHAR(2000),
     8	    price           DOUBLE PRECISION NOT NULL,
     9	    stock           INTEGER        NOT NULL,
    10	    category        VARCHAR(255)   NOT NULL,
    11	    seller_uuid     VARCHAR(36)    NOT NULL,
    12	    status          VARCHAR(20),
    13	    is_deleted      BOOLEAN        NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    14	    average_rating  DOUBLE PRECISION NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,
    15	    total_reviews   INTEGER        NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    16	    created_at      TIMESTAMP,
    17	    updated_at      TIMESTAMP
    18	);
    19	
    20	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_product_uuid        ON product(uuid);
    21	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_product_seller_uuid ON product(seller_uuid);
    22	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_product_category    ON product(category);
    23	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_product_status      ON product(status);
```

## review-service/dockerfile

Path: `review-service/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl review-service dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY review-service/src review-service/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl review-service package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/review-service/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8080
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

```xml
   178					<groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
   179					<artifactId>spring-boot-maven-plugin</artifactId>
   180				</plugin>
   181			</plugins>
   182		</build>
   183	
   184	</project>
```

```java
     2
```

```java
     4	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	
     8	@Configuration
     9	public class FeignConfig {
    10	
    11	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    12	    private String internalSecret;
    13	
    14	    @Bean
    15	    public RequestInterceptor feignOutboundSecretInterceptor() {
    16	        return template -> template.header("X-Internal-Secret", internalSecret);
    17	    }
    18	}
```
