## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
     9	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.Collections;
    15	import java.util.List;
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Reads the {@code X-User-Role} header forwarded by the API Gateway and
    19	 * populates the Spring Security context so that {@code @PreAuthorize}
    20	 * method-level annotations can be evaluated.
    21	 */
    22	@Component
    23	public class HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    24	
    25	    @Override
    26	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    27	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    28	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    29	        String role = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    30	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    31	
    32	        if (role != null && !role.isBlank()) {
    33	            List<SimpleGrantedAuthority> authorities =
    34	                    Collections.singletonList(new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role.toUpperCase()));
    35	            UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken authentication =
    36	                    new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(userUuid, null, authorities);
    37	            SecurityContextHolder.getContext().setAuthentication(authentication);
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    41	    }
    42	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	
     8	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    11	
    12	import java.io.IOException;
    13	
    14	@Component
    15	public class InternalSecretFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    16	
    17	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    18	    private String internalSecret;
    19	
    20	    @Override
    21	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    22	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    23	                                    FilterChain filterChain)
    24	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    25	
    26	        String header = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (!internalSecret.equals(header)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    34	    }
    35	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.config;
     2	
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
     5	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.jsontype.impl.LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator;
     6	import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
     7	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.EnableCaching;
     8	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     9	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
    10	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheConfiguration;
    11	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheManager;
    12	import org.springframework.data.redis.connection.RedisConnectionFactory;
    13	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer;
    14	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.RedisSerializationContext;
    15	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.StringRedisSerializer;
    16	
    17	import java.time.Duration;
    18	import java.util.HashMap;
    19	import java.util.Map;
    20	
    21	@Configuration
    22	@EnableCaching
    23	public class RedisCacheConfig {
    24	
    25	    /** Cache name — used in @Cacheable/@CacheEvict throughout review-service */
    26	    public static final String REVIEWS_CACHE = "reviews";
    27	
    28	    @Bean
    29	    public RedisCacheManager cacheManager(RedisConnectionFactory factory) {
    30	
    31	        ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
    32	        om.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    33	        om.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
    34	        om.activateDefaultTyping(
    35	                LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator.instance,
    36	                ObjectMapper.DefaultTyping.NON_FINAL);
    37	        GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer jsonSerializer =
    38	                new GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer(om);
    39	
    40	        RedisCacheConfiguration defaultConfig = RedisCacheConfiguration
    41	                .defaultCacheConfig()
    42	                .serializeKeysWith(
    43	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    44	                                .fromSerializer(new StringRedisSerializer()))
    45	                .serializeValuesWith(
    46	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    47	                                .fromSerializer(jsonSerializer))
    48	                .disableCachingNullValues();
    49	
    50	        Map<String, RedisCacheConfiguration> cacheConfigs = new HashMap<>();
    51	        cacheConfigs.put(REVIEWS_CACHE, defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(10)));
    52	
    53	        return RedisCacheManager.builder(factory)
    54	                .cacheDefaults(defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(10)))
    55	                .withInitialCacheConfigurations(cacheConfigs)
    56	                .build();
    57	    }
    58	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/config/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.method.configuration.EnableMethodSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
     9	import org.springframework.security.config.http.SessionCreationPolicy;
    10	import org.springframework.security.web.SecurityFilterChain;
    11	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter;
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * JWT validation happens at the API Gateway; this service trusts the
    15	 * forwarded {@code X-User-Role} header for method-level RBAC via {@code @PreAuthorize}.
    16	 */
    17	@Configuration
    18	@EnableMethodSecurity
    19	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    20	public class SecurityConfig {
    21	
    22	    private final HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter headerRoleAuthFilter;
    23	
    24	    @Bean
    25	    public SecurityFilterChain securityFilterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
    26	        http
    27	                .csrf(csrf -> csrf.disable())
    28	                .formLogin(form -> form.disable())
    29	                .httpBasic(basic -> basic.disable())
    30	                .sessionManagement(session -> session.sessionCreationPolicy(SessionCreationPolicy.STATELESS))
    31	                .exceptionHandling(ex -> ex
    32	                        .authenticationEntryPoint((req, res, e) ->
    33	                                res.sendError(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN, "Forbidden"))
    34	                )
    35	                .authorizeHttpRequests(auth -> auth.anyRequest().permitAll())
    36	                .addFilterBefore(headerRoleAuthFilter, UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter.class);
    37	        return http.build();
    38	    }
    39	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/controller/ReviewController.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/controller/ReviewController.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.controller;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.review_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.CreateReviewRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.ReviewResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.UpdateReviewRequest;
     7	import com.sourabh.review_service.service.ReviewService;
     8	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     9	import jakarta.validation.Valid;
    10	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    11	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    12	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    13	import org.springframework.security.access.prepost.PreAuthorize;
    14	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
    15	
    16	@RestController
    17	@RequestMapping("/api/review")
    18	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    19	@Slf4j
    20	public class ReviewController {
    21	
    22	    private final ReviewService reviewService;
    23	
    24	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    25	    // CREATE REVIEW  —  BUYER only
    26	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    27	
    28	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('BUYER')")
    29	    @PostMapping
    30	    public ResponseEntity<ReviewResponse> createReview(
    31	            @Valid @RequestBody CreateReviewRequest request,
    32	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    33	
    34	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    35	        return ResponseEntity.ok(reviewService.createReview(request, buyerUuid));
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    39	    // GET REVIEWS BY PRODUCT  —  public
    40	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    41	
    42	    @GetMapping("/product/{productUuid}")
    43	    public ResponseEntity<PageResponse<ReviewResponse>> getReviewsByProduct(
    44	            @PathVariable String productUuid,
    45	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
    46	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size) {
    47	
    48	        return ResponseEntity.ok(reviewService.getReviewsByProduct(productUuid, page, size));
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    52	    // GET SINGLE REVIEW  —  public
    53	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    54	
    55	    @GetMapping("/{uuid}")
    56	    public ResponseEntity<ReviewResponse> getReviewByUuid(@PathVariable String uuid) {
    57	        return ResponseEntity.ok(reviewService.getReviewByUuid(uuid));
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    61	    // UPDATE REVIEW  —  BUYER (own review only)
    62	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    63	
    64	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('BUYER')")
    65	    @PutMapping("/{uuid}")
    66	    public ResponseEntity<ReviewResponse> updateReview(
    67	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    68	            @Valid @RequestBody UpdateReviewRequest request,
    69	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    70	
    71	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    72	        return ResponseEntity.ok(reviewService.updateReview(uuid, request, buyerUuid));
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    76	    // DELETE REVIEW  —  BUYER (own) or ADMIN
    77	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    78	
    79	    @PreAuthorize("hasAnyRole('BUYER', 'ADMIN')")
    80	    @DeleteMapping("/{uuid}")
    81	    public ResponseEntity<String> deleteReview(
    82	            @PathVariable String uuid,
    83	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
    84	
    85	        String role = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    86	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    87	        return ResponseEntity.ok(reviewService.deleteReview(uuid, role, buyerUuid));
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    91	    // MY REVIEWS  —  BUYER only, paginated
    92	    // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    93	
    94	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('BUYER')")
    95	    @GetMapping("/me")
    96	    public ResponseEntity<PageResponse<ReviewResponse>> getMyReviews(
    97	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
    98	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size,
    99	            HttpServletRequest httpRequest) {
   100	
   101	        String buyerUuid = httpRequest.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
   102	        return ResponseEntity.ok(reviewService.getMyReviews(buyerUuid, page, size));
   103	    }
   104	}
   105	
   106	
```

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.dto;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.validation.constraints.Max;
     4	import jakarta.validation.constraints.Min;
     5	import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotBlank;
     6	import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotNull;
     7	import lombok.Getter;
     8	import lombok.Setter;
     9	
    10	@Getter
    11	@Setter
    12	public class CreateReviewRequest {
    13	
    14	    @NotBlank(message = "Order UUID is required")
    15	    private String orderUuid;
    16	
    17	    @NotBlank(message = "Product UUID is required")
    18	    private String productUuid;
    19	
    20	    @NotNull(message = "Rating is required")
    21	    @Min(value = 1, message = "Rating must be at least 1")
    22	    @Max(value = 5, message = "Rating must not exceed 5")
    23	    private Integer rating;
    24	
    25	    private String comment;
    26	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/entity/Review.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import jakarta.validation.constraints.Max;
     5	import jakarta.validation.constraints.Min;
     6	import lombok.*;
     7	
     8	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
     9	
    10	@Entity
    11	@Getter
    12	@Setter
    13	@Builder
    14	@NoArgsConstructor
    15	@AllArgsConstructor
    16	public class Review {
    17	
    18	    @Id
    19	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    20	    private Long id;
    21	
    22	    @Column(unique = true)
    23	    private String uuid;
    24	
    25	    private String productUuid;
    26	
    27	    private String sellerUuid;
    28	
    29	    private String buyerUuid;
    30	
    31	    @Min(1)
    32	    @Max(5)
    33	    private Integer rating;
    34	
    35	    @Column(length = 2000)
    36	    private String comment;
    37	
    38	    private LocalDateTime createdAt;
    39	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.exception;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.review_service.common.ErrorResponse;
     4	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     5	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
     7	import org.springframework.validation.FieldError;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
     9	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ExceptionHandler;
    10	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestControllerAdvice;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	import java.util.List;
    14	
    15	@Slf4j
    16	@RestControllerAdvice
    17	public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
    18	
    19	    @ExceptionHandler(ReviewException.class)
    20	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleReviewException(ReviewException ex) {
    21	        return buildError("REVIEW_ERROR", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    @ExceptionHandler(ReviewAlreadyExistsException.class)
    25	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleDuplicate(ReviewAlreadyExistsException ex) {
    26	        return buildError("REVIEW_ALREADY_EXISTS", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.CONFLICT);
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    @ExceptionHandler(ReviewAccessException.class)
    30	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleAccess(ReviewAccessException ex) {
    31	        return buildError("REVIEW_ACCESS_DENIED", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.FORBIDDEN);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @ExceptionHandler(ReviewNotFoundException.class)
    35	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleNotFound(ReviewNotFoundException ex) {
    36	        return buildError("REVIEW_NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    40	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    41	        List<String> errors = ex.getBindingResult()
    42	                .getAllErrors()
    43	                .stream()
    44	                .map(e -> ((FieldError) e).getField() + " : " + e.getDefaultMessage())
    45	                .toList();
    46	
    47	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    48	                .errorCode("VALIDATION_ERROR")
    49	                .message("Validation failed")
    50	                .details(errors)
    51	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    52	                .build();
    53	
    54	        return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(response);
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    58	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneral(Exception ex) {
    59	        log.error("Unhandled exception", ex);
    60	        return buildError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", "Something went wrong", HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR);
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    private ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> buildError(String code, String message, HttpStatus status) {
    64	        return new ResponseEntity<>(
    65	                ErrorResponse.builder()
    66	                        .errorCode(code)
    67	                        .message(message)
    68	                        .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    69	                        .build(),
    70	                status);
    71	    }
    72	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.filter;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     8	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     9	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.UUID;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Picks up the {@code X-Correlation-Id} header set by the API Gateway and
    18	 * stores it in SLF4J MDC so it appears in every log statement for the request.
    19	 *
    20	 * <p>Also attaches the header to the HTTP response so callers can trace
    21	 * requests end-to-end.
    22	 */
    23	@Component
    24	@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    25	public class CorrelationIdFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    26	
    27	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    28	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    29	
    30	    @Override
    31	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    32	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    33	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    34	        String correlationId = request.getHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    35	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    36	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        MDC.put(MDC_KEY, correlationId);
    40	        response.addHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, correlationId);
    41	
    42	        try {
    43	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    44	        } finally {
    45	            MDC.remove(MDC_KEY);
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.security;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     5	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     6	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     7	import org.springframework.web.servlet.HandlerInterceptor;
     8	
     9	@Component
    10	public class InternalSecretInterceptor implements HandlerInterceptor {
    11	
    12	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    13	    private String expectedSecret;
    14	
    15	    @Override
    16	    public boolean preHandle(HttpServletRequest request,
    17	                             HttpServletResponse response,
    18	                             Object handler) throws Exception {
    19	
    20	        String providedSecret = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    21	
    22	        if (providedSecret == null || !providedSecret.equals(expectedSecret)) {
    23	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    24	            return false;
    25	        }
    26	
    27	        return true;
    28	    }
    29	}
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/service/ReviewService.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/service/ReviewService.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.service;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.review_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.CreateReviewRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.ReviewResponse;
     6	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.UpdateReviewRequest;
     7	
     8	public interface ReviewService {
     9	
    10	    /**
    11	     * Create a new review. Only buyers may call this; the buyer's identity comes
    12	     * from the gateway-forwarded X-User-UUID header (buyerUuid).
    13	     */
    14	    ReviewResponse createReview(CreateReviewRequest request, String buyerUuid);
    15	
    16	    /**
    17	     * List paginated reviews for a product (visible to everyone).
    18	     */
    19	    PageResponse<ReviewResponse> getReviewsByProduct(String productUuid, int page, int size);
    20	
    21	    /**
    22	     * Get a single review by its UUID.
    23	     */
    24	    ReviewResponse getReviewByUuid(String reviewUuid);
    25	
    26	    /**
    27	     * Update the comment on an existing review.
    28	     * Only the review's author (buyer) may update it.
    29	     */
    30	    ReviewResponse updateReview(String reviewUuid, UpdateReviewRequest request, String buyerUuid);
    31	
    32	    /**
    33	     * Delete a review.
    34	     * Buyers may delete their own; ADMIN may delete any.
    35	     */
    36	    String deleteReview(String reviewUuid, String role, String buyerUuid);
    37	
    38	    /**
    39	     * List all reviews written by the authenticated buyer.
    40	     */
    41	    PageResponse<ReviewResponse> getMyReviews(String buyerUuid, int page, int size);
    42	}
    43	
    44	
```

## review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/service/impl/ReviewServiceImpl.java

Path: `review-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/review_service/service/impl/ReviewServiceImpl.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.service.impl;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.review_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.CreateReviewRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.OrderDto;
     6	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.OrderItemDto;
     7	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.ReviewResponse;
     8	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.UpdateReviewRequest;
     9	import com.sourabh.review_service.entity.Review;
    10	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewAccessException;
    11	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewAlreadyExistsException;
    12	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewException;
    13	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewNotFoundException;
    14	import com.sourabh.review_service.feign.OrderServiceClient;
    15	import com.sourabh.review_service.kafka.event.ReviewSubmittedEvent;
    16	import com.sourabh.review_service.repository.ReviewRepository;
    17	import com.sourabh.review_service.service.ReviewService;
    18	import feign.FeignException;
    19	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    20	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    21	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.CacheEvict;
    22	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.Cacheable;
    23	import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
    24	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
    25	import org.springframework.data.domain.Pageable;
    26	import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort;
    27	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    28	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    29	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    30	
    31	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    32	import java.util.List;
    33	import java.util.UUID;
    34	
    35	@Service
    36	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    37	@Transactional
    38	@Slf4j
    39	public class ReviewServiceImpl implements ReviewService {
    40	
    41	    private final ReviewRepository reviewRepository;
    42	    private final OrderServiceClient orderServiceClient;
    43	    private final KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    44	
    45	    private static final String TOPIC_REVIEW_SUBMITTED = "review.submitted";
    46	
    47	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    48	    // CREATE REVIEW
    49	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    50	
    51	    @Override
    52	    @CacheEvict(value = "reviews", key = "#request.productUuid")
    53	    public ReviewResponse createReview(CreateReviewRequest request, String buyerUuid) {
    54	
    55	        OrderDto order = fetchOrder(request.getOrderUuid());
    56	
    57	        if (!order.getBuyerUuid().equals(buyerUuid)) {
    58	            throw new ReviewAccessException("You can only review orders that belong to you");
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        if (!"DELIVERED".equalsIgnoreCase(order.getStatus())) {
    62	            throw new ReviewException("Reviews can only be submitted after the order is delivered");
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        OrderItemDto item = order.getItems()
    66	                .stream()
    67	                .filter(i -> i.getProductUuid().equals(request.getProductUuid()))
    68	                .findFirst()
    69	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ReviewException(
    70	                        "Product " + request.getProductUuid() + " is not part of this order"));
    71	
    72	        if (reviewRepository.existsByProductUuidAndBuyerUuid(request.getProductUuid(), buyerUuid)) {
    73	            throw new ReviewAlreadyExistsException("You have already reviewed this product");
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        String reviewUuid = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    77	
    78	        Review review = Review.builder()
    79	                .uuid(reviewUuid)
    80	                .productUuid(request.getProductUuid())
    81	                .sellerUuid(item.getSellerUuid())
    82	                .buyerUuid(buyerUuid)
    83	                .rating(request.getRating())
    84	                .comment(request.getComment())
    85	                .createdAt(LocalDateTime.now())
    86	                .build();
    87	
    88	        reviewRepository.save(review);
    89	        log.info("Review saved: productUuid={}, buyerUuid={}, rating={}",
    90	                request.getProductUuid(), buyerUuid, request.getRating());
    91	
    92	        kafkaTemplate.send(TOPIC_REVIEW_SUBMITTED,
    93	                new ReviewSubmittedEvent(request.getProductUuid(), request.getRating(), reviewUuid));
    94	        log.info("ReviewSubmittedEvent published: productUuid={}", request.getProductUuid());
    95	
    96	        return mapToResponse(review);
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   100	    // GET REVIEWS BY PRODUCT (paginated)
   101	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   102	
   103	    @Override
   104	    @Cacheable(value = "reviews", key = "#productUuid + '-' + #page + '-' + #size")
   105	    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
   106	    public PageResponse<ReviewResponse> getReviewsByProduct(String productUuid, int page, int size) {
   107	        log.debug("Fetching reviews for productUuid={}, page={}", productUuid, page);
   108	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, Sort.by("createdAt").descending());
   109	        Page<Review> reviewPage = reviewRepository.findByProductUuid(productUuid, pageable);
   110	        return toPageResponse(reviewPage);
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   114	    // GET REVIEW BY UUID
   115	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   116	
   117	    @Override
   118	    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
   119	    public ReviewResponse getReviewByUuid(String reviewUuid) {
   120	        Review review = reviewRepository.findByUuid(reviewUuid)
   121	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ReviewNotFoundException("Review not found: " + reviewUuid));
   122	        return mapToResponse(review);
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   126	    // UPDATE REVIEW (comment only)
   127	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   128	
   129	    @Override
   130	    @CacheEvict(value = "reviews", allEntries = true)
   131	    public ReviewResponse updateReview(String reviewUuid, UpdateReviewRequest request, String buyerUuid) {
   132	        Review review = reviewRepository.findByUuid(reviewUuid)
   133	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ReviewNotFoundException("Review not found: " + reviewUuid));
   134	
   135	        if (!review.getBuyerUuid().equals(buyerUuid)) {
   136	            throw new ReviewAccessException("You can only edit your own reviews");
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        if (request.getComment() != null) {
   140	            review.setComment(request.getComment());
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        reviewRepository.save(review);
   144	        log.info("Review updated: uuid={}", reviewUuid);
   145	        return mapToResponse(review);
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   149	    // DELETE REVIEW
   150	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   151	
   152	    @Override
   153	    @CacheEvict(value = "reviews", allEntries = true)
   154	    public String deleteReview(String reviewUuid, String role, String buyerUuid) {
   155	        Review review = reviewRepository.findByUuid(reviewUuid)
   156	                .orElseThrow(() -> new ReviewNotFoundException("Review not found: " + reviewUuid));
   157	
   158	        boolean isAdmin = "ADMIN".equalsIgnoreCase(role);
   159	        if (!isAdmin && !review.getBuyerUuid().equals(buyerUuid)) {
   160	            throw new ReviewAccessException("You can only delete your own reviews");
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        reviewRepository.delete(review);
   164	        log.info("Review deleted: uuid={}, by role={}", reviewUuid, role);
   165	        return "Review deleted successfully";
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   169	    // GET MY REVIEWS (buyer's own reviews, paginated)
   170	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   171	
   172	    @Override
   173	    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
   174	    public PageResponse<ReviewResponse> getMyReviews(String buyerUuid, int page, int size) {
   175	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, Sort.by("createdAt").descending());
   176	        Page<Review> reviewPage = reviewRepository.findByBuyerUuid(buyerUuid, pageable);
   177	        return toPageResponse(reviewPage);
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   181	    // Helpers
   182	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   183	
   184	    private OrderDto fetchOrder(String orderUuid) {
   185	        try {
   186	            return orderServiceClient.getOrder(orderUuid);
   187	        } catch (FeignException.NotFound e) {
   188	            throw new ReviewException("Order not found: " + orderUuid);
   189	        }
   190	    }
   191	
   192	    private PageResponse<ReviewResponse> toPageResponse(Page<Review> page) {
   193	        List<ReviewResponse> content = page.getContent().stream()
   194	                .map(this::mapToResponse)
   195	                .toList();
   196	        return PageResponse.<ReviewResponse>builder()
   197	                .content(content)
   198	                .page(page.getNumber())
   199	                .size(page.getSize())
   200	                .totalElements(page.getTotalElements())
   201	                .totalPages(page.getTotalPages())
   202	                .last(page.isLast())
   203	                .build();
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    private ReviewResponse mapToResponse(Review review) {
   207	        return ReviewResponse.builder()
   208	                .uuid(review.getUuid())
   209	                .productUuid(review.getProductUuid())
   210	                .sellerUuid(review.getSellerUuid())
   211	                .buyerUuid(review.getBuyerUuid())
   212	                .rating(review.getRating())
   213	                .comment(review.getComment())
   214	                .createdAt(review.getCreatedAt())
   215	                .build();
   216	    }
   217	}
```

## review-service/src/main/resources/application.properties

Path: `review-service/src/main/resources/application.properties`

```properties
     1	spring.application.name=review-service
     2	server.port=8080
     3	
     4	spring.datasource.url=jdbc:postgresql://postgres:5432/review_db
     5	spring.datasource.username=${DB_USERNAME:postgres}
     6	spring.datasource.password=${DB_PASSWORD:postgres}
     7	
     8	spring.jpa.hibernate.ddl-auto=validate
     9	spring.jpa.show-sql=false
    10	spring.jpa.properties.hibernate.format_sql=true
    11	
    12	internal.secret=${INTERNAL_SECRET:veryStrongInternalSecret123}
    13	
    14	spring.data.redis.host=${REDIS_HOST:redis}
    15	spring.data.redis.port=${REDIS_PORT:6379}
    16	
    17	logging.level.com.sourabh.review_service=INFO
    18	logging.level.org.springframework.cache=DEBUG
    19	
    20	springdoc.api-docs.enabled=true
    21	springdoc.api-docs.path=/api/review/v3/api-docs
    22	springdoc.swagger-ui.enabled=false
    23	
    24	spring.cache.type=redis
    25	spring.cache.redis.time-to-live=600000
    26	spring.cache.redis.cache-null-values=false
    27	
    28	# Downstream Service URLs (Feign)
    29	service.order.url=${ORDER_SERVICE_URL:http://order-service:8080}
    30	
    31	# Feign + Resilience4j Circuit Breaker
    32	spring.cloud.openfeign.circuitbreaker.enabled=true
    33	resilience4j.circuitbreaker.instances.order-service.sliding-window-size=10
    34	resilience4j.circuitbreaker.instances.order-service.failure-rate-threshold=50
    35	resilience4j.circuitbreaker.instances.order-service.wait-duration-in-open-state=10s
    36	resilience4j.circuitbreaker.instances.order-service.permitted-number-of-calls-in-half-open-state=3
    37	
    38	# Kafka (producer: review.submitted)
    39	spring.kafka.bootstrap-servers=${KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS:kafka:9092}
    40	spring.kafka.producer.key-serializer=org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringSerializer
    41	spring.kafka.producer.value-serializer=org.springframework.kafka.support.serializer.JsonSerializer
    42	
    43	spring.flyway.enabled=true
    44	spring.flyway.locations=classpath:db/migration
    45	spring.flyway.baseline-on-migrate=true
    46	
    47	# Config Server (loads eureka, management, tracing, logging.pattern — see config-server/config/application.properties)
    48	spring.config.import=optional:configserver:${CONFIG_SERVER_URL:http://config-server:8888}
```

## review-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql

Path: `review-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql`

```sql
     1	-- review-service: initial schema
     2	
     3	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS review (
     4	    id           BIGSERIAL    PRIMARY KEY,
     5	    uuid         VARCHAR(36)  UNIQUE,
     6	    product_uuid VARCHAR(36),
     7	    seller_uuid  VARCHAR(36),
     8	    buyer_uuid   VARCHAR(36),
     9	    rating       INTEGER,
    10	    comment      VARCHAR(2000),
    11	    created_at   TIMESTAMP
    12	);
    13	
    14	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_review_product_uuid ON review(product_uuid);
    15	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_review_buyer_uuid   ON review(buyer_uuid);
```

## review-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/review_service/service/ReviewServiceImplTest.java

Path: `review-service/src/test/java/com/sourabh/review_service/service/ReviewServiceImplTest.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.review_service.service;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.review_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.CreateReviewRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.OrderDto;
     6	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.OrderItemDto;
     7	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.ReviewResponse;
     8	import com.sourabh.review_service.dto.UpdateReviewRequest;
     9	import com.sourabh.review_service.entity.Review;
    10	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewAccessException;
    11	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewAlreadyExistsException;
    12	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewException;
    13	import com.sourabh.review_service.exception.ReviewNotFoundException;
    14	import com.sourabh.review_service.feign.OrderServiceClient;
    15	import com.sourabh.review_service.kafka.event.ReviewSubmittedEvent;
    16	import com.sourabh.review_service.repository.ReviewRepository;
    17	import com.sourabh.review_service.service.impl.ReviewServiceImpl;
    18	import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
    19	import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
    20	import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
    21	import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtendWith;
    22	import org.mockito.InjectMocks;
    23	import org.mockito.Mock;
    24	import org.mockito.junit.jupiter.MockitoExtension;
    25	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageImpl;
    26	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
    27	import org.springframework.kafka.core.KafkaTemplate;
    28	
    29	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    30	import java.util.List;
    31	import java.util.Optional;
    32	
    33	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
    34	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThatThrownBy;
    35	import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.any;
    36	import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.eq;
    37	import static org.mockito.Mockito.*;
    38	
    39	@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
    40	@DisplayName("ReviewServiceImpl Unit Tests")
    41	class ReviewServiceImplTest {
    42	
    43	    @Mock private ReviewRepository reviewRepository;
    44	    @Mock private OrderServiceClient orderServiceClient;
    45	    @Mock private KafkaTemplate<String, Object> kafkaTemplate;
    46	
    47	    @InjectMocks
    48	    private ReviewServiceImpl reviewService;
    49	
    50	    private OrderDto deliveredOrder;
    51	    private CreateReviewRequest createRequest;
    52	
    53	    @BeforeEach
    54	    void setUp() {
    55	        OrderItemDto item = new OrderItemDto();
    56	        item.setProductUuid("prod-uuid");
    57	        item.setSellerUuid("seller-uuid");
    58	
    59	        deliveredOrder = new OrderDto();
    60	        deliveredOrder.setUuid("order-uuid");
    61	        deliveredOrder.setBuyerUuid("buyer-uuid");
    62	        deliveredOrder.setStatus("DELIVERED");
    63	        deliveredOrder.setItems(List.of(item));
    64	
    65	        createRequest = new CreateReviewRequest();
    66	        createRequest.setOrderUuid("order-uuid");
    67	        createRequest.setProductUuid("prod-uuid");
    68	        createRequest.setRating(5);
    69	        createRequest.setComment("Great product!");
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    73	    // createReview
    74	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    75	
    76	    @Test
    77	    @DisplayName("createReview: success — valid buyer, delivered order, new review")
    78	    void createReview_success() {
    79	        when(orderServiceClient.getOrder("order-uuid")).thenReturn(deliveredOrder);
    80	        when(reviewRepository.existsByProductUuidAndBuyerUuid("prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid")).thenReturn(false);
    81	        when(reviewRepository.save(any(Review.class))).thenAnswer(inv -> {
    82	            Review r = inv.getArgument(0);
    83	            r.setCreatedAt(LocalDateTime.now());
    84	            return r;
    85	        });
    86	
    87	        ReviewResponse result = reviewService.createReview(createRequest, "buyer-uuid");
    88	
    89	        assertThat(result).isNotNull();
    90	        assertThat(result.getProductUuid()).isEqualTo("prod-uuid");
    91	        assertThat(result.getRating()).isEqualTo(5);
    92	        verify(kafkaTemplate).send(eq("review.submitted"), any(ReviewSubmittedEvent.class));
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    @Test
    96	    @DisplayName("createReview: fails — order belongs to different buyer")
    97	    void createReview_wrongBuyer_throwsReviewAccessException() {
    98	        when(orderServiceClient.getOrder("order-uuid")).thenReturn(deliveredOrder);
    99	
   100	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.createReview(createRequest, "other-buyer"))
   101	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewAccessException.class)
   102	                .hasMessageContaining("belong to you");
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    @Test
   106	    @DisplayName("createReview: fails — order not yet delivered")
   107	    void createReview_notDelivered_throwsReviewException() {
   108	        deliveredOrder.setStatus("CONFIRMED");
   109	        when(orderServiceClient.getOrder("order-uuid")).thenReturn(deliveredOrder);
   110	
   111	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.createReview(createRequest, "buyer-uuid"))
   112	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewException.class)
   113	                .hasMessageContaining("after the order is delivered");
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    @Test
   117	    @DisplayName("createReview: fails — product not in order")
   118	    void createReview_productNotInOrder_throwsReviewException() {
   119	        createRequest.setProductUuid("other-prod");
   120	        when(orderServiceClient.getOrder("order-uuid")).thenReturn(deliveredOrder);
   121	
   122	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.createReview(createRequest, "buyer-uuid"))
   123	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewException.class)
   124	                .hasMessageContaining("not part of this order");
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    @Test
   128	    @DisplayName("createReview: fails — duplicate review")
   129	    void createReview_duplicate_throwsReviewAlreadyExistsException() {
   130	        when(orderServiceClient.getOrder("order-uuid")).thenReturn(deliveredOrder);
   131	        when(reviewRepository.existsByProductUuidAndBuyerUuid("prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid")).thenReturn(true);
   132	
   133	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.createReview(createRequest, "buyer-uuid"))
   134	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewAlreadyExistsException.class)
   135	                .hasMessageContaining("already reviewed");
   136	
   137	        verify(kafkaTemplate, never()).send(any(), any());
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   141	    // getReviewsByProduct
   142	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   143	
   144	    @Test
   145	    @DisplayName("getReviewsByProduct: returns paginated reviews")
   146	    void getReviewsByProduct_returnsPaginatedResults() {
   147	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   148	        var pageImpl = new PageImpl<>(List.of(r), PageRequest.of(0, 10), 1);
   149	        when(reviewRepository.findByProductUuid(eq("prod-uuid"), any())).thenReturn(pageImpl);
   150	
   151	        PageResponse<ReviewResponse> response = reviewService.getReviewsByProduct("prod-uuid", 0, 10);
   152	
   153	        assertThat(response.getContent()).hasSize(1);
   154	        assertThat(response.getTotalElements()).isEqualTo(1);
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   158	    // getReviewByUuid
   159	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   160	
   161	    @Test
   162	    @DisplayName("getReviewByUuid: success")
   163	    void getReviewByUuid_success() {
   164	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   165	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("rev-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.of(r));
   166	
   167	        ReviewResponse result = reviewService.getReviewByUuid("rev-uuid");
   168	
   169	        assertThat(result.getUuid()).isEqualTo("rev-uuid");
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    @Test
   173	    @DisplayName("getReviewByUuid: not found throws ReviewNotFoundException")
   174	    void getReviewByUuid_notFound() {
   175	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("bad-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.empty());
   176	
   177	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.getReviewByUuid("bad-uuid"))
   178	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewNotFoundException.class);
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   182	    // updateReview
   183	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   184	
   185	    @Test
   186	    @DisplayName("updateReview: success — buyer can update own review comment")
   187	    void updateReview_success() {
   188	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   189	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("rev-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.of(r));
   190	        when(reviewRepository.save(any(Review.class))).thenAnswer(inv -> inv.getArgument(0));
   191	
   192	        UpdateReviewRequest req = new UpdateReviewRequest();
   193	        req.setComment("Updated comment");
   194	
   195	        ReviewResponse result = reviewService.updateReview("rev-uuid", req, "buyer-uuid");
   196	
   197	        assertThat(result.getComment()).isEqualTo("Updated comment");
   198	    }
   199	
   200	    @Test
   201	    @DisplayName("updateReview: fails — wrong buyer")
   202	    void updateReview_wrongBuyer() {
   203	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   204	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("rev-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.of(r));
   205	
   206	        UpdateReviewRequest req = new UpdateReviewRequest();
   207	        req.setComment("Hacked!");
   208	
   209	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.updateReview("rev-uuid", req, "other-buyer"))
   210	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewAccessException.class);
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   214	    // deleteReview
   215	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   216	
   217	    @Test
   218	    @DisplayName("deleteReview: buyer can delete own review")
   219	    void deleteReview_byBuyer_success() {
   220	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   221	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("rev-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.of(r));
   222	
   223	        String result = reviewService.deleteReview("rev-uuid", "BUYER", "buyer-uuid");
   224	
   225	        assertThat(result).contains("deleted");
   226	        verify(reviewRepository).delete(r);
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    @Test
   230	    @DisplayName("deleteReview: admin can delete any review")
   231	    void deleteReview_byAdmin_success() {
   232	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   233	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("rev-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.of(r));
   234	
   235	        String result = reviewService.deleteReview("rev-uuid", "ADMIN", "admin-uuid");
   236	
   237	        assertThat(result).contains("deleted");
   238	        verify(reviewRepository).delete(r);
   239	    }
   240	
   241	    @Test
   242	    @DisplayName("deleteReview: fails — buyer tries to delete another's review")
   243	    void deleteReview_wrongBuyer_throwsReviewAccessException() {
   244	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   245	        when(reviewRepository.findByUuid("rev-uuid")).thenReturn(Optional.of(r));
   246	
   247	        assertThatThrownBy(() -> reviewService.deleteReview("rev-uuid", "BUYER", "other-buyer"))
   248	                .isInstanceOf(ReviewAccessException.class);
   249	    }
   250	
   251	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   252	    // getMyReviews
   253	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   254	
   255	    @Test
   256	    @DisplayName("getMyReviews: returns paginated reviews for the buyer")
   257	    void getMyReviews_returnsResults() {
   258	        Review r = buildReview("rev-uuid", "prod-uuid", "buyer-uuid");
   259	        var pageImpl = new PageImpl<>(List.of(r), PageRequest.of(0, 10), 1);
   260	        when(reviewRepository.findByBuyerUuid(eq("buyer-uuid"), any())).thenReturn(pageImpl);
   261	
   262	        PageResponse<ReviewResponse> response = reviewService.getMyReviews("buyer-uuid", 0, 10);
   263	
   264	        assertThat(response.getContent()).hasSize(1);
   265	        assertThat(response.getContent().get(0).getBuyerUuid()).isEqualTo("buyer-uuid");
   266	    }
   267	
   268	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   269	    // Helper
   270	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   271	
   272	    private Review buildReview(String uuid, String productUuid, String buyerUuid) {
   273	        return Review.builder()
   274	                .uuid(uuid)
   275	                .productUuid(productUuid)
   276	                .sellerUuid("seller-uuid")
   277	                .buyerUuid(buyerUuid)
   278	                .rating(4)
   279	                .comment("Good")
   280	                .createdAt(LocalDateTime.now())
   281	                .build();
   282	    }
   283	}
```

## user-service/dockerfile

Path: `user-service/dockerfile`

```dockerfile
     1	# ---- Build stage ----
     2	FROM maven:3.9-eclipse-temurin-17-alpine AS builder
     3	WORKDIR /workspace
     4	
     5	COPY pom.xml .
     6	COPY api-gateway/pom.xml api-gateway/
     7	COPY auth-service/pom.xml auth-service/
     8	COPY user-service/pom.xml user-service/
     9	COPY product-service/pom.xml product-service/
    10	COPY order-service/pom.xml order-service/
    11	COPY review-service/pom.xml review-service/
    12	COPY payment-service/pom.xml payment-service/
    13	COPY eureka-server/pom.xml eureka-server/
    14	COPY config-server/pom.xml config-server/
    15	RUN mvn -pl user-service dependency:go-offline -B --no-transfer-progress || true
    16	
    17	COPY user-service/src user-service/src
    18	RUN mvn -pl user-service package -DskipTests -B --no-transfer-progress
    19	
    20	# ---- Runtime stage ----
    21	FROM eclipse-temurin:17-jre-alpine
    22	WORKDIR /app
    23	COPY --from=builder /workspace/user-service/target/*.jar app.jar
    24	EXPOSE 8080
    25	ENTRYPOINT ["java", "-jar", "app.jar"]
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/common/ApiResponse.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/common/ApiResponse.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.common;
     2	
     3	import lombok.Builder;
     4	import lombok.Getter;
     5	
     6	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
     7	
     8	@Getter
     9	@Builder
    10	public class ApiResponse<T> {
    11	
    12	    private boolean success;
    13	    private String message;
    14	    private T data;
    15	    private LocalDateTime timestamp;
    16	
    17	    public static <T> ApiResponse<T> success(String message, T data) {
    18	        return ApiResponse.<T>builder()
    19	                .success(true)
    20	                .message(message)
    21	                .data(data)
    22	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    23	                .build();
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    public static <T> ApiResponse<T> failure(String message) {
    27	        return ApiResponse.<T>builder()
    28	                .success(false)
    29	                .message(message)
    30	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    31	                .build();
    32	    }
    33	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.springframework.security.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken;
     8	import org.springframework.security.core.authority.SimpleGrantedAuthority;
     9	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.Collections;
    15	import java.util.List;
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Reads the {@code X-User-Role} header forwarded by the API Gateway and
    19	 * populates the Spring Security context so that {@code @PreAuthorize}
    20	 * method-level annotations can be evaluated.
    21	 */
    22	@Component
    23	public class HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    24	
    25	    @Override
    26	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    27	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    28	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    29	        String role     = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    30	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    31	
    32	        if (role != null && !role.isBlank()) {
    33	            List<SimpleGrantedAuthority> authorities =
    34	                    Collections.singletonList(new SimpleGrantedAuthority("ROLE_" + role.toUpperCase()));
    35	            UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken authentication =
    36	                    new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(userUuid, null, authorities);
    37	            SecurityContextHolder.getContext().setAuthentication(authentication);
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    41	    }
    42	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/InternalSecretFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	
     8	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     9	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    10	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    11	
    12	import java.io.IOException;
    13	
    14	@Component
    15	public class InternalSecretFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    16	
    17	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    18	    private String internalSecret;
    19	
    20	    @Override
    21	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    22	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    23	                                    FilterChain filterChain)
    24	            throws ServletException, IOException {
    25	
    26	        String header = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    27	
    28	        if (!internalSecret.equals(header)) {
    29	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    30	            return;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    34	    }
    35	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/RedisCacheConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.config;
     2	
```
```java
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
     5	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.jsontype.impl.LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator;
     6	import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
     7	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.EnableCaching;
     8	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     9	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
    10	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheConfiguration;
    11	import org.springframework.data.redis.cache.RedisCacheManager;
    12	import org.springframework.data.redis.connection.RedisConnectionFactory;
    13	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer;
    14	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.RedisSerializationContext;
    15	import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.StringRedisSerializer;
    16	
    17	import java.time.Duration;
    18	import java.util.HashMap;
    19	import java.util.Map;
    20	
    21	@Configuration
    22	@EnableCaching
    23	public class RedisCacheConfig {
    24	
    25	    /** Cache names — used in @Cacheable/@CacheEvict throughout user-service */
    26	    public static final String USERS_BY_EMAIL_CACHE = "usersByEmail";
    27	    public static final String USERS_BY_UUID_CACHE  = "usersByUuid";
    28	
    29	    @Bean
    30	    public RedisCacheManager cacheManager(RedisConnectionFactory factory) {
    31	
    32	        ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
    33	        om.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    34	        om.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
    35	        om.activateDefaultTyping(
    36	                LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator.instance,
    37	                ObjectMapper.DefaultTyping.NON_FINAL);
    38	        GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer jsonSerializer =
    39	                new GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer(om);
    40	
    41	        RedisCacheConfiguration defaultConfig = RedisCacheConfiguration
    42	                .defaultCacheConfig()
    43	                .serializeKeysWith(
    44	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    45	                                .fromSerializer(new StringRedisSerializer()))
    46	                .serializeValuesWith(
    47	                        RedisSerializationContext.SerializationPair
    48	                                .fromSerializer(jsonSerializer))
    49	                .disableCachingNullValues();
    50	
    51	        // User lookups cached for 15 minutes (auth-service calls these on every login)
    52	        Map<String, RedisCacheConfiguration> cacheConfigs = new HashMap<>();
    53	        cacheConfigs.put(USERS_BY_EMAIL_CACHE, defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(15)));
    54	        cacheConfigs.put(USERS_BY_UUID_CACHE,  defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(15)));
    55	
    56	        return RedisCacheManager.builder(factory)
    57	                .cacheDefaults(defaultConfig.entryTtl(Duration.ofMinutes(15)))
    58	                .withInitialCacheConfigurations(cacheConfigs)
    59	                .build();
    60	    }
    61	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/SecurityConfig.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/SecurityConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.config;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
     6	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     7	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.method.configuration.EnableMethodSecurity;
     8	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
     9	import org.springframework.security.config.http.SessionCreationPolicy;
    10	import org.springframework.security.crypto.bcrypt.BCryptPasswordEncoder;
    11	import org.springframework.security.crypto.password.PasswordEncoder;
    12	import org.springframework.security.web.SecurityFilterChain;
    13	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter;
    14	
    15	/**
    16	 * User-service security config.
    17	 *
    18	 * JWT validation is handled exclusively at the API Gateway.
    19	 * The gateway injects X-User-Role / X-User-UUID headers which are read by
    20	 * {@link HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter} to populate the Spring Security context,
    21	 * enabling {@code @PreAuthorize} evaluation on controller methods.
    22	 */
    23	@Configuration
    24	@EnableMethodSecurity
    25	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    26	public class SecurityConfig {
    27	
    28	    private final HeaderRoleAuthenticationFilter headerRoleAuthFilter;
    29	
    30	    @Bean
    31	    public SecurityFilterChain securityFilterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
    32	        http
    33	                .csrf(csrf -> csrf.disable())
    34	                .formLogin(form -> form.disable())
    35	                .httpBasic(basic -> basic.disable())
    36	                .sessionManagement(session -> session.sessionCreationPolicy(SessionCreationPolicy.STATELESS))
    37	                .exceptionHandling(ex -> ex
    38	                        .authenticationEntryPoint((req, res, e) ->
    39	                                res.sendError(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN, "Forbidden"))
    40	                )
    41	                .authorizeHttpRequests(auth -> auth.anyRequest().permitAll())
    42	                .addFilterBefore(headerRoleAuthFilter, UsernamePasswordAuthenticationFilter.class);
    43	        return http.build();
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    @Bean
    47	    public PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder() {
    48	        return new BCryptPasswordEncoder();
    49	    }
    50	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/WebConfig.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/config/WebConfig.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.config;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.user_service.security.RoleInterceptor;
     4	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
     5	import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
     6	import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.InterceptorRegistry;
     7	import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.WebMvcConfigurer;
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * MVC interceptor registration.
    11	 *
    12	 * InternalSecretInterceptor is intentionally removed — its function is
    13	 * covered by InternalSecretFilter (a servlet filter that runs before Spring
    14	 * Security and applies to all request paths).
    15	 */
    16	@Configuration
    17	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    18	public class WebConfig implements WebMvcConfigurer {
    19	
    20	    private final RoleInterceptor roleInterceptor;
    21	
    22	    @Override
    23	    public void addInterceptors(InterceptorRegistry registry) {
    24	        registry.addInterceptor(roleInterceptor);
    25	    }
    26	}
    27	
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/controller/UserController.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/controller/UserController.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.controller;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.user_service.common.ApiResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.user_service.common.PageResponse;
     5	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.ChangePasswordRequest;
     6	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.RegisterRequest;
     7	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.UpdateProfileRequest;
     8	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.VerifyOTPRequest;
     9	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.response.InternalUserDto;
    10	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.response.UserResponse;
    11	import com.sourabh.user_service.service.UserService;
    12	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
    13	import jakarta.validation.Valid;
    14	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    15	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    16	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    17	import org.springframework.security.access.prepost.PreAuthorize;
    18	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
    19	
    20	@RestController
    21	@RequestMapping("/api/user")
    22	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    23	@Slf4j
    24	public class UserController {
    25	
    26	    private final UserService userService;
    27	
    28	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    29	    // PUBLIC ROUTES (no JWT required)
    30	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    31	
    32	    @PostMapping("/register")
    33	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<UserResponse>> register(
    34	            @Valid @RequestBody RegisterRequest request) {
    35	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
    36	                ApiResponse.success("User registered successfully. OTP sent.", userService.registerUser(request)));
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    @PostMapping("/verify-otp")
    40	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> verifyOTP(
    41	            @Valid @RequestBody VerifyOTPRequest request) {
    42	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.verifyOTP(request), null));
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    @PostMapping("/resend-otp")
    46	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> resendOTP(@RequestParam String email) {
    47	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.resendOTP(email), null));
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    51	    // AUTHENTICATED USER ROUTES (any verified user)
    52	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    53	
    54	    /** Get own profile. */
    55	    @PreAuthorize("isAuthenticated()")
    56	    @GetMapping("/me")
    57	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<UserResponse>> getProfile(HttpServletRequest request) {
    58	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    59	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success("Profile fetched successfully", userService.getProfile(userUuid)));
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    /** Update own profile (first/last name, phone). */
    63	    @PreAuthorize("isAuthenticated()")
    64	    @PutMapping("/me")
    65	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<UserResponse>> updateProfile(
    66	            @Valid @RequestBody UpdateProfileRequest body,
    67	            HttpServletRequest request) {
    68	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    69	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success("Profile updated successfully", userService.updateProfile(userUuid, body)));
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    /** Change own password. */
    73	    @PreAuthorize("isAuthenticated()")
    74	    @PutMapping("/me/change-password")
    75	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> changePassword(
    76	            @Valid @RequestBody ChangePasswordRequest body,
    77	            HttpServletRequest request) {
    78	        String userUuid = request.getHeader("X-User-UUID");
    79	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.changePassword(userUuid, body), null));
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    83	    // ADMIN ROUTES
    84	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    85	
    86	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
    87	    @PutMapping("/admin/approve/{uuid}")
    88	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> approveSeller(@PathVariable String uuid) {
    89	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.approveSeller(uuid), null));
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
    93	    @PutMapping("/admin/reject/{uuid}")
    94	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> rejectSeller(@PathVariable String uuid) {
    95	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.rejectSeller(uuid), null));
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
    99	    @PutMapping("/admin/block/{uuid}")
   100	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> blockUser(@PathVariable String uuid) {
   101	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.blockUser(uuid), null));
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
   105	    @PutMapping("/admin/unblock/{uuid}")
   106	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> unblockUser(@PathVariable String uuid) {
   107	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.unblockUser(uuid), null));
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
   111	    @GetMapping
   112	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<PageResponse<UserResponse>>> listUsers(
   113	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
   114	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size,
   115	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "createdAt") String sortBy,
   116	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "desc") String direction,
   117	            @RequestParam(required = false) String role,
   118	            @RequestParam(required = false) String status) {
   119	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success("Users fetched successfully",
   120	                userService.getAllUsers(page, size, sortBy, direction, role, status)));
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
   124	    @DeleteMapping("/{uuid}")
   125	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> softDelete(@PathVariable String uuid) {
   126	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.softDeleteUser(uuid), null));
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
   130	    @PutMapping("/restore/{uuid}")
   131	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<String>> restore(@PathVariable String uuid) {
   132	        return ResponseEntity.ok(ApiResponse.success(userService.restoreUser(uuid), null));
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    @PreAuthorize("hasRole('ADMIN')")
   136	    @GetMapping("/search")
   137	    public ResponseEntity<ApiResponse<PageResponse<UserResponse>>> searchUsers(
   138	            @RequestParam String keyword,
   139	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "0") int page,
   140	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "10") int size) {
   141	        return ResponseEntity.ok(
   142	                ApiResponse.success("Search results fetched successfully",
   143	                        userService.searchUsers(keyword, page, size)));
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   147	    // INTERNAL ROUTES — reachable only with X-Internal-Secret
   148	    // Returns InternalUserDto (contains hashed password for auth-service).
   149	    // Must NEVER be exposed publicly.
   150	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   151	
   152	    @GetMapping("/internal/email/{email}")
   153	    public ResponseEntity<InternalUserDto> getUserByEmailInternal(@PathVariable String email) {
   154	        log.debug("Internal lookup by email={}", email);
   155	        InternalUserDto dto = userService.getUserByEmailInternal(email);
   156	        return dto != null ? ResponseEntity.ok(dto) : ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    @GetMapping("/internal/uuid/{uuid}")
   160	    public ResponseEntity<InternalUserDto> getUserByUuidInternal(@PathVariable String uuid) {
   161	        log.debug("Internal lookup by uuid={}", uuid);
   162	        InternalUserDto dto = userService.getUserByUuidInternal(uuid);
   163	        return dto != null ? ResponseEntity.ok(dto) : ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
   164	    }
   165	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/dto/request/ChangePasswordRequest.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/dto/request/ChangePasswordRequest.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotBlank;
     4	import jakarta.validation.constraints.Size;
     5	import lombok.Getter;
     6	import lombok.Setter;
     7	
     8	@Getter
     9	@Setter
    10	public class ChangePasswordRequest {
    11	
    12	    @NotBlank(message = "Current password is required")
    13	    private String currentPassword;
    14	
    15	    @NotBlank(message = "New password is required")
    16	    @Size(min = 8, message = "New password must be at least 8 characters")
    17	    private String newPassword;
    18	
    19	    @NotBlank(message = "Confirm password is required")
    20	    private String confirmNewPassword;
    21	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/dto/request/RegisterRequest.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/dto/request/RegisterRequest.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.user_service.entity.Role;
     4	import jakarta.validation.constraints.*;
     5	
     6	import lombok.Getter;
     7	import lombok.Setter;
     8	
     9	@Getter
    10	@Setter
    11	public class RegisterRequest {
    12	
    13	    @NotBlank
    14	    @Size(max = 50)
    15	    private String firstName;
    16	
    17	    @NotBlank
    18	    @Size(max = 50)
    19	    private String lastName;
    20	
    21	    @Email
    22	    @NotBlank
    23	    @Size(max = 100)
    24	    private String email;
    25	
    26	    @NotBlank
    27	    @Size(min = 8, max = 100)
    28	    private String password;
    29	
    30	    @Pattern(regexp = "^[0-9]{10}$",
    31	            message = "Phone number must be 10 digits")
    32	    private String phoneNumber;
    33	
    34	    @NotNull
    35	    private Role role;
    36	
    37	}
```

```java
     3	import lombok.Builder;
     4	import lombok.Getter;
     5	import lombok.extern.jackson.Jacksonized;
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Internal-only DTO returned by /api/user/internal/** endpoints.
     9	 *
    10	 * This DTO includes the hashed password so the auth-service can perform
    11	 * BCrypt comparison. It must NEVER be served on a public/external endpoint.
    12	 */
    13	@Getter
    14	@Builder
    15	@Jacksonized
    16	public class InternalUserDto {
    17	
    18	    private String uuid;
    19	    private String email;
    20	    private String password;   // BCrypt hash — for auth-service comparison only
    21	    private String role;
    22	    private String status;
    23	    private boolean emailVerified;
    24	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/entity/BaseAuditEntity.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/entity/BaseAuditEntity.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.Column;
     4	import jakarta.persistence.EntityListeners;
     5	import jakarta.persistence.MappedSuperclass;
     6	import lombok.Getter;
     7	import lombok.Setter;
     8	import org.springframework.data.annotation.CreatedDate;
     9	import org.springframework.data.annotation.LastModifiedDate;
    10	import org.springframework.data.jpa.domain.support.AuditingEntityListener;
    11	
    12	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Shared audit fields for all entities.
    16	 * Spring Data JPA populates {@code createdAt} and {@code updatedAt}
    17	 * automatically when {@code @EnableJpaAuditing} is present on the main class.
    18	 */
    19	@MappedSuperclass
    20	@EntityListeners(AuditingEntityListener.class)
    21	@Getter
    22	@Setter
    23	public abstract class BaseAuditEntity {
    24	
    25	    @CreatedDate
    26	    @Column(updatable = false)
    27	    private LocalDateTime createdAt;
    28	
    29	    @LastModifiedDate
    30	    private LocalDateTime updatedAt;
    31	}
```
