## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/entity/OTPVerification.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/entity/OTPVerification.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.entity;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.*;
     5	
     6	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
     7	
     8	@Entity
     9	@Table(name = "otp_verifications")
    10	@Getter
    11	@Setter
    12	@NoArgsConstructor
    13	@AllArgsConstructor
    14	@Builder
    15	public class OTPVerification extends BaseAuditEntity {
    16	
    17	    @Id
    18	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    19	    private Long id;
    20	
    21	    @Column(nullable = false)
    22	    private String otpCode;
    23	
    24	    @Enumerated(EnumType.STRING)
    25	    @Column(nullable = false)
    26	    private OTPType type;
    27	
    28	    @Column(nullable = false)
    29	    private LocalDateTime expiryTime;
    30	
    31	    @Column(nullable = false)
    32	    private boolean verified;
    33	
    34	    @Column(nullable = false)
    35	    private int attemptCount;
    36	
    37	    private LocalDateTime lastSentAt;
    38	
    39	
    40	    // Relationship with User
    41	    @ManyToOne(fetch = FetchType.LAZY)
    42	    @JoinColumn(name = "user_id", nullable = false)
    43	    private User user;
    44	
    45	    // Lifecycle
    46	    @PrePersist
    47	    protected void onCreateOTP() {
    48	        this.verified = false;
    49	        this.attemptCount = 0;
    50	        this.lastSentAt = LocalDateTime.now();
    51	
    52	    }
    53	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/entity/User.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/entity/User.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.entity;
     2	
```
```java
     3	import jakarta.persistence.*;
     4	import lombok.*;
     5	
     6	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
     7	import java.util.UUID;
     8	
     9	@Entity
    10	@Table(name = "users",
    11	        uniqueConstraints = {
    12	                @UniqueConstraint(columnNames = "email"),
    13	                @UniqueConstraint(columnNames = "uuid")
    14	        }
    15	)
    16	@Getter
    17	@Setter
    18	@NoArgsConstructor
    19	@AllArgsConstructor
    20	@Builder
    21	public class User extends BaseAuditEntity {
    22	
    23	    // ========================
    24	    // Identity
    25	    // ========================
    26	
    27	    @Id
    28	    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    29	    private Long id;
    30	
    31	    @Column(nullable = false, updatable = false)
    32	    private String uuid;
    33	
    34	    // ========================
    35	    // Personal Information
    36	    // ========================
    37	
    38	    @Column(nullable = false)
    39	    private String firstName;
    40	
    41	    @Column(nullable = false)
    42	    private String lastName;
    43	
    44	    @Column(nullable = false, unique = true)
    45	    private String email;
    46	
    47	    @Column(length = 15)
    48	    private String phoneNumber;
    49	
    50	    // ========================
    51	    // Security
    52	    // ========================
    53	
    54	    @Column(nullable = false)
    55	    private String password;
    56	
    57	    @Enumerated(EnumType.STRING)
    58	    @Column(nullable = false)
    59	    private Role role;
    60	
    61	    @Enumerated(EnumType.STRING)
    62	    @Column(nullable = false)
    63	    private UserStatus status;
    64	
    65	    @Column(nullable = false)
    66	    private boolean emailVerified;
    67	
    68	    @Column(nullable = false)
    69	    private boolean isApproved; // for seller approval
    70	
    71	    @Column(nullable = false)
    72	    private boolean isDeleted;
    73	
    74	    private LocalDateTime lastLoginAt;
    75	
    76	    // ========================
    77	    // Lifecycle Hook
    78	    // ========================
    79	
    80	    @PrePersist
    81	    protected void onCreateUser() {
    82	        this.uuid = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    83	        this.emailVerified = false;
    84	        this.isApproved = false;
    85	        this.isDeleted = false;
    86	
    87	        if (this.status == null) {
    88	            this.status = UserStatus.PENDING_VERIFICATION;
    89	        }
    90	    }
    91	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/exception/GlobalExceptionHandler.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.exception;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.user_service.common.ErrorResponse;
     4	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
     5	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
     7	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
     8	import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
     9	import org.springframework.validation.FieldError;
    10	
    11	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    12	import java.util.List;
    13	
    14	@Slf4j
    15	@RestControllerAdvice
    16	public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
    17	
    18	    @ExceptionHandler(UserAlreadyExistsException.class)
    19	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleUserExists(UserAlreadyExistsException ex) {
    20	        return buildError("USER_ALREADY_EXISTS", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.CONFLICT);
    21	    }
    22	
    23	    @ExceptionHandler(UserNotFoundException.class)
    24	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleUserNotFound(UserNotFoundException ex) {
    25	        return buildError("USER_NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    @ExceptionHandler(OTPException.class)
    29	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleOTPException(OTPException ex) {
    30	        return buildError("OTP_ERROR", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    @ExceptionHandler(UserStateException.class)
    34	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleUserState(UserStateException ex) {
    35	        return buildError("USER_STATE_ERROR", ex.getMessage(), HttpStatus.CONFLICT);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    39	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidationException(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
    40	
    41	        List<String> errors = ex.getBindingResult()
    42	                .getAllErrors()
    43	                .stream()
    44	                .map(error -> ((FieldError) error).getField() + " : " + error.getDefaultMessage())
    45	                .toList();
    46	
    47	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    48	                .errorCode("VALIDATION_ERROR")
    49	                .message("Validation failed")
    50	                .details(errors)
    51	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    52	                .build();
    53	
    54	        return ResponseEntity.badRequest().body(response);
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    58	    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneralException(Exception ex) {
    59	        return buildError("INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR",
    60	                "Something went wrong",
    61	                HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR);
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    private ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> buildError(
    65	            String code,
    66	            String message,
    67	            HttpStatus status) {
    68	
    69	        ErrorResponse response = ErrorResponse.builder()
    70	                .errorCode(code)
    71	                .message(message)
    72	                .timestamp(LocalDateTime.now())
    73	                .build();
    74	
    75	        return new ResponseEntity<>(response, status);
    76	    }
    77	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/filter/CorrelationIdFilter.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.filter;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
     5	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     6	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     7	import org.slf4j.MDC;
     8	import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
     9	import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
    10	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    11	import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;
    12	
    13	import java.io.IOException;
    14	import java.util.UUID;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Picks up the {@code X-Correlation-Id} header set by the API Gateway and
    18	 * stores it in SLF4J MDC so it appears in every log statement for the request.
    19	 *
    20	 * <p>Also attaches the header to the HTTP response so callers can trace
    21	 * requests end-to-end.
    22	 */
    23	@Component
    24	@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    25	public class CorrelationIdFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {
    26	
    27	    public static final String CORRELATION_ID_HEADER = "X-Correlation-Id";
    28	    public static final String MDC_KEY = "correlationId";
    29	
    30	    @Override
    31	    protected void doFilterInternal(HttpServletRequest request,
    32	                                    HttpServletResponse response,
    33	                                    FilterChain filterChain) throws ServletException, IOException {
    34	        String correlationId = request.getHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER);
    35	        if (correlationId == null || correlationId.isBlank()) {
    36	            correlationId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        MDC.put(MDC_KEY, correlationId);
    40	        response.addHeader(CORRELATION_ID_HEADER, correlationId);
    41	
    42	        try {
    43	            filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    44	        } finally {
    45	            MDC.remove(MDC_KEY);
    46	        }
    47	    }
    48	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/repository/OTPVerificationRepository.java

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/repository/UserRepository.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/repository/UserRepository.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.repository;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.user_service.entity.Role;
     4	import com.sourabh.user_service.entity.User;
     5	import com.sourabh.user_service.entity.UserStatus;
     6	import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.JpaRepository;
     7	import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
     8	import org.springframework.data.domain.Pageable;
     9	import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Query;
    10	import org.springframework.data.repository.query.Param;
    11	
    12	import java.util.Optional;
    13	
    14	public interface UserRepository extends JpaRepository<User, Long> {
    15	
    16	    Optional<User> findByEmail(String email);
    17	
    18	    Optional<User> findByUuid(String uuid);
    19	
    20	    boolean existsByEmail(String email);
    21	
    22	    Page<User> findByRoleAndStatus(Role role, UserStatus status, Pageable pageable);
    23	
    24	    Page<User> findByIsDeletedFalse(Pageable pageable);
    25	
    26	    Page<User> findByRoleAndIsDeletedFalse(Role role, Pageable pageable);
    27	
    28	    Page<User> findByStatusAndIsDeletedFalse(UserStatus status, Pageable pageable);
    29	
    30	    Page<User> findByRoleAndStatusAndIsDeletedFalse(
    31	            Role role,
    32	            UserStatus status,
    33	            Pageable pageable
    34	    );
    35	
    36	    @Query("""
    37	       SELECT u FROM User u
    38	       WHERE u.isDeleted = false AND
    39	       (
    40	           LOWER(u.email) LIKE LOWER(CONCAT('%', :keyword, '%')) OR
    41	           LOWER(u.firstName) LIKE LOWER(CONCAT('%', :keyword, '%')) OR
    42	           LOWER(u.lastName) LIKE LOWER(CONCAT('%', :keyword, '%')) OR
    43	           u.phoneNumber LIKE CONCAT('%', :keyword, '%')
    44	       )
    45	       """)
    46	    Page<User> searchUsers(@Param("keyword") String keyword, Pageable pageable);
    47	
    48	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/security/InternalSecretInterceptor.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.security;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     5	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
     6	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     7	import org.springframework.web.servlet.HandlerInterceptor;
     8	
     9	@Component
    10	public class InternalSecretInterceptor implements HandlerInterceptor {
    11	
    12	    @Value("${internal.secret}")
    13	    private String expectedSecret;
    14	
    15	    @Override
    16	    public boolean preHandle(HttpServletRequest request,
    17	                             HttpServletResponse response,
    18	                             Object handler) throws Exception {
    19	
    20	        String providedSecret = request.getHeader("X-Internal-Secret");
    21	
    22	        if (providedSecret == null || !providedSecret.equals(expectedSecret)) {
    23	            response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    24	            return false;
    25	        }
    26	
    27	        return true;
    28	    }
    29	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/security/RoleInterceptor.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/security/RoleInterceptor.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.security;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
     4	import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
     5	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
     6	import org.springframework.web.servlet.HandlerInterceptor;
     7	
     8	@Component
     9	public class RoleInterceptor implements HandlerInterceptor {
    10	
    11	    @Override
    12	    public boolean preHandle(HttpServletRequest request,
    13	                             HttpServletResponse response,
    14	                             Object handler) throws Exception {
    15	
    16	        String role = request.getHeader("X-User-Role");
    17	
    18	        // Protect admin endpoints
    19	        if (request.getRequestURI().contains("/admin/")) {
    20	
    21	            if (role == null || !role.equals("ADMIN")) {
    22	                response.setStatus(HttpServletResponse.SC_FORBIDDEN);
    23	                return false;
    24	            }
    25	        }
    26	
    27	        return true;
    28	    }
    29	}
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/service/UserService.java

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.service;
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/service/impl/UserServiceImpl.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/service/impl/UserServiceImpl.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.service.impl;
     2	
     3	import com.sourabh.user_service.common.PageResponse;
     4	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.ChangePasswordRequest;
     5	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.RegisterRequest;
     6	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.UpdateProfileRequest;
     7	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.request.VerifyOTPRequest;
     8	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.response.InternalUserDto;
     9	import com.sourabh.user_service.dto.response.UserResponse;
    10	import com.sourabh.user_service.entity.*;
    11	import com.sourabh.user_service.exception.OTPException;
    12	import com.sourabh.user_service.exception.UserStateException;
    13	import com.sourabh.user_service.exception.UserAlreadyExistsException;
    14	import com.sourabh.user_service.exception.UserNotFoundException;
    15	import com.sourabh.user_service.repository.OTPVerificationRepository;
    16	import com.sourabh.user_service.repository.UserRepository;
    17	import com.sourabh.user_service.service.UserService;
    18	import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
    19	import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
    20	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.CacheEvict;
    21	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.Cacheable;
    22	import org.springframework.cache.annotation.Caching;
    23	import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
    24	import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;
    25	import org.springframework.data.domain.Pageable;
    26	import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort;
    27	import org.springframework.security.crypto.password.PasswordEncoder;
    28	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    29	import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
    30	
    31	import java.time.LocalDateTime;
    32	import java.util.List;
    33	import java.util.Random;
    34	
    35	@Slf4j
    36	@Service
    37	@RequiredArgsConstructor
    38	public class UserServiceImpl implements UserService {
    39	
    40	    private final UserRepository userRepository;
    41	    private final OTPVerificationRepository otpRepository;
    42	    private final PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder;
    43	
    44	
    45	    @Override
    46	    @Transactional
    47	    public UserResponse registerUser(RegisterRequest request) {
    48	
    49	        if (userRepository.existsByEmail(request.getEmail())) {
    50	            throw new UserAlreadyExistsException("Email already registered");
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        User user = User.builder()
    54	                .firstName(request.getFirstName())
    55	                .lastName(request.getLastName())
    56	                .email(request.getEmail())
    57	                .phoneNumber(request.getPhoneNumber())
    58	                .password(passwordEncoder.encode(request.getPassword()))
    59	                .role(request.getRole())
    60	                .status(UserStatus.PENDING_VERIFICATION)
    61	                .build();
    62	
    63	        user = userRepository.save(user);
    64	
    65	        generateAndSendOTP(user, OTPType.EMAIL);
    66	
    67	        log.info("New user registered: email={}, role={}", user.getEmail(), user.getRole());
    68	
    69	        return mapToResponse(user);
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    @Override
    73	    @Transactional
    74	    public String verifyOTP(VerifyOTPRequest request) {
    75	
    76	        User user = userRepository.findByEmail(request.getEmail())
    77	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
    78	
    79	        OTPVerification otp = otpRepository
    80	                .findTopByUserAndTypeOrderByCreatedAtDesc(user, OTPType.EMAIL)
    81	                .orElseThrow(() -> new OTPException("OTP not found"));
    82	
    83	        if (user.getStatus() != UserStatus.PENDING_VERIFICATION) {
    84	            throw new OTPException("User not in verification state");
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        if (otp.isVerified()) {
    88	            throw new OTPException("OTP already verified");
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        if (otp.getExpiryTime().isBefore(LocalDateTime.now())) {
    92	            throw new OTPException("OTP expired");
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        // Block brute-force after 5 failed attempts
    96	        if (otp.getAttemptCount() >= 5) {
    97	            throw new OTPException("OTP locked - too many failed attempts. Please request a new OTP.");
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        if (!otp.getOtpCode().equals(request.getOtpCode())) {
   101	            otp.setAttemptCount(otp.getAttemptCount() + 1);
   102	            otpRepository.save(otp);
   103	            throw new OTPException("Invalid OTP. " + (5 - otp.getAttemptCount()) + " attempt(s) remaining.");
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        otp.setVerified(true);
   107	        otpRepository.save(otp);
   108	
   109	        user.setEmailVerified(true);
   110	
   111	        if (user.getRole() == Role.SELLER) {
   112	            user.setStatus(UserStatus.PENDING_APPROVAL);
   113	        } else {
   114	            user.setStatus(UserStatus.ACTIVE);
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        userRepository.save(user);
   118	
   119	        return "OTP verified successfully";
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    // ========================
   123	    // Helper Methods
   124	    // ========================
   125	
   126	    private void generateAndSendOTP(User user, OTPType type) {
   127	
   128	        String otpCode = String.valueOf(100000 + new Random().nextInt(900000));
   129	
   130	        OTPVerification otp = OTPVerification.builder()
   131	                .otpCode(otpCode)
   132	                .type(type)
   133	                .expiryTime(LocalDateTime.now().plusMinutes(5))
   134	                .user(user)
   135	                .build();
   136	
   137	        otpRepository.save(otp);
   138	
   139	        // Simulate sending OTP
   140	        log.info("[OTP] Generated for email={}: {}", user.getEmail(), otpCode);
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    private UserResponse mapToResponse(User user) {
   144	
   145	        return UserResponse.builder()
   146	                .uuid(user.getUuid())
   147	                .firstName(user.getFirstName())
   148	                .lastName(user.getLastName())
   149	                .email(user.getEmail())
   150	                .phoneNumber(user.getPhoneNumber())
   151	                .role(user.getRole())
   152	                .status(user.getStatus())
   153	                .emailVerified(user.isEmailVerified())
   154	                .approved(user.isApproved())
   155	                .build();
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    @Override
   159	    @Transactional
   160	    @Caching(evict = {
   161	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   162	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   163	    })
   164	    public String approveSeller(String userUuid) {
   165	
   166	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   167	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   168	
   169	        if (!user.isEmailVerified()) {
   170	            throw new OTPException("Email not verified yet");
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        if (user.getRole() != Role.SELLER) {
   174	            throw new UserStateException("User is not a seller");
   175	        }
   176	
   177	        if (user.getStatus() != UserStatus.PENDING_APPROVAL) {
   178	            throw new UserStateException("Seller is not pending approval");
   179	        }
   180	
   181	
   182	
   183	        user.setStatus(UserStatus.ACTIVE);
   184	        user.setApproved(true);
   185	
   186	        userRepository.save(user);
   187	
   188	        log.info("Seller approved: uuid={}", userUuid);
   189	        return "Seller approved successfully";
   190	    }
   191	
   192	    @Override
   193	    @Transactional
   194	    @Caching(evict = {
   195	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   196	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   197	    })
   198	    public String rejectSeller(String userUuid) {
   199	
   200	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   201	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   202	
   203	        if (user.getRole() != Role.SELLER) {
   204	            throw new UserStateException("User is not a seller");
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        user.setStatus(UserStatus.BLOCKED);
   208	        user.setApproved(false);
   209	        userRepository.save(user);
   210	
   211	        log.info("Seller rejected: uuid={}", userUuid);
   212	        return "Seller rejected successfully";
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    @Override
   216	    @Transactional
   217	    @Caching(evict = {
   218	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   219	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   220	    })
   221	    public String blockUser(String userUuid) {
   222	
   223	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   224	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   225	
   226	        user.setStatus(UserStatus.BLOCKED);
   227	
   228	        userRepository.save(user);
   229	
   230	        log.info("User blocked: uuid={}", userUuid);
   231	        return "User blocked successfully";
   232	    }
   233	
   234	    @Override
   235	    public PageResponse<UserResponse> getAllUsers(
   236	            int page,
   237	            int size,
   238	            String sortBy,
   239	            String direction,
   240	            String role,
   241	            String status) {
   242	
   243	        Sort sort = direction.equalsIgnoreCase("asc")
   244	                ? Sort.by(sortBy).ascending()
   245	                : Sort.by(sortBy).descending();
   246	
   247	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(page, size, sort);
   248	
   249	
   250	        Page<User> userPage;
   251	
   252	        if (role != null && status != null) {
   253	            userPage = userRepository
   254	                    .findByRoleAndStatusAndIsDeletedFalse(
   255	                            Role.valueOf(role.toUpperCase()),
   256	                            UserStatus.valueOf(status.toUpperCase()),
   257	                            pageable
   258	                    );
   259	        } else if (role != null) {
   260	            userPage = userRepository
   261	                    .findByRoleAndIsDeletedFalse(
   262	                            Role.valueOf(role.toUpperCase()),
   263	                            pageable
   264	                    );
   265	        } else if (status != null) {
   266	            userPage = userRepository
   267	                    .findByStatusAndIsDeletedFalse(
   268	                            UserStatus.valueOf(status.toUpperCase()),
   269	                            pageable
   270	                    );
   271	        } else {
   272	            userPage = userRepository
   273	                    .findByIsDeletedFalse(pageable);
   274	        }
   275	
   276	        List<UserResponse> responses = userPage.getContent()
   277	                .stream()
   278	                .map(this::mapToResponse)
   279	                .toList();
   280	
   281	        return PageResponse.<UserResponse>builder()
   282	                .content(responses)
   283	                .page(userPage.getNumber())
   284	                .size(userPage.getSize())
   285	                .totalElements(userPage.getTotalElements())
   286	                .totalPages(userPage.getTotalPages())
   287	                .last(userPage.isLast())
   288	                .build();
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    @Override
   292	    @Transactional
   293	    @Caching(evict = {
   294	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   295	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   296	    })
   297	    public String softDeleteUser(String userUuid) {
   298	
   299	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   300	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   301	
   302	        user.setDeleted(true);
   303	        user.setStatus(UserStatus.DELETED);
   304	
   305	        userRepository.save(user);
   306	
   307	        log.info("User soft-deleted: uuid={}", userUuid);
   308	        return "User soft deleted successfully";
   309	    }
   310	
   311	    @Override
   312	    @Transactional
   313	    @Caching(evict = {
   314	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   315	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   316	    })
   317	    public String restoreUser(String userUuid) {
   318	
   319	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   320	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   321	
   322	        user.setDeleted(false);
   323	        // Sellers need re-approval after being restored; buyers/admins go straight to ACTIVE
   324	        if (user.getRole() == Role.SELLER && !user.isApproved()) {
   325	            user.setStatus(UserStatus.PENDING_APPROVAL);
   326	        } else {
   327	            user.setStatus(UserStatus.ACTIVE);
   328	        }
   329	
   330	        userRepository.save(user);
   331	
   332	        log.info("User restored: uuid={}", userUuid);
   333	        return "User restored successfully";
   334	    }
   335	
   336	    @Override
   337	    public PageResponse<UserResponse> searchUsers(
   338	            String keyword,
   339	            int page,
   340	            int size) {
   341	
   342	        Pageable pageable = PageRequest.of(
   343	                page,
   344	                size,
   345	                Sort.by("createdAt").descending()
   346	        );
   347	
   348	        Page<User> userPage =
   349	                userRepository.searchUsers(keyword, pageable);
   350	
   351	        List<UserResponse> responses = userPage.getContent()
   352	                .stream()
   353	                .map(this::mapToResponse)
   354	                .toList();
   355	
   356	        return PageResponse.<UserResponse>builder()
   357	                .content(responses)
   358	                .page(userPage.getNumber())
   359	                .size(userPage.getSize())
   360	                .totalElements(userPage.getTotalElements())
   361	                .totalPages(userPage.getTotalPages())
   362	                .last(userPage.isLast())
   363	                .build();
   364	    }
   365	
   366	    @Override
   367	    @Transactional
   368	    public String resendOTP(String email) {
   369	
   370	        User user = userRepository.findByEmail(email)
   371	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   372	
   373	        OTPVerification otp = otpRepository
   374	                .findTopByUserAndTypeOrderByCreatedAtDesc(user, OTPType.EMAIL)
   375	                .orElseThrow(() -> new OTPException("No previous OTP found"));
   376	
   377	        if (otp.getLastSentAt().plusSeconds(60)
   378	                .isAfter(LocalDateTime.now())) {
   379	            throw new OTPException("Please wait before requesting OTP again");
   380	        }
   381	
   382	        generateAndSendOTP(user, OTPType.EMAIL);
   383	
   384	        return "OTP resent successfully";
   385	    }
   386	
   387	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   388	    // INTERNAL — cached for auth-service lookups
   389	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   390	
   391	    @Override
   392	    @Cacheable(value = "usersByEmail", key = "#email")
   393	    public InternalUserDto getUserByEmailInternal(String email) {
   394	        log.debug("Cache miss for usersByEmail email={} — fetching from DB", email);
   395	        return userRepository.findByEmail(email)
   396	                .map(this::toInternalDto)
   397	                .orElse(null);
   398	    }
   399	
   400	    @Override
   401	    @Cacheable(value = "usersByUuid", key = "#uuid")
   402	    public InternalUserDto getUserByUuidInternal(String uuid) {
   403	        log.debug("Cache miss for usersByUuid uuid={} — fetching from DB", uuid);
   404	        return userRepository.findByUuid(uuid)
   405	                .map(this::toInternalDto)
   406	                .orElse(null);
   407	    }
   408	
   409	    private InternalUserDto toInternalDto(User user) {
   410	        return InternalUserDto.builder()
   411	                .uuid(user.getUuid())
   412	                .email(user.getEmail())
   413	                .password(user.getPassword())
   414	                .role(user.getRole().name())
   415	                .status(user.getStatus().name())
   416	                .emailVerified(user.isEmailVerified())
   417	                .build();
   418	    }
   419	
   420	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   421	    // PROFILE MANAGEMENT (authenticated user)
   422	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   423	
   424	    @Override
   425	    @Cacheable(value = "usersByUuid", key = "#userUuid")
   426	    public UserResponse getProfile(String userUuid) {
   427	        log.debug("getProfile: uuid={}", userUuid);
   428	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   429	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   430	        return mapToResponse(user);
   431	    }
   432	
   433	    @Override
   434	    @Transactional
   435	    @Caching(evict = {
   436	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   437	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   438	    })
   439	    public UserResponse updateProfile(String userUuid, UpdateProfileRequest request) {
   440	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   441	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   442	
   443	        if (request.getFirstName() != null)   user.setFirstName(request.getFirstName());
   444	        if (request.getLastName() != null)    user.setLastName(request.getLastName());
   445	        if (request.getPhoneNumber() != null) user.setPhoneNumber(request.getPhoneNumber());
   446	
   447	        userRepository.save(user);
   448	        log.info("Profile updated: uuid={}", userUuid);
   449	        return mapToResponse(user);
   450	    }
   451	
   452	    @Override
   453	    @Transactional
   454	    public String changePassword(String userUuid, ChangePasswordRequest request) {
   455	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   456	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   457	
   458	        if (!passwordEncoder.matches(request.getCurrentPassword(), user.getPassword())) {
   459	            throw new UserStateException("Current password is incorrect");
   460	        }
   461	        if (!request.getNewPassword().equals(request.getConfirmNewPassword())) {
   462	            throw new UserStateException("New passwords do not match");
   463	        }
   464	
   465	        user.setPassword(passwordEncoder.encode(request.getNewPassword()));
   466	        userRepository.save(user);
   467	        log.info("Password changed: uuid={}", userUuid);
   468	        return "Password changed successfully";
   469	    }
   470	
   471	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   472	    // UNBLOCK USER (Admin)
   473	    // ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   474	
   475	    @Override
   476	    @Transactional
   477	    @Caching(evict = {
   478	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByUuid",  key = "#userUuid"),
   479	            @CacheEvict(value = "usersByEmail", allEntries = true)
   480	    })
   481	    public String unblockUser(String userUuid) {
   482	        User user = userRepository.findByUuid(userUuid)
   483	                .orElseThrow(() -> new UserNotFoundException("User not found"));
   484	
   485	        if (user.getStatus() != UserStatus.BLOCKED) {
   486	            throw new UserStateException("User is not blocked");
   487	        }
   488	
   489	        // Sellers who were blocked need re-approval unless already approved
   490	        if (user.getRole() == Role.SELLER && !user.isApproved()) {
   491	            user.setStatus(UserStatus.PENDING_APPROVAL);
   492	        } else {
   493	            user.setStatus(UserStatus.ACTIVE);
   494	        }
   495	
   496	        userRepository.save(user);
   497	        log.info("User unblocked: uuid={}", userUuid);
   498	        return "User unblocked successfully";
   499	    }
   500	
   501	}
   502	
```

## user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/util/EnumUtil.java

Path: `user-service/src/main/java/com/sourabh/user_service/util/EnumUtil.java`

```java
     1	package com.sourabh.user_service.util;
     2	
     3	public class EnumUtil {
     4	
     5	    public static <T extends Enum<T>> T parseEnum(
     6	            Class<T> enumClass,
     7	            String value,
     8	            String errorMessage) {
     9	
    10	        try {
    11	            return Enum.valueOf(enumClass, value.toUpperCase());
    12	        } catch (Exception e) {
    13	            throw new IllegalArgumentException(errorMessage);
    14	        }
    15	    }
    16	}
```

## user-service/src/main/resources/application.properties

Path: `user-service/src/main/resources/application.properties`

```properties
     1	spring.application.name=user-service
     2	server.port=8080
     3	
     4	spring.datasource.url=jdbc:postgresql://postgres:5432/user_db
     5	spring.datasource.username=${DB_USERNAME:postgres}
     6	spring.datasource.password=${DB_PASSWORD:postgres}
     7	
     8	spring.jpa.hibernate.ddl-auto=validate
     9	spring.jpa.show-sql=false
    10	spring.jpa.properties.hibernate.format_sql=true
    11	
    12	# JWT secret must match api-gateway for token header extraction
    13	jwt.secret=${JWT_SECRET:mysupersecuresecretkeythatislongenough123}
    14	
    15	internal.secret=${INTERNAL_SECRET:veryStrongInternalSecret123}
    16	
    17	spring.data.redis.host=${REDIS_HOST:redis}
    18	spring.data.redis.port=${REDIS_PORT:6379}
    19	
    20	logging.level.com.sourabh.user_service=INFO
    21	logging.level.org.springframework.cache=DEBUG
    22	
    23	springdoc.api-docs.enabled=true
    24	springdoc.api-docs.path=/api/user/v3/api-docs
    25	springdoc.swagger-ui.enabled=false
    26	
    27	spring.cache.type=redis
    28	spring.cache.redis.time-to-live=900000
    29	spring.cache.redis.cache-null-values=false
    30	
    31	spring.flyway.enabled=true
    32	spring.flyway.locations=classpath:db/migration
    33	spring.flyway.baseline-on-migrate=true
    34	
    35	# Config Server (loads eureka, management, tracing, logging.pattern — see config-server/config/application.properties)
    36	spring.config.import=optional:configserver:${CONFIG_SERVER_URL:http://config-server:8888}
```

## user-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql

Path: `user-service/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__initial_schema.sql`

```sql
     1	-- user-service: initial schema
     2	-- V1 - creates users + otp_verifications tables
     3	-- NOTE: this reflects the JPA entity structure; ddl-auto=validate hereafter.
     4	
     5	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
     6	    id               BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
     7	    uuid             VARCHAR(36)  NOT NULL UNIQUE,
     8	    first_name       VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
     9	    last_name        VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    10	    email            VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    11	    phone_number     VARCHAR(15),
    12	    password         VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    13	    role             VARCHAR(20)  NOT NULL,
    14	    status           VARCHAR(30)  NOT NULL,
    15	    email_verified   BOOLEAN      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    16	    is_approved      BOOLEAN      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    17	    is_deleted       BOOLEAN      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    18	    last_login_at    TIMESTAMP,
    19	    created_at       TIMESTAMP,
    20	    updated_at       TIMESTAMP
    21	);
    22	
    23	-- Performance indexes
    24	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_email      ON users(email);
    25	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_uuid       ON users(uuid);
    26	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_role       ON users(role);
    27	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_status     ON users(status);
    28	
    29	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS otp_verifications (
    30	    id             BIGSERIAL    PRIMARY KEY,
    31	    otp_code       VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    32	    type           VARCHAR(30)  NOT NULL,
    33	    expiry_time    TIMESTAMP    NOT NULL,
    34	    verified       BOOLEAN      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
    35	    attempt_count  INTEGER      NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    36	    last_sent_at   TIMESTAMP,
    37	    user_id        BIGINT       NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    38	    created_at     TIMESTAMP,
    39	    updated_at     TIMESTAMP
    40	);
    41	
    42	CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_otp_user_id ON otp_verifications(user_id);
```
